yah saawvabhauik roop se sveekaar kiya gaya ek satya hai, ki ek saubhaagya ke lie ek akela vyakti, ek patnee kee ichchha mein hona chaahie.

haalaanki, is tarah ke ek aadamee kee bhaavanaon ya vichaaron ko usake pados mein pravesh karane par pahalee baar jaana ja sakata hai, yah sachchaee aasapaas ke parivaaron ke dimaag mein itanee achchhee tarah se tay ho gaee hai, ki unhen kisee ek ya unakee betiyon kee sahee sampatti maana jaata hai .

"mere priy shree benet," ek din unakee mahila ne unase kaha, "kya aapane suna hai ki needaralainds paark antim hai?"

shree benet ne uttar diya ki vah nahin tha.

"lekin yah hai," usane lauta diya; "misej long abhee-abhee yahaan aaee hai, aur usane mujhe isake baare mein bataaya."

shree benet ne koee javaab nahin diya.

"kya aap jaanana nahin chaahate ki ise kisane liya hai?" apanee patnee ko adheerata se roya.

"aap mujhe bataana chaahate hain, aur mujhe ise sunane mein koee aapatti nahin hai."

yah paryaapt nimantran tha.

"kyon, mere pyaare, tumhen pata hona chaahie, shreematee long ka kahana hai ki needaralaind ka maidaan inglaind ke uttar se bade bhaagy ke ek yuvak dvaara liya gaya hai, ki vah somavaar ko ek chaar aur neeche chaar jagah dekhane ke lie aaya tha, aur aisa hee tha. isase bahut khushee huee ki vah shree moris ke saath turant sahamat ho gaya, ki use maikalamaas ke saamane kabja karana hai, aur usake kuchh naukar agale haphte ke ant tak ghar mein rahane vaale hain. "

"usaka naam kya hai?"

"bingale."

"vah shaadeeshuda hai ya singal?"

"oh! ekale, mere priye, nishchit hona! bade bhaagy ka ek akela aadamee; chaar ya paanch hajaar ek varsh. hamaaree ladakiyon ke lie ek achchhee baat kya hai!"

"aisa kaise? yah unhen kaise prabhaavit kar sakata hai?"

"mere pyaare mistar benet," ne apanee patnee ko javaab diya, "aap itane thakaoo kaise ho sakate hain! aapako pata hona chaahie ki main unamen se ek se shaadee karane ke baare mein soch raha hoon."

"kya usaka dizain yahaan basane mein hai?"

"dijain! bakavaas, aap kaise baat kar sakate hain! lekin yah bahut sambhaavana hai ki vah unamen se ek ke saath pyaar mein pad sakata hai, aur isalie jaise hee vah aata hai aapako usase milana chaahie."

"main isake lie koee avasar nahin dekhata hoon. aap aur ladakiyaan ja sakate hain, ya aap unhen svayan bhej sakate hain, jo shaayad abhee bhee behatar hoga, kyonki aap unamen se kisee ke roop mein sundar hain, mistar bingale aapako sabase achchha lag sakata hai paartee."

"mere priy, tum meree chaapaloosee karate ho. main nishchit roop se meree sundarata ka hissa raha hoon, lekin main ab kisee bhee cheej ke lie asaadhaaran hone ka dikhaava nahin karata. jab ek mahila kee paanch betiyaan ho jaatee hain, to use apanee sundarata ke baare mein sochane ka mauka dena chaahie."

"aise maamalon mein, ek mahila ke paas sochane ke lie aksar bahut sundarata nahin hotee hai."

"lekin, mere priy, aapako pados mein aane par mistar bingale ko avashy dekhana chaahie."

"isase adhik hai ki main isake lie sanlagn hoon, main aapako aashvaasan deta hoon."

"lekin apanee betiyon par vichaar karen. keval yah sochen ki unamen se kisee ek ke lie yah kya sthaapana hogee. sar viliyam aur ledee lukaas jaane ke lie drdh hain, keval us khaate par, saamaany taur par aap jaanate hain ki ve kisee nae kaamared se milane nahin jaate. vaastav mein aapako avashy jaana chaahie." yadi aap nahin karate hain, to usake lie hamen yaatra karana asambhav hoga. "

"aap nishchit roop se adhik spasht hain. mera kahana hai ki shree bingale aapako dekhakar bahut khush honge, aur main aapako unakee shaadee ke lie meree haardik sahamati ka aashvaasan dene ke lie kuchh panktiyaan bhejoonga, jo kabhee bhee vah ladakiyon kee chugalee karate hain; haalaanki main mere chhote lijee ke lie ek achchhe shabd mein phenk dena chaahie. "

"meree ichchha hai ki aap aisa koee kaam nahin karenge. lizee doosaron kee tulana mein thoda behatar nahin hai; aur mujhe yakeen hai ki vah jen ke roop mein itanee sundar nahin hai, aur na hee lidiya ke roop mein itanee achchhee vinamr. lekin aap hamesha use vareeyata de rahe hain. "

"unake paas unakee siphaarish karane ke lie unamen se koee bhee nahin hai," unhonne javaab diya; "ve any ladakiyon kee tarah moorkhataapoorn aur agyaanee hain; lekin lizee ko apanee bahanon kee tulana mein kuchh jyaada hee phurtee hai."

"shree benet, aap is tarah se apane bachchon ka durupayog kaise kar sakate hain? aap mujhe khush karane mein aanand lete hain. aapako meree kharaab nason par koee daya nahin hai."

"aap mujhase galatee karate hain, mere pyaare. aapakee nason ke prati mera bahut sammaan hai. ve mere puraane mitr hain. mainne suna hai ki aapane in bees varshon mein kam se kam un par vichaar kiya hai."

"aah! tum nahin jaanate ki main kya peedit hoon."

"lekin mujhe ummeed hai ki aap is par kaaboo pa lenge, aur pados mein rahane vaale chaar hajaar ek saal ke kaee yuvaon ko dekhane ke lie jeevit rahenge."

"yah hamaare lie koee phaayada nahin hoga, agar bees aise aane chaahie, jab se aap unase nahin milenge."

"is par nirbhar, mere priy, ki jab bees hote hain, to main un sabhee ka daura karoonga."

mistar benet itane ajeeb the ki tvarit bhaagon, vyangyaatmak haasy, rijarv aur kaipris ka mishran tha, ki unakee patnee ko unake charitr ko samajhane ke lie teen aur bees saal ka anubhav aparyaapt tha. usaka dimaag vikasit hone mein kam mushkil tha. vah ausat samajh, kam jaanakaaree aur anishchit svabhaav kee mahila thee. jab vah asantusht thee to usane khud ko ghabaraaya hua dekha. usake jeevan ka vyavasaay usakee betiyon kee shaadee karana tha; isakee ekaant yaatra aur samaachaar the.

mistar benet un logon mein se the jo mistar bingale ka intajaar karate the. usane hamesha use dekhane ka iraada kiya tha, haalaanki aakhiree mein hamesha apanee patnee ko aashvaasan diya tha ki use nahin jaana chaahie; aur yaatra ka bhugataan hone ke baad shaam tak, use isaka koee gyaan nahin tha. phir nimn tareeke se isaka khulaasa kiya gaya. ek topee ko trim karane mein kaaryarat apanee doosaree betee ko dekhate hue, usane achaanak use sambodhit kiya,

"mujhe ummeed hai ki mistar bingale ise lizee pasand karenge."

"ham ek tarah se yah jaanane ke lie nahin hain ki mistar bingale ko kya pasand hai," usakee maan ne naaraajagee se kaha, "choonki ham yaatra karane ke lie nahin hain."

"lekin aap bhool jaate hain, maama," elijaabeth ne kaha, "ham use vidhaanasabhaon mein milenge, aur shreematee long ne use pesh karane ka vaada kiya hai."

"mujhe vishvaas nahin hai ki shreematee long koee aisa kaam karegee. usakee apanee do bhateejee hain. vah ek svaarthee, paakhandee mahila hai, aur meree usakee koee raay nahin hai."

"aur nahin mere paas," shree benet ne kaha; "aur mujhe yah jaanakar khushee huee ki aap usakee seva par nirbhar nahin hain."

shreematee benet ne koee javaab nahin diya; lekin khud ko shaamil karane mein asamarth, apanee betiyon mein se ek ko daantana shuroo kar diya.

"svarg kee khaatir, kitee ko khaansate mat rakho! meree nason par thodee daya karo. tum unhen tukade tukade kar do."

"kittee ka usakee khaansee mein koee vivek nahin hai," usake pita ne kaha; "vah unhen beemaar samay."

"mujhe apane khud ke manoranjan ke lie khaansee nahin hai," kittee ne jhallaahat se javaab diya.

"aapakee agalee gend kab hogee, lijee?"

"du: kh pakhavaade ke lie."

"ai, to yah hai," usakee maan roya, "aur shreematee laang din pahale tak vaapas nahin aatee hai; isalie, usake lie use pesh karana asambhav hoga, kyonki vah use khud nahin jaan paegee."

"phir, mere pyaare, aapako apane dost ka phaayada ho sakata hai, aur mistar bingale ko usase milava sakate hain."

"asambhav, shree benet, asambhav, jab main khud unase parichit nahin hoon, to aap itane khush kaise ho sakate hain?"

"main aapake parichaarak ka sammaan karata hoon. ek pakhavaade ka parichit nishchit roop se bahut kam hai. ek pakhavaade ke ant tak ek aadamee vaastav mein kya kar sakata hai yah nahin jaan sakata. lekin agar ham udyam nahin karate hain, to koee aur karega; aur aakhirakaar, shreematee laang aur usakee bhateejee. unhen apana mauka khada karana chaahie, aur isalie, jaisa ki vah ise daya ka kaary samajhengee, yadi aap kaaryaalay ko asveekaar karate hain, to main ise apane saath le jaoongee. "

ladakiyon ne apane pita ko dekha. shreematee benet ne keval kaha, "bakavaas, bakavaas!"

"us sashakt vismayaadibodhak ka kya arth ho sakata hai?" vah roya. "kya aap parichay ke roopon par vichaar karate hain, aur un par jo tanaav hai, vah bakavaas ke roop mein hai? main vahaan aapake saath kaaphee sahamat nahin ho sakata. aap kya kahate hain, mairee? aapake lie main gaharee pratibimb kee ek yuva mahila hoon jo mujhe pata hai, aur mahaan padhen kitaaben, aur ark banaate hain. "

mairee kuchh samajhadaar kahana chaahatee thee, lekin nahin jaanatee thee ki kaise.

"jabaki mariyam apane vichaaron ko samaayojit kar rahee hai," unhonne jaaree rakha, "hamen mistar bingale par vaapas jaane den."

"main mistar bingale se beemaar hoon," apanee patnee ko roya.

"mujhe yah sunakar dukh hua; lekin aapane mujhe pahale aisa kyon nahin bataaya? agar main aaj subah jitana jaanata tha, to main nishchit roop se us par phon nahin karata tha. yah bahut ashubh hai; lekin jaisa ki mainne vaastav mein yaatra ka bhugataan kiya hai." ab ham parichit se bach nahin sakate.

deviyon kee vismayakaaree ichchha thee ki vah kya kare; shreematee benet kee jo shaayad baakee ko paar kar gaee ho; haalaanki jab khushee ka pahala daur khatm ho gaya tha, to usane ghoshana karana shuroo kar diya ki yah vahee hai jisakee use ummeed thee.

"yah aap mein kitana achchha tha, mere pyaare mistar benet! lekin mujhe pata tha ki mujhe aapako aakhirakaar raajee karana chaahie. mujhe yakeen tha ki aap apanee ladakiyon ko bhee is tarah ke ek parichit kee upeksha karane ke lie pyaar karate the. khair, main kitana khush hoon! aur yah aisa hai!" ek achchha majaak, bhee, ki aapako aaj subah jaana chaahie tha, aur ab tak isake baare mein ek shabd bhee nahin kaha. "

"ab, kittee, aap jitana chus sakate hain utana khaansee le sakate hain," shree benet ne kaha; aur, jaisa ki usane baat kee thee, usane apanee patnee ke utsaah se thakakar kamara chhod diya.

"tumhaare paas ek utkrsht pita hai, ladakiyon," usane kaha, jab daravaaja band tha. "mujhe nahin pata ki aap use kabhee usakee daya ke lie kaise banaenge? ya mujhe ya to us baat ke lie. hamaare jeevan ke samay mein, yah itana sukhad nahin hai ki main aapako bata sakata hoon, har din nae parichit banaana; lekin ke lie aapakee khaatir, ham koee bhee kaam karenge. lida, mera pyaar, haalaanki aap sabase chhote hain, main kahata hoon ki mistar bingale agalee gend par aapake saath daans karenge. "

"oh!" lidiya ne drdhata se kaha, "main darane vaalee nahin hoon; haalaanki main sabase chhotee hoon, main sabase badee hoon."

shesh shaam ko yah anumaan lagaane mein bitaaya gaya tha ki vah kitanee jaldee shree benet kee yaatra par lautenge, aur yah nirdhaarit karate hue ki unhen raat ke khaane ke lie poochhana chaahie.

haalaanki, shreematee benet ne apanee paanch betiyon kee sahaayata se, is vishay par nahin poochha ki unake pati shree bingale ke kisee bhee santoshajanak vivaran ko aakarshit karane ke lie paryaapt the. unhonne vibhinn tareekon se us par hamala kiya; nange savaalon ke saath, saral suppositions, aur door surmisais; lekin usane un sabhee ke kaushal ko khaarij kar diya; aur ve aakhiree baar apane padosee ledee lukaas kee doosaree buddhi ko sveekaar karane ke lie baadhy the. usakee riport atyadhik anukool thee. sar viliyam usase khush ho gaya tha. vah kaaphee yuva, aashcharyajanak roop se sundar, behad sahamat the, aur poore taaj ko banaane ke lie unaka matalab ek badee paartee ke saath agalee vidhaanasabha mein hona tha. kuchh bhee adhik ramaneey nahin ho sakata hai! naachane ka shauk hona pyaar mein padane kee disha mein ek nishchit kadam tha; aur shree bingale ke dil kee bahut jeevant aashaon ka manoranjan kiya gaya tha.

"agar main apanee betiyon mein se ek ko khushee se needaralainds mein basa dekh sakatee hoon," shreematee benet ne apane pati se kaha, "aur any sabhee samaan roop se achchhee tarah se vivaahit hain, to mere paas ichchha ke lie kuchh bhee nahin hoga."

kuchh hee dinon mein mistar bingale mistar benet kee yaatra par laute, aur apane pustakaalay mein unake saath lagabhag das minat baithe. unhonne un yuva mahilaon kee drshti mein bhartee hone kee ummeedon ka manoranjan kiya tha, jinakee sundarata ke baare mein unhonne bahut kuchh suna tha; lekin usane keval pita ko dekha. mahilaen kuchh adhik bhaagyashaalee theen, kyonki unhen ooparee khidakee se pata lagaane ka phaayada tha ki unhonne ek neela kot pahana tha aur ek kaale ghode kee savaaree kee thee.

khaane ke lie nimantran jald hee bhej diya gaya tha; aur pahale se hee shreematee benet ne un paathyakramon kee yojana banaee thee jo usake hausakeeping ko shrey dene ke lie the, jab ek javaab aaya jisane ise sabhee ke lie sthagit kar diya. shree bingale ko agale din shahar mein rahane ke lie baadhy kiya gaya tha, aur parinaamasvaroop unake nimantran ke sammaan ko sveekaar karane mein asamarth tha, aur see. shreematee benet kaaphee asantusht theen. vah kalpana nahin kar sakata tha ki hartaphordashaayar mein aane ke turant baad vah shahar mein kya vyavasaay kar sakata hai; aur use dar lagane laga ki shaayad vah hamesha ek jagah se doosaree jagah ke lie udaan bharatee rahe, aur kabhee bhee nedarapheeld mein nahin basatee kyonki vah hona chaahie. ledee lukaas ne apane dar ko thoda shaant kiya aur keval ek badee paartee ke lie landan jaane ke vichaar ko shuroo kiya; aur jald hee ek riport ke baad shree bingale ko baarah mahilaon aur saat sajjanon ko apane saath vidhaanasabha mein laana tha. ladakiyon ko aisee kaee mahilaon par shok hua; lekin yah sunakar ki gend ko ek din pahale aaraam diya gaya tha, baarah ke bajaay, vah landan se keval chhah lae the, unakee paanch bahanen aur ek chachera bhaee. aur jab paartee ne vidhaanasabha kaksh mein pravesh kiya, to isamen keval paanch shaamil the; mistar bingale, unakee do bahanen, sabase bade aur doosare yuvak ke pati.

mistar bingale achchhe dikhane vaale aur sajjan vyakti the; unake paas ek sukhad kauntens aur aasaan, aprabhaavit shishtaachaar tha. unakee bahanen theek-thaak phaishan vaalee mahila theen. unake bahanoee, shree harst, keval sajjan ko dekha; lekin unake dost mistar daarsee ne jald hee apane theek, lambe vyakti, sundar suvidhaon, mahaan miyaan dvaara kamare ka dhyaan aakarshit kiya; aur vah riport jo unake pravesh ke baad paanch minat ke bheetar saamaany prachalan mein thee, unake varsh mein das hajaar hone kee. sajjanon ne use ek aadamee ka theek-thaak hone ka uchchaaran kiya, mahilaon ne ghoshana kee ki vah mistar bingale kee tulana mein bahut sundar hai, aur use lagabhag aadhe shaam tak badee prashansa ke saath dekha gaya, jab tak ki usake shishyon ne ghrna prakat nahin kee, jo jvaar ka kaaran banee unakee lokapriyata; kyonki vah apanee kampanee ke oopar, aur prasann hone ke lie, garv karane ke lie khoja gaya tha; aur darbeeshaayar mein unakee saaree badee sampatti tab unhen sabase jyaada mana karane, asahamat hone aur apane dost ke saath tulana karane ke lie ayogy hone se bacha sakatee thee.

mistar bingale ne jald hee khud ko kamare ke sabhee pramukh logon se parichit karaaya tha; vah jeevant aur anaarakshit tha, har nrty mein naachata tha, gusse mein tha ki gend itanee jaldee band ho gaee, aur usane khud ko needaralaind mein dene kee baat kahee. is tarah ke milanasaar gunon ko apane lie bolana chaahie. usake aur usake dost ke beech kya vipareet hai! mistar daarsee ne misej harst ke saath keval ek baar daans kiya aur ek baar mis bingale ke saath, kisee any mahila ke saath pesh hone se mana kar diya, aur shesh shaam kamare mein ghoomane mein bitaee, kabhee-kabhee apanee khud kee paartee mein. unaka charitr tay kiya gaya. vah duniya ka sabase ghamandee, sabase badanaam aadamee tha aur har shareer ko ummeed thee ki vah phir kabhee vahaan nahin aaega. unake khilaaph sabase adhik hinsak shreematee benet theen, jinake saamaany vyavahaar ke prati unakee naapasandagee, unakee ek betee ko maamoolee roop se naaraajagee mein badal diya gaya tha.

elijaabeth benet ko sajjanon kee kamee ke kaaran, do nrtyon ke lie baithane ke lie baadhy kiya gaya tha; aur us samay ke dauraan, mistar daarsee unake aur mistar bingale ke beech huee baatacheet ko sunaane ke lie unake paas kaaphee der se khade the, jo kuchh minaton ke lie nrty se aae the aur apane mitr ko isamen shaamil hone ke lie dabaav daala.

"aao, daarsee," unhonne kaha, "mujhe aapake paas nrty karana chaahie. mujhe is bevakooph tareeke se khud ke baare mein khade dekhane se napharat hai. aapake paas bahut behatar nrty tha."

"main nishchit roop se nahin karoonga. aap jaanate hain ki main kaise isaka pata lagaata hoon, jab tak ki main vishesh roop se parichit nahin hoon

shree bingale ne unakee salaah ka paalan kiya. mistar daarsee chal basa; aur elijaabeth usake prati bahut sauhaardapoorn bhaavanaon ke saath nahin rahee. usane haalaanki apane doston ke beech badee bhaavana ke saath kahaanee bataee; kyonki usake paas ek jeevant, chanchal svabhaav tha, jo kisee bhee cheej mein haasyaaspad tha.

shaam pooree tarah se poore parivaar ke lie sukhad rahee. shreematee benet ne apanee badee betee ko needaralaind paartee dvaara bahut prashansa karate dekha tha. mistar bingale ne do baar usake saath nrty kiya tha, aur vah apanee bahanon se alag ho gaee thee. jen ko is baat se bahut santushti milee, kyonki usakee maan shaantachitt tareeke se ho sakatee thee. elijaabeth ko jen ka sukh mahasoos hua. mairee ne khud ko mis bingale ke baare mein suna tha jo pados mein sabase nipun ladakee thee; aur kaithareen aur lidaaya bhaagyashaalee rahe hain jo kabhee bhee bina saathee ke nahin rahe, jo ki ek gend par unakee dekhabhaal karana seekh gaya tha. isalie ve achchhee aatmaon ke lie lautegoran, us gaanv mein laut aae jahaan ve rahate the, aur jisake ve pramukh nivaasee the. unhonne paaya ki shree benet abhee bhee oopar hain. ek pustak ke saath vah samay kee paravaah kie bina tha; aur vartamaan avasar par vah ek shaam kee ghatana ke roop mein utsukata ka ek achchha sauda tha jisane is tarah kee shaanadaar ummeedon ko badhaaya tha. unhonne balki yah aasha kee thee ki ajanabee par unakee patnee ke sabhee vichaar niraash honge; lekin jald hee usane paaya ki usake paas sunane ke lie bahut alag kahaanee hai.

"oh! mere pyaare mistar benet," jaise hee vah kamare mein daakhil huee, "hamaare paas sabase ramaneey shaam thee, ek sabase shaanadaar gend. kaash ki aap vahaan hote. jen kee itanee prashansa hotee, aisa kuchh nahin ho sakata. har shareer. usane kaha ki vah kitanee achchhee lag rahee thee aur mistar bingale ne use bahut sundar samajha, aur usake saath do baar nrty kiya. keval mere priy ke baare mein sochen; usane vaastav mein usake saath do baar nrty kiya, aur vah kamare mein ekamaatr praanee thee jisase usane doosaree baar poochha. sabase pahale, usane mis lukaas se poochha. main use usake saath khade dekhane ke lie bahut chintit tha; lekin, haalaanki, usane usakee bilkul bhee prashansa nahin kee: vaastav mein, koee nahin kar sakata, aap jaanate hain, aur vah jen ke saath kaaphee maara gaya tha. vah nrty se baahar ja rahee thee. isalie, usane poochhataachh kee ki vah kaun hai, aur mil gaya, aur usase agale donon ke lie poochha. phir, do teesare usane mis king ke saath nrty kiya, aur do chauthe ke saath maariya lukaas, aur do paanchaven. jen ke saath phir se, aur lizee ke saath do chhathe, aur baulanger —— "

"agar use mujh par koee daya aatee," apane pati ko adheerata se pukaaratee, "vah itana aadha nahin dooba hota! bhagavaan kee khaatir, apane saathiyon se aur kuchh nahin kahana. oh! ki usane pahale daans mein apane chaacha ko ukasaaya tha." "

"oh! meree pyaaree," shreematee benet ne jaaree rakha, "main usake saath kaaphee khush hoon. vah bahut adhik sundar hai! aur usakee bahanen aakarshak mahilaen hain. mainne apane jeevan mein kabhee bhee kisee bhee cheej ko unake kapade se adhik suruchipoorn nahin dekha. main himmat karata hoon. shreematee harst ka gaun par pheeta -

yahaan vah phir se baadhit ho gaya tha. shree benet ne parimit ke kisee bhee vivaran ke khilaaph virodh kiya. isalie use vishay kee ek aur shaakha kee talaash karane ke lie baadhy kiya gaya tha, aur sambandhit, aatma kee bahut kadavaahat aur kuchh atishayokti ke saath, shree daarsee kee chaunkaane vaalee ashishtata.

जब महिलाएं रात के खाने के बाद हटाती हैं, तो एलिजाबेथ अपनी बहन के पास भागती है, और उसे अच्छी तरह से ठंड से बचाते हुए, उसे ड्राइंग-रूम में ले जाती है; जहाँ उसके दो दोस्तों ने आनंद के कई पेशों के साथ उसका स्वागत किया; और एलिजाबेथ ने उन्हें कभी इतने सहमत नहीं देखा था क्योंकि वे उस समय के दौरान थे जो सज्जनों के सामने आने से पहले गुजर गए थे। उनकी बातचीत की शक्तियां काफी थीं। वे सटीकता के साथ एक मनोरंजन का वर्णन कर सकते हैं, हास्य के साथ एक किस्सा संबंधित कर सकते हैं, और आत्मा के साथ अपने परिचित पर हंस सकते हैं।

लेकिन जब सज्जनों ने प्रवेश किया, तो जेन अब पहली वस्तु नहीं थी। मिस बिंगले की आंखें तुरंत डार्सी की ओर मुड़ गईं, और इससे पहले कि वह कई कदम आगे बढ़े, उन्हें कुछ कहना था। उन्होंने खुद को मिस बेनेट को सीधे संबोधित किया, एक विनम्र बधाई के साथ; श्री हर्स्ट ने उसे एक मामूली धनुष भी बनाया, और कहा कि वह "बहुत खुश है;" लेकिन बिंगले के सलाम के लिए विस्मय और गर्मजोशी बनी रही। वह आनंद और ध्यान से भरा हुआ था। पहले आधे घंटे को आग लगाने में बिताया गया था, ऐसा न हो कि वह कमरे के परिवर्तन से पीड़ित हो; और वह आग की जगह के दूसरी ओर जाने की अपनी इच्छा पर हटा दिया, कि वह दरवाजे से दूर हो सकता है। फिर वह उसके पास बैठ गया, और किसी और से बात की। एलिजाबेथ, विपरीत कोने में काम करते हुए, यह सब बहुत खुशी के साथ देखा।

जब चाय खत्म हो गई, तो श्री हर्स्ट ने अपनी भाभी को कार्ड-टेबल की याद दिलाई - लेकिन व्यर्थ। उसने निजी बुद्धि प्राप्त की थी कि मिस्टर डार्सी ने कार्ड की इच्छा नहीं की थी; और मिस्टर हर्स्ट ने जल्द ही अपनी खुली याचिका भी खारिज कर दी। उसने उसे आश्वासन दिया कि कोई भी खेलने का इरादा नहीं करता है, और इस विषय पर पूरी पार्टी की चुप्पी, उसे उचित ठहराने के लिए लग रहा था। इसलिए श्री हर्स्ट के पास करने के लिए कुछ नहीं था, लेकिन सोफों में से एक पर खुद को फैलाने और सो जाने के लिए। डार्सी ने एक पुस्तक ली; मिस बिंगले ने भी यही किया; और श्रीमती हर्स्ट, मुख्य रूप से अपने कंगन और अंगूठियों के साथ खेलने में व्यस्त थीं, अब मिस बेनेट के साथ अपने भाई की बातचीत में शामिल हुईं।

मिस बिंगले का ध्यान अपनी पुस्तक के माध्यम से मिस्टर डार्सी की प्रगति को देखने में काफी व्यस्त था, जैसा कि उन्होंने खुद पढ़ा था; और वह लगातार कुछ पूछताछ कर रही थी, या अपने पेज को देख रही थी। हालाँकि, वह उसे किसी भी बातचीत के लिए नहीं जीत सकती थी; उसने केवल उसके प्रश्न का उत्तर दिया, और पढ़ा। लंबाई में, अपनी खुद की किताब के साथ आनंदित होने के प्रयास से काफी थक गई, जिसे उसने केवल इसलिए चुना क्योंकि यह उसकी दूसरी मात्रा थी, उसने एक शानदार जम्हाई दी और कहा, "इस तरह एक शाम बिताना कितना सुखद है मैं घोषणा करता हूं कि पढ़ने के बाद कोई आनंद नहीं मिलता है! किसी किताब की तुलना में किसी भी चीज का कितना जल्दी एक टायर होता है! -जब मेरे पास अपना खुद का घर है, तो मैं एक उत्कृष्ट पुस्तकालय नहीं होने पर दुखी रहूंगा। "

किसी ने कोई जवाब नहीं दिया। वह फिर से जम्हाई लेती है, अपनी पुस्तक को एक तरफ फेंक देती है, और कुछ मनोरंजन की तलाश में अपनी आँखें गोल कमरे में डालती है; जब उसके भाई ने मिस बेनेट को एक गेंद का उल्लेख करते हुए सुना, तो वह अचानक उसकी ओर मुड़ी और बोली,

"अलविदा, चार्ल्स, क्या आप वास्तव में नीदरलैंड में एक नृत्य का ध्यान करने में गंभीर हैं? - मैं आपको सलाह दूंगा, इससे पहले कि आप इसे निर्धारित करें, वर्तमान पार्टी की इच्छाओं से परामर्श करने के लिए; मैं बहुत गलत हूं अगर हमारे बीच कुछ नहीं हैं; जिनके लिए गेंद खुशी के बजाय सजा होगी। ”

"यदि आप डार्सी का मतलब है," उसके भाई रोया, "वह बिस्तर पर जा सकता है, अगर वह chuses, शुरू होने से पहले - लेकिन गेंद के लिए के रूप में, यह काफी सुलझी हुई बात है, और जैसे ही निकोल्स ने सफेद सूप को पर्याप्त बना दिया है; मेरे कार्ड राउंड भेज देंगे। "

"मुझे गेंदों को असीम रूप से बेहतर पसंद करना चाहिए," उसने जवाब दिया, "अगर उन्हें एक अलग तरीके से किया गया था, लेकिन इस तरह की बैठक की सामान्य प्रक्रिया में कुछ अनुचित है। यह निश्चित रूप से बहुत अधिक तर्कसंगत होगा यदि नृत्य के बजाय तर्कसंगत होगा। दिन का क्रम बना। "

"बहुत अधिक तर्कसंगत, मेरे प्रिय कैरोलिन, मैं कहने की हिम्मत करता हूं, लेकिन यह गेंद की तरह बहुत करीब नहीं होगा।"

मिस बिंगले ने कोई जवाब नहीं दिया; और जल्द ही उठकर कमरे के बारे में चला गया। उसकी आकृति सुरुचिपूर्ण थी, और वह अच्छी तरह से चली; —लेकिन डार्सी, जिस पर यह सब लक्षित था, अभी भी अनम्य रूप से अध्ययनशील थी। उसकी भावनाओं की हताशा में उसने एक प्रयास में अधिक हल किया; और, एलिजाबेथ की ओर मुड़कर कहा,

"मिस एलिजा बेनेट, मुझे अपने उदाहरण का पालन करने के लिए मना लें, और कमरे के बारे में बारी ले लें। - मैं आपको विश्वास दिलाता हूं कि एक दृष्टिकोण में इतने लंबे समय तक बैठने के बाद यह बहुत ताज़ा है।"

एलिजाबेथ आश्चर्यचकित थी, लेकिन तुरंत इसके लिए सहमत हो गई। मिस बिंगले अपनी नागरिकता की वास्तविक वस्तु में कम सफल नहीं हुई; मिस्टर डार्सी ने देखा। वह उस तिमाही में ध्यान की नवीनता के लिए उतना ही जागृत था जितना कि एलिजाबेथ स्वयं हो सकती है, और अनजाने में अपनी पुस्तक बंद कर दी। उन्हें सीधे अपनी पार्टी में शामिल होने के लिए आमंत्रित किया गया था, लेकिन उन्होंने इसे अस्वीकार कर दिया, यह देखते हुए कि वह कल्पना कर सकते हैं, लेकिन उनके चुइंग के लिए दो इरादों के साथ-साथ कमरे में ऊपर और नीचे चलना, जिनमें से किसी भी उद्देश्य से उनके शामिल होने में हस्तक्षेप होगा। "उसका क्या मतलब हो सकता है? वह यह जानना चाह रही थी कि उसका क्या अर्थ हो सकता है" - और एलिजाबेथ से पूछा कि क्या वह उसे समझ सकती है?

"बिल्कुल नहीं," उसका जवाब था; "लेकिन यह निर्भर करता है, वह हम पर गंभीर होने का मतलब है, और हमारा सबसे अच्छा वा
jab mahilaen raat ke khaane ke baad hataatee hain, to elijaabeth apanee bahan ke paas bhaagatee hai, aur use achchhee tarah se thand se bachaate hue, use draing-room mein le jaatee hai; jahaan usake do doston ne aanand ke kaee peshon ke saath usaka svaagat kiya; aur elijaabeth ne unhen kabhee itane sahamat nahin dekha tha kyonki ve us samay ke dauraan the jo sajjanon ke saamane aane se pahale gujar gae the. unakee baatacheet kee shaktiyaan kaaphee theen. ve sateekata ke saath ek manoranjan ka varnan kar sakate hain, haasy ke saath ek kissa sambandhit kar sakate hain, aur aatma ke saath apane parichit par hans sakate hain.

lekin jab sajjanon ne pravesh kiya, to jen ab pahalee vastu nahin thee. mis bingale kee aankhen turant daarsee kee or mud gaeen, aur isase pahale ki vah kaee kadam aage badhe, unhen kuchh kahana tha. unhonne khud ko mis benet ko seedhe sambodhit kiya, ek vinamr badhaee ke saath; shree harst ne use ek maamoolee dhanush bhee banaaya, aur kaha ki vah "bahut khush hai;" lekin bingale ke salaam ke lie vismay aur garmajoshee banee rahee. vah aanand aur dhyaan se bhara hua tha. pahale aadhe ghante ko aag lagaane mein bitaaya gaya tha, aisa na ho ki vah kamare ke parivartan se peedit ho; aur vah aag kee jagah ke doosaree or jaane kee apanee ichchha par hata diya, ki vah daravaaje se door ho sakata hai. phir vah usake paas baith gaya, aur kisee aur se baat kee. elijaabeth, vipareet kone mein kaam karate hue, yah sab bahut khushee ke saath dekha.

jab chaay khatm ho gaee, to shree harst ne apanee bhaabhee ko kaard-tebal kee yaad dilaee - lekin vyarth. usane nijee buddhi praapt kee thee ki mistar daarsee ne kaard kee ichchha nahin kee thee; aur mistar harst ne jald hee apanee khulee yaachika bhee khaarij kar dee. usane use aashvaasan diya ki koee bhee khelane ka iraada nahin karata hai, aur is vishay par pooree paartee kee chuppee, use uchit thaharaane ke lie lag raha tha. isalie shree harst ke paas karane ke lie kuchh nahin tha, lekin sophon mein se ek par khud ko phailaane aur so jaane ke lie. daarsee ne ek pustak lee; mis bingale ne bhee yahee kiya; aur shreematee harst, mukhy roop se apane kangan aur angoothiyon ke saath khelane mein vyast theen, ab mis benet ke saath apane bhaee kee baatacheet mein shaamil hueen.

mis bingale ka dhyaan apanee pustak ke maadhyam se mistar daarsee kee pragati ko dekhane mein kaaphee vyast tha, jaisa ki unhonne khud padha tha; aur vah lagaataar kuchh poochhataachh kar rahee thee, ya apane pej ko dekh rahee thee. haalaanki, vah use kisee bhee baatacheet ke lie nahin jeet sakatee thee; usane keval usake prashn ka uttar diya, aur padha. lambaee mein, apanee khud kee kitaab ke saath aanandit hone ke prayaas se kaaphee thak gaee, jise usane keval isalie chuna kyonki yah usakee doosaree maatra thee, usane ek shaanadaar jamhaee dee aur kaha, "is tarah ek shaam bitaana kitana sukhad hai main ghoshana karata hoon ki padhane ke baad koee aanand nahin milata hai! kisee kitaab kee tulana mein kisee bhee cheej ka kitana jaldee ek taayar hota hai! -jab mere paas apana khud ka ghar hai, to main ek utkrsht pustakaalay nahin hone par dukhee rahoonga. "

kisee ne koee javaab nahin diya. vah phir se jamhaee letee hai, apanee pustak ko ek taraph phenk detee hai, aur kuchh manoranjan kee talaash mein apanee aankhen gol kamare mein daalatee hai; jab usake bhaee ne mis benet ko ek gend ka ullekh karate hue suna, to vah achaanak usakee or mudee aur bolee,

"alavida, chaarls, kya aap vaastav mein needaralaind mein ek nrty ka dhyaan karane mein gambheer hain? - main aapako salaah doonga, isase pahale ki aap ise nirdhaarit karen, vartamaan paartee kee ichchhaon se paraamarsh karane ke lie; main bahut galat hoon agar hamaare beech kuchh nahin hain; jinake lie gend khushee ke bajaay saja hogee. ”

"yadi aap daarsee ka matalab hai," usake bhaee roya, "vah bistar par ja sakata hai, agar vah chhusais, shuroo hone se pahale - lekin gend ke lie ke roop mein, yah kaaphee sulajhee huee baat hai, aur jaise hee nikols ne saphed soop ko paryaapt bana diya hai; mere kaard raund bhej denge. "

"mujhe gendon ko aseem roop se behatar pasand karana chaahie," usane javaab diya, "agar unhen ek alag tareeke se kiya gaya tha, lekin is tarah kee baithak kee saamaany prakriya mein kuchh anuchit hai. yah nishchit roop se bahut adhik tarkasangat hoga yadi nrty ke bajaay tarkasangat hoga. din ka kram bana. "

"bahut adhik tarkasangat, mere priy kairolin, main kahane kee himmat karata hoon, lekin yah gend kee tarah bahut kareeb nahin hoga."

mis bingale ne koee javaab nahin diya; aur jald hee uthakar kamare ke baare mein chala gaya. usakee aakrti suruchipoorn thee, aur vah achchhee tarah se chalee; —lekin daarsee, jis par yah sab lakshit tha, abhee bhee anamy roop se adhyayanasheel thee. usakee bhaavanaon kee hataasha mein usane ek prayaas mein adhik hal kiya; aur, elijaabeth kee or mudakar kaha,

"mis elija benet, mujhe apane udaaharan ka paalan karane ke lie mana len, aur kamare ke baare mein baaree le len. - main aapako vishvaas dilaata hoon ki ek drshtikon mein itane lambe samay tak baithane ke baad yah bahut taaza hai."

elijaabeth aashcharyachakit thee, lekin turant isake lie sahamat ho gaee. mis bingale apanee naagarikata kee vaastavik vastu mein kam saphal nahin huee; mistar daarsee ne dekha. vah us timaahee mein dhyaan kee naveenata ke lie utana hee jaagrt tha jitana ki elijaabeth svayan ho sakatee hai, aur anajaane mein apanee pustak band kar dee. unhen seedhe apanee paartee mein shaamil hone ke lie aamantrit kiya gaya tha, lekin unhonne ise asveekaar kar diya, yah dekhate hue ki vah kalpana kar sakate hain, lekin unake chuing ke lie do iraadon ke saath-saath kamare mein oopar aur neeche chalana, jinamen se kisee bhee uddeshy se unake shaamil hone mein hastakshep hoga. "usaka kya matalab ho sakata hai? vah yah jaanana chaah rahee thee ki usaka kya arth ho sakata hai" - aur elijaabeth se poochha ki kya vah use samajh sakatee hai?

"bilkul nahin," usaka javaab tha; "lekin yah nirbhar karata hai, vah ham par gambheer hone ka matalab hai
bahanon ke beech ek samajhaute ke parinaamasvaroop, elijaabeth ne agalee subah apanee maan ko likha, bheekh maangane ke lie ki gaadee ko din ke samay unake lie bheja jae. lekin shreematee benet, jinhonne apanee betiyon kee ganana agale mangalavaar tak nedarapheeld mein shesh bachee thee, jo jen ke saptaah ko pooree tarah se samaapt kar dengee, unhen khud ko pahale khushee ke saath praapt karane ke lie nahin laaya ja sakata tha. isalie, usaka javaab bhavishyavakta nahin tha, kam se kam elijaabeth kee ichchhaon ke lie nahin, kyonki vah ghar paane ke lie adheer thee. shreematee benet ne unhen yah shabd bheja ki ve sambhavatah mangalavaar se pahale gaadee nahin le sakate; aur usakee postaskript mein yah joda gaya tha, ki yadi mistar bingale aur usakee bahan ne unhen adhik samay tak rahane ke lie dabaaya, to vah unhen bahut achchhee tarah se bakhsh sakata hai. - haalaanki, lambe samay tak rahane ke baavajood, elijaabeth sakaaraatmak roop se hal ho gaee thee - aur na hee usane yah apeksha kee thee ki use poochha jaega ; aur bhayabheet, isake vipareet, jaisa ki khud ko zaroorat se zyaada lamba ghusapaith karane vaala maana jaata hai, usane jen se shree bingale kee gaadee ko turant udhaar lene ka aagrah kiya, aur lambaee par yah tay kiya gaya ki us subah needaralainds chhodane ke unake mool dijain ka ullekh kiya jaana chaahie, aur anurodh kiya gaya .

sanchaar ne chinta ke kaee vyavasaayon ko uttejit kiya; aur jen ke kaam karane ke lie agale din tak kam se kam rahane ke lie unhen badhaee dene ke lie paryaapt tha; aur du: kh tak, unake jaane ko taal diya gaya. mis bingale ko tab aphasos hua ki usane deree ka prastaav diya tha, usakee eershya ke lie aur ek bahan ke prati aruchi doosare ke prati sneh se adhik thee.

ghar ke maalik ne vaastavik vyatha ke saath suna ki ve itanee jaldee jaane vaale the, aur baar-baar mis benet ko manaane kee koshish kee ki yah usake lie surakshit nahin hoga - ki vah paryaapt baraamad nahin thee; lekin jen drdh tha jahaan usane khud ko sahee samajha.

mistar daarsee ke lie yah svaagat yogy buddhimatta thee - elijaabeth kaaphee lambe samay se nedarapheeld mein thee. usane use apanee pasand se adhik aakarshit kiya - aur mis bingale usake lie asabhy tha, aur khud ko saamaany se adhik teeking. unhonne buddhimaanee se vishesh roop se saavadhaan rahane ka sankalp liya ki prashansa ka koee sanket ab use bachana chaahie, aisa kuchh bhee nahin jo use usakee gundaagardee ko prabhaavit karane kee ummeed se ooncha kar sake; samajhadaar hai ki agar is tarah ke vichaar ka sujhaav diya gaya tha, to antim din ke dauraan usake vyavahaar kee pushti ya use kuchalane mein bhautik vajan hona chaahie. apane uddeshy ke lie sthir, usane poore shanivaar ke maadhyam se usase das shabd bole, aur haalaanki ve ek samay mein aadhe ghante ke lie khud ko chhod dete the, usane apanee pustak ke lie sabase adhik sajagata se paalan kiya, aur usakee or dekha bhee nahin.

ravivaar ko, subah kee seva ke baad, alagaav, lagabhag sabhee ke lie sahamat ho gaya. elijaabeth ke lie mis bingale kee naagarikata bahut tejee se badhee, saath hee jen ke prati unaka sneh bhee badha; aur jab unhonne bhaag liya, to khushee ke uttaraardh ko aashvast karane ke baad yah hamesha use longaboran ya nedarapheeld mein dekhane ke lie dega, aur use sabase komalata se gale lagaate hue, usane pahale se haath milaaya.-elijaabeth ne pooree paartee ko chhod diya jeevant aatmaen.

unakee maan dvaara bahut sauhaardapoorvak ghar mein svaagat nahin kiya gaya. shreematee benet ne unake aane par aashchary jataaya, aur socha ki unhen itanee pareshaanee dena bahut galat hai, aur yakeen hai ki jen ne phir se thandee pakad lee hogee. - lekin unake pita, haalaanki khushee ke bhaavon mein bahut hee sust the, unhen dekhakar vaastav mein khushee huee; unhonne parivaar ke daayare mein apana mahatv mahasoos kiya tha. shaam kee baatacheet, jab ve sabhee ikatthe hue the, jen aur elijaabeth kee anupasthiti mein, apane eneemeshan ka bahut kuchh kho diya tha, aur lagabhag sabhee arthon mein.

unhonne mairee ko hamesha kee tarah, gahan baas aur maanav prakrti ke adhyayan mein gahara paaya; aur prashansa karane ke lie kuchh nae ark the, aur sunane ke lie thred-nange naitikata ke kuchh nae avalokan. kaithareen aur lida ke paas unake lie alag tarah kee jaanakaaree thee. bahut kuchh kiya gaya tha, aur pichhale budhavaar se rejiment mein bahut kuchh kaha gaya tha; kaee adhikaariyon ne apane chaacha ke saath haal hee mein bhojan kiya tha, ek nijee jhagade hue the, aur yah vaastav mein sanket diya gaya tha ki karnal phostar shaadee karane ja rahe the.

mujhe aasha hai, mere priy," shree benet ne apanee patnee se kaha, kyonki ve agalee subah naashte par the, "ki aapane din ke khaane ke lie ek achchha bhojan ka aadesh diya hai, kyonki mere paas hamaare parivaar kee paartee ke lie ek atirikt ummeed hai. "

"aap kisase matalab rakhate hain, mere pyaare? main kisee ko nahin jaanata ki main aa raha hoon, jab tak ki shaarlot lukaas ko kol karane ke lie nahin hona chaahie, aur mujhe aasha hai ki mere dinar usake lie kaaphee achchhe hain. mujhe nahin lagata ki vah aksar ghar par aisa dekhatee hai. . "

"main jis vyakti se baat karata hoon, vah ek sajjan aur ajanabee hai." misez benet kee aankhen chamak utheen. - "ek sajjan aur ek ajanabee! yah mistar bingale mujhe yakeen hai. kyon jen-aapane kabhee is par ek shabd nahin chhoda; aap dhoort baat! khair, mujhe yakeen hai ki mujhe dekhakar bahut khushee hogee. mistar bingale. — lekin achchha bhagavaan! kaisa badakismat hai! din-bhar kee machhalee milane vaalee nahin hai. lida, mere pyaar, ghantee bajao. mujhe hil se bolana chaahie, is pal. isase ek saamaany vismay hua; aur unhen apanee patnee aur paanch betiyon se ek saath utsukata se poochhataachh karane kee khushee thee.

    apane aur mere svargeey sammaanit pita ke beech kee asahamati, hamesha mujhe bahut bechainee detee thee, aur jab se mujhe use khone ka durbhaagy hua hai, mainne aksar breech ko theek karane kee kaamana kee hai; lekin kuchh samay ke lie mujhe apane svayan ke sandeh se vaapas rakha gaya tha, aisa na ho ki aisa lagata hai ki yah meree smrti ke lie kisee bhee ek ke saath achchhe shabdon mein hone ke lie apamaanajanak lag sakata hai, jisake saath yah hamesha use vicharan karane ke lie prasann kar raha tha. - "vahaan, shreematee. benet. raat ke khaane ke dauraan, shree benet ghabarae hue the; lekin jab naukaron ko vaapas le liya gaya, to usane socha ki yah apane mehamaan ke saath kuchh baatacheet karane ka samay hai, aur isalie ek vishay shuroo kiya, jisamen usane ummeed kee ki vah usake sanrakshan mein bahut bhaagyashaalee lag raha hai. ledee kaithareen de borg ka unakee ichchhaon par dhyaan, aur unake aaraam ke lie vichaar, bahut ullekhaneey dikhaee diya. mistar benet ko behatar nahin chuna ja sakata tha. shree kolins usakee prashansa mein vaakpatu the. is vishay ne unhen saamaany se adhik tareeke se ooncha kar diya, aur ek sabase mahatvapoorn pahaloo ke saath unhonne virodh kiya ki unhonne apane jeevan mein kabhee bhee raink ke vyakti mein is tarah ke vyavahaar ko nahin dekha - aisa vyavahaaryata aur krpaaluta, jaisa ki unhonne khud ko ledee kaithareen se anubhav kiya tha. vah un donon pravachanon ko sveekaar karane ke lie anugrah se prasann ho gaya tha, jinhen usake pahale se hee upadesh ka sammaan praapt tha. usane do baar rojings mein bhojan karane ke lie bhee kaha tha, aur shaam ko kvaadril ka pool banaane ke lie usake lie keval shanivaar se pahale bheja tha. ledee kaithareen ko kaee aise logon par garv tha, jinhen vah jaanatee thee, lekin usane kabhee bhee kisee cheej ko dekha nahin tha, lekin usake andar usakee yogyata nahin thee. usane hamesha usase baat kee thee jaise vah kisee any sajjan se karegee; usane pados ke samaaj mein shaamil hone ke lie sabase chhotee aapatti nahin kee, aur na hee apane sambandhon ko dekhane ke lie, ek ya do saptaah ke lie kabhee-kabhee apane pallee ko chhod diya. usane use salaah dee thee ki vah use jald se jald shaadee karane kee salaah de, kyonki usane vivek ke saath use chuna tha; aur ek baar unhen apane vinamr abhivaadan mein ek yaatra ka bhugataan kiya tha; jahaan usane apane dvaara kie gae sabhee parivartanon ko pooree tarah se manjooree de dee thee, aur yahaan tak ki kuchh khud ko sujhaav dene ke lie vauchasaphed kiya tha, - seedhiyon ke oopar kee alamaariyon mein kuchh alamaariyon.

shreematee benet ne kaha, "yah sab bahut hee uchit aur sabhy hai, mujhe yakeen hai," aur main kahatee hoon ki vah bahut hee sahamat mahila hain. yah ek daya hai ki saamaany taur par mahaan mahilaen unake jaisee nahin hotee hain. aap shreemaan?"

"jis bageeche mein mera vinamr vaas hai, use roshan paark kee ek galee se alag kiya gaya hai, jo usake nivaas sthaan hai."

"mujhe lagata hai ki aapane kaha tha ki vah ek vidhava thee, shreemaan? kya unaka koee parivaar hai?"

"unakee ek hee betee hai, rozings kee uttaraadhikaarinee, aur bahut vyaapak sampatti kee."

"aah!" shreematee benet ne apana sir hilaate hue kaha, "to vah kaee ladakiyon se behatar hai. aur vah kis tarah kee yuva mahila hai? kya vah sundar hai?"

"vah vaastav mein ek sabase aakarshak yuva mahila hai. ledee kaithareen khud kahatee hain ki sachchee sundarata ke maamale mein, mis dee borg apane seks ke lie sabase behatar hain, kyonki unakee visheshataen hain jo vishisht janm kee yuva mahila ko chihnit karatee hain. vah durbhaagy se ek beemaar sanvidhaan hai, jisane use kaee upalabdhiyon mein vah pragati karane se rok diya hai, jise vah viphal nahin kar sakatee thee, jaisa ki mujhe us mahila dvaara soochit kiya gaya hai jisane apanee shiksha ko adheekshan kiya tha, aur jo abhee bhee unake saath rahatee hai. pooree tarah se milanasaar, aur aksar apane chhote se ghar aur tattoo mein mere vinamr nivaas dvaara draiv karane ke lie krpaalu. "

"kya use prastut kiya gaya hai? mujhe adaalat mein mahilaon ke beech usaka naam yaad nahin hai."

"svaasthy ke prati usakee udaaseen avastha use shahar mein rahane se rokatee hai; aur us maadhyam se, jaisa ki mainne ek din ledee kaithareen ko bataaya tha, usane british kort ko usake sabase chamakeele aabhooshan se vanchit kar diya hai. usakee laadalee is vichaar se prasann thee, aur aap kalpana kar sakate hain. main har mauke par un chhotee naajuk taareephon kee peshakash karata hoon, jo hamesha mahilaon ko sveekaary hotee hain. mujhe ledee kaithareen ke lie ek se adhik baar dekha gaya hai, ki unakee aakarshak betee ek khoobasoorat mahila ke roop mein janm letee hai, aur yah sabase ooncha pad dene ke bajaay usaka parinaam, usake dvaara sushobhit hoga. — ye ek prakaar kee chhotee-chhotee baaten hain, jo use prasannata pradaan karatee hain, aur yah ek prakaar ka dhyaan hai jo main svayan ko bhugataan karane ke lie baadhy karata hoon. ”

"aap bahut sahee tareeke se nyaay karate hain," shree benet ne kaha, "aur yah aapake lie khushee kee baat hai ki aap vinamrata ke saath chaapaloosee karane kee pratibha rakhate hain. kya main poochh sakata hoon ki kya ye manabhaavan upasthiti pal ke aaveg se aage badhate hain, ya pichhale ka parinaam hain. adhyayan?"

"ve mukhy roop se us samay se gujar rahe hain, aur haalaanki main kabhee-kabhee khud ko sujhaav deta hoon aur aisee chhotee-chhotee taareephon kee vyavastha karata hoon, jinhen aam maukon ke anukool banaaya ja sakata hai, main hamesha unhen anachaahee hava dena chaahata hoon."

mistar benet kee ummeedon ka pooree tarah se javaab diya gaya. usaka chachera bhaee utana hee besudh tha jitana usane aasha kee thee, aur usane use sabase adhik aanand ke saath suna, ek hee samay mein sahavaas ke sabase drdh sankalp ko banae rakha, aur elijaabeth mein ek saamayik nazar ko chhodakar, usakee khushee mein kisee bhee saathee kee aavashyakata nahin thee.

chaay ke samay tak, lekin khuraak kaaphee ho chukee thee, aur mistar benet ko apane mehamaan ko phir se draing-room mein le jaane mein khushee huee, aur jab chaay khatm ho gaee, to unhen mahilaon ko jor se padhane ke lie aamantrit karane mein khushee huee. shree kolins ne aasaanee se aashvaasan diya, aur ek pustak ka utpaadan kiya gaya; lekin ise nihaarane par, (har cheez ke lie yah ek parisanchaaree pustakaalay se hone kee ghoshana kee), usane vaapas shuroo kiya, aur kshama maangate hue, virodh kiya ki vah kabhee upanyaas nahin padhata hai - kittee ne use dekha, aur lidiya ne kaha. - any pustakon ka utpaadan kiya gaya tha,
shree kolins ek samajhadaar aadamee nahin the, aur prakrti kee kamee shiksha ya samaaj dvaara thodee madad kee gaee thee; unake jeevan ka sabase bada hissa ek anapadh aur dukhee pita ke maargadarshan mein beeta; aur yadyapi vah vishvavidyaalayon mein se ek ke the, unhonne keval aavashyak sharton ko rakha tha, bina kisee upayogee parichit ke. jis adheenata mein unake pita ne unhen paala tha, unhonne mool roop se unhen bahut vinamrata dee thee, lekin yah ab kamajor sir ke aatm-dambh, sevaanivrtti mein rahane, aur jaldee aur apratyaashit kee parinaamee bhaavanaon se mukaabala karane ke lie ek achchha sauda tha. samrddhi. ek bhaagyashaalee avasar ne use ledee kaithareen de borg ke lie siphaarish kee thee jab hansaphord ke rahane kee jagah khaalee thee; aur jo sammaan usane apane uchch pad ke lie mahasoos kiya, aur apane sanrakshak ke roop mein usake lie usakee vandana, khud kee bahut achchhee raay ke saath sambhog, ek paadaree ke roop mein apane adhikaar, aur ek rektar ke roop mein usake adhikaaron ne, use pooree tarah se garv ka mishran bana diya. aur parinaam, aatm-mahatv aur vinamrata.

ab ek achchha ghar aur paryaapt aay hone ke baad, usane shaadee karane ka iraada kiya; aur longaborn parivaar ke saath saamanjasy sthaapit karane kee chaahat mein, unakee ek patnee thee, kyonki unaka matalab tha ki betiyon mein se ek ko chugaana, agar vah unhen sundar aur milanasaar lagatee hai, kyonki ve saamaany riport dvaara pratinidhitv karate the. yah unakee yojana thee - apane pita kee sampatti ko praapt karane ke lie praayashchitt kee - aur unhonne socha ki yah ek utkrsht ek hai, paatrata aur upayuktata se bhara hai, aur atyadhik udaar aur apane svayan ke hisse par udaaseen hai.

unakee yojana unhen dekhane par alag nahin huee. - mis benet ke pyaare chehare ne unake vichaaron kee pushti kee, aur varishthata ke kaaran unakee sabhee sakht dhaaranaon ko sthaapit kiya; aur pahalee shaam ke lie vah unakee pasand thee. agalee subah, haalaanki, ek parivartan kiya gaya; naashte se pahale shreematee benet ke saath ek ghante ke ek-de-tete ke ek ghante ke lie, ek baatacheet jo unake paarsan-haus se shuroo hotee hai, aur svaabhaavik roop se unakee aashaon ko poora karane ke lie agranee hotee hai, ki isake lie ek maalakin longaboran mein mil sakatee hai, jo utpaadan kiya gaya tha. usake beech se, bahut hee hansamukh muskuraahat aur saamaany protsaahan ke beech, usane jis jen ko theek kiya tha, usake khilaaph ek saavadhaanee. - "apanee chhotee betiyon ke roop mein vah kahane ke lie use nahin le sakatee thee - vah sakaaraatmak javaab nahin de sakatee thee - lekin use pata nahin tha kisee bhee poorvadhaarana; - sabase badee betee, use sirph ullekh karana chaahie - usane mahasoos kiya ki yah sanket karane ke lie us par avalambee hai, bahut jald sagaee hone kee sambhaavana thee. "

shree kolins ko keval jen se elijaabeth mein badalana tha — aur yah jald hee ho gaya tha - jabaki shreematee benet aag ko hila rahee thee. janm aur saundary mein jen ke bagal mein elijaabeth, use nishchit roop se saphal huee.

shreematee benet ne sanket diya, aur bharosa kiya ki jald hee unakee do betiyon kee shaadee ho sakatee hai; aur vah aadamee jise vah ek din pahale bolana sahan nahin kar sakee thee, ab usakee achchhee krpa thee.

meridatan chalane ke lie lida ka iraada bhula nahin gaya tha; mairee ko chhodakar har bahan usake saath jaane ko taiyaar ho gaee; aur mistar kolins, shree benet ke anurodh par, jo ki usase chhutakaara paane ke lie sabase adhik utsuk the, aur unake pustakaalay ko apane paas rakhane ke lie unhen shaamil karana tha; shree kolins ne naashte ke baad usaka peechha kiya tha, aur vahaan vah jaaree rahega, naamamaatr ke sangrah mein sabase bade pholiyo mein se ek ke saath, lekin vaastav mein mistar benet se baat karate hue, honaphord mein apane ghar aur bageeche ke chhote se bandan ke saath. is tarah ke kaaryon ne shree benet ko atyadhik visthaapit kar diya. apane pustakaalay mein vah hamesha aaraam aur shaanti ke baare mein nishchit tha; aur yadyapi taiyaar kiya gaya tha, jaisa ki usane elijaabeth se kaha, ghar mein har doosare kamare mein moorkhataapoorn aur dambh ke saath milane ke lie, vah vahaan se mukt ho jaata tha; isalie, shree kolins ko apanee betiyon ko apanee paidal yaatra mein shaamil hone ke lie aamantrit karane mein sabase adhik tatparata thee; aur shree kolins, vaastav mein ek paathak kee tulana mein ek vokar ke lie behatar roop se phit the, apanee badee pustak ko band karane aur jaane ke lie behad khush the.

unakee or se dhoomadhaam se, aur unake chachere bhaiyon par naagarik sahaayata ke lie, unaka samay meriyatan mein pravesh karane tak beet gaya. yuva logon ka dhyaan tab usake dvaara praapt karane ke lie nahin tha. unakee aankhen turant adhikaariyon kee talaash mein sadak par bhatak rahee theen, aur vaastav mein ek bahut smaart bonat se kam kuchh bhee nahin, ya ek dukaan kee khidakee mein vaastav mein ek naya malamal tha, jo unhen pun: praapt kar sakata tha.

lekin har mahila ka dhyaan jald hee ek yuvak ne pakad liya tha, jise unhonne pahale kabhee nahin dekha tha, jyaadaatar sajjan jaise dikhane vaale, raaste ke doosaree taraph ek adhikaaree ke saath chalate hue. vah adhikaaree bahut hee mistar denee the, jinake vishay mein landan se laute lidiya poochhataachh karane aae the, aur unhonne paas aate hee jhuk gae. sabhee ajanabee kee hava ke saath maare gae, sabhee aashcharyachakit the ki vah kaun ho sakata hai, aur kittee aur lida ne nirdhaarit kiya ki yadi sambhav ho to pata karen, sadak ke paar raaste ka netrtv kiya, ek vipareet dukaan mein kuchh chaahane ke dhong ke tahat, aur saubhaagy se bas praapt hua tha phutapaath jab do sajjan peechhe mudakar usee sthaan par pahunche the. mistar denee ne unhen seedhe sambodhit kiya, aur apane dost, shree vikam se milaane kee anumati dee, jo shahar se ek din pahale unake saath laute the, aur unhen yah kahate hue khushee huee ki unhonne kom sveekaar kar liya hai

choonki unakee chaachee ke saath yuva logon ke judaav par koee aapatti nahin kee gaee thee, aur mistar aur misez benet ko chhodane ke sabhee shree kolins kee apanee yaatra ke dauraan ek shaam ke lie sabase adhik drdhata se virodh kiya gaya tha, koch ne unhen aur unake paanchon bhaiyon ko is baat se avagat karaaya. mairyton ko upayukt ghante; aur ladakiyon ko sunane ka aanand tha, kyonki ve draing-room mein pravesh karatee theen, ki mistar vikam ne apane chaacha ke nimantran ko sveekaar kar liya tha, aur tab vah ghar mein theen.

jab yah jaanakaaree dee gaee, aur unhonne apanee sabhee seeten le leen, to shree kolins apane aas-paas dekhane aur prashansa karane ke lie itmeenaan se the, aur vah apaartament ke aakaar aur pharneechar ke saath itana maara gaya tha, ki usane ghoshana kee ki vah lagabhag maana jaata hai rozings mein chhote garmiyon ke naashte ke paarlar mein; ek tulana jo pahale bahut aabhaar vyakt nahin karatee thee; lekin jab shreematee philips ne unhen samajha ki rosings kya theen, aur isake maalik kaun the, jab unhonne ledee kaithareen ke draing-room mein se keval ek ka varnan suna tha, aur paaya ki akele chimanee-pees kee keemat aath sau paund thee, vah taareeph ke sabhee bal mahasoos kiya, aur shaayad hee grhasvaamee ke kamare ke saath tulana naaraajagee hogee.

ledee kaithareen aur usakee havelee kee sabhee bhavyata ka varnan karane ke lie, apane svayan ke vinamr nivaas kee prashansa mein saamayik khudaee ke saath, aur ise praapt karane vaale sudhaar, vah khushee se kaaryarat the jab tak ki sajjan log unake saath shaamil nahin hue; aur unhonne misej philips ko ek bahut hee chaukas shrota paaya, jisake parinaam ke baare mein usakee raay badh gaee, jo usane suna, aur jo apane padosiyon ke beech jitanee jaldee ho sake use ritel karane ka sankalp le rahee thee. ladakiyon ke lie, jo apane chachere bhaee kee baat nahin sun sakatee theen, aur jinake paas saadhan ke lie ichchha karane ke alaava kuchh bhee nahin tha, aur mental-pees par cheen kee apanee udaaseen nakal kee jaanch karane ke lie, prateeksha ka antaraal bahut lamba dikhaee diya. haalaanki yah pichhale khatm ho gaya tha. sajjanon ne drshtikon kiya; aur jab shree vikam kamare mein chale gae, to elijaabeth ne mahasoos kiya ki vah na to pahale unhen dekh rahee thee, aur na hee usake baare mein soch rahee thee, kyonki vah sabase chhotee thee. -shree ke adhikaaree saamaany roop se ek bahut hee vishvasaneey, sajjan vyakti jaise the, aur unamen se adhikaansh vartamaan paartee ke the; lekin mistar vikam un sabhee se pare tha, jahaan vah vyakti, sahooliyat, hava, aur paidal chalata tha, kyonki ve vyaapak saamana karane vaale bharavaan chaacha philips, shvaas bandaragaah sharaab se behatar the, jo kamare mein unaka peechha karate the.

mistar vikam vah khushamijaaj aadamee tha jisakee or lagabhag har mahila kee nazar jaatee thee, aur elijaabeth vah khushamijaaj mahila thee jisake dvaara aakhirakaar usane khud ko baithaaya; aur jis tarah se vah turant baatacheet mein gir gaya, haalaanki yah keval geelee raat hone par tha, aur ek barasaat ke mausam kee sambhaavana par, use lagata hai ki sabase aam, sust, sabase thred-nange vishay dilachasp ho sakata hai vakta ke kaushal se.

mele kee soochana ke lie is tarah ke pratidvandviyon ke saath, mistar vikam aur adhikaariyon ke roop mein, shree kolins ko asambhaavana mein doobane kee sambhaavana thee; yuva mahilaon ke lie vah nishchit roop se kuchh bhee nahin tha; lekin vah abhee bhee shreematee philips mein ek dayaalu shrota ke roop mein antaraal par tha, aur usakee ghadee ke anusaar, kophee aur maphin ke saath sabase adhik aapoorti kee jaatee thee.

jab kaard tebal rakha gaya tha, to usake paas badale mein use baithane ke lie majaboor karane ka ek avasar tha, neeche baithakar.

unhonne kaha, "vartamaan mein main khel ke baare mein bahut kam jaanata hoon, lekin mujhe apane jeevan kee sthiti ke lie khud ko sudhaarane mein khushee hogee-" shreematee philips apane anupaalan ke lie bahut aabhaaree theen, lekin unake lie intajaar nahin kar sakatee theen kaaran.

mistar vikam seetee mein nahin khelate the, aur taiyaar khushee ke saath unhen elijaabeth aur lida ke beech doosaree tebal par mila tha. pahale to leediya ka use pooree tarah se gherane ka khatara tha, kyonki vah ek sabase drdh baat karane vaalee thee; lekin isee tarah lotaree tikaton ke behad shaukeen hone ke kaaran, vah jald hee khel mein bahut adhik dilachaspee letee thee, vishesh roop se kisee ek ke lie dhyaan aakarshit karane ke lie, puraskaar banaane ke baad aur puraskaar praapt karane ke lie bahut utsuk thee. khel kee saamaany maangon ke kaaran, shree vikam elijaabeth se baat karane ke lie avakaash par tha, aur vah use sunane ke lie bahut ichchhuk thee, haalaanki vah mukhy roop se jo sunana chaahatee thee, vah usake parichit ke itihaas ke baare mein nahin bataaya ja sakata tha. mistar daarsee ke saath. usane us sajjan ka jikr tak nahin kiya. usakee jigyaasa haalaanki apratyaashit roop se raahat milee thee. shree vikam ne svayan vishay shuroo kiya. unhonne poochhataachh kee ki mairyton se needaralaind kitanee door tha; aur, usaka uttar praapt karane ke baad, sankochavash tareeke se poochha ki mistar daarsee kitane samay tak vahaan rahe the.

"ek maheene ke baare mein," elijaabeth ne kaha; aur phir, vishay ko chhodane dene ke lie anichchhuk, joda, "vah darbeeshaayar mein bahut badee sampatti ka aadamee hai, main samajhata hoon."

elijaabeth nahin balki aashcharyachakit dikh sakatee thee.

"aap achchhee tarah se aashcharyachakit ho sakate hain, mis benet, is tarah ke daave par, dekhane ke baad,
elijaabeth jen se sambandhit agale din, shree vikam aur khud ke beech kya hua tha. jen ne vismay aur chinta ke saath suna; —vah nahin jaanata tha ki kaise vishvaas karana hai ki mistar daarsee shree bingale ke sambandh ke itane ayogy ho sakate hain; aur phir bhee, vikam ke roop mein is tarah ke milanasaar upasthiti ke ek yuva vyakti kee satyata par savaal uthaana usake svabhaav mein nahin tha. — usakee vaastav mein is tarah kee bedardee se peedit hone kee sambhaavana, usakee sabhee komal bhaavanaon ko ruchi dene ke lie paryaapt thee; aur isalie kuchh bhee nahin kiya gaya, lekin un donon ko achchhee tarah se sochane ke lie, pratyek ke aacharan ka bachaav karane ke lie, aur durghatana ya galatee ke kaaran, jo bhee anyatha nahin bataaya ja sakata hai, phenk diya.

"ve donon hain," usane kaha, "dhokha diya gaya hai, main kahata hoon, kisee tarah ya any, jisamen se ham koee vichaar nahin bana sakate hain. ichchhuk logon ne sambhavatah ek-doosare ko galat tareeke se prastut kiya hai. yah sankshep mein, hamaare lie asambhav hai. un kaaranon ya paristhitiyon ko vyakt karane ke lie, jinhonne unhen alag-thalag kar diya hai, donon taraph vaastavik dosh ke bina. "

"bahut sach, vaastav mein - aur ab, mere priy jen, aapako un ichchhuk logon kee or se kya kahana hai, jo shaayad vyavasaay mein chintit hain? - unhen bhee saaph karen, ya ham beemaar ke baare mein sochane ke lie baadhy honge koee."

"jitana aap hansate hain utana hansate hain, lekin aap meree raay se baahar nahin hansenge. mere sabase pyaare lizee, karate hain, lekin is baat par vichaar karen ki yah kitana ghrnit prakaash hai shree daarsee, apane pita ke pasandeeda ka is tarah se vyavahaar karane ke lie, - , jinake pita ne pradaan karane ka vaada kiya tha. — yah asambhav hai. koee bhee saamaany maanavata ka aadamee nahin, koee bhee aisa vyakti jisake paas apane charitr ke lie koee mooly nahin hai, vah isake lie saksham ho sakata hai. kya usake sabase antarang dost usake saath bahut adhik dhokha de sakate hain? ! nahin."

"main bahut aasaanee se vishvaas kar sakata hoon ki mistar bingale ko lagaaya ja raha hai, isase shree vikm ko khud ka aisa itihaas eejaad karana chaahie jaisa unhonne kal raat mujhe diya tha; naam, tathy, bina samaaroh ke ullekhit har baat. — agar aisa nahin hai, to shree daarsee ne isaka khandan kiya. isake alaava, unake luk mein sachchaee thee. "

"yah vaastav mein mushkil hai - yah chintaajanak hai. - kisee ko nahin pata ki kya sochana hai."

elijaabeth aisee shuruaat ke ek nishkarsh par muskura nahin sakatee thee; lekin shreematee benet, jinhonne khud ko samajha diya tha ki unake pati ne unakee ichchha ke anusaar sambandh ko maana, atyadhik niraash the.

"is tarah se baat karake, shree benet, aapaka kya matalab hai? aapane mujhe usase shaadee karane par jor dene ka vaada kiya tha."

"mere pyaare," ne apane pati ko javaab diya, "mere paas anurodh karane ke lie do chhote ehasaan hain. pahala, ki aap mujhe vartamaan avasar par meree samajh ka mupht upayog karane kee anumati denge; aur doosaree baat, mere kamare kee. mujhe khushee hogee. jitanee jaldee ho sake khud ko pustakaalay.

haalaanki, abhee tak, apane pati mein niraasha ke baavajood, shreematee benet ne is baat ko nahin chhoda. usane baar-baar elijaabeth se baat kee; baaree-baaree se use sahalaaya aur dhamakaaya. usane jen ko usake hit mein surakshit karane ka prayaas kiya, lekin jen ne har sambhav saumyata ke saath hastakshep karane se mana kar diya; -aur elijaabeth kabhee vaastavik eemaanadaaree se aur kabhee-kabhee chanchal ullaas ke saath usake hamalon ka javaab detee thee. haalaanki usaka tareeka alag tha, lekin usaka drdh nishchay kabhee nahin hua.

is beech, shree kolins, jo beet chuka tha, ekaant mein dhyaan kar rahe the. usane khud hee socha tha ki usaka chachera bhaee use mana kar sakata hai ya nahin; aur haalaanki unake abhimaan ko chot pahunchee thee, lekin unhen kisee any tareeke se nukasaan nahin hua unake lie unaka sambandh kaaphee kaalpanik tha; 
shree kolins kee peshakash kee charcha ab lagabhag samaapt ho gaee thee, aur elijaabeth ko keval asuvidhaajanak bhaavanaon se peedit hone ke lie jarooree tha, aur kabhee-kabhee apanee maan ke kuchh peevash sanlayan se. khud sajjan ke lie, unakee bhaavanaon ko mukhy roop se vyakt kiya gaya tha, na ki sharmindagee ya aapatti se, ya usase bachane kee koshish karake, lekin dhang se aur krodhapoorn chuppee se. vah shaayad hee kabhee usase baat karata tha, aur vah adig atenshan jo vah khud samajhadaar tha, baakee din mis lukaas ke lie sthaanaantarit kar diya gaya tha, jisakee baat sunane mein usakee shishtata un sabhee ke lie ek vishesh roop se raahat dene vaalee thee, aur vishesh roop se usake dost.

du: kh ne shreematee benet ke beemaar haasy ya beemaar svaasthy ka koee unmoolan nahin kiya. shree kolins bhee gusse mein garv kee sthiti mein the. elijaabeth ko ummeed thee ki unakee naaraajagee unakee yaatra ko chhota kar sakatee hai, lekin unakee yojana isase kam prabhaavit nahin huee. vah hamesha shanivaar ko gaya tha, aur shanivaar ko vah abhee bhee rahane ke lie tha.

naashte ke baad, ladakiyaan mistar vikam ke lautane aur nedarapheeld bol se usakee anupasthiti par vilaap karane ke lie poochhataachh karane ke lie merittan chalee gaeen. vah unake shahar mein pravesh karane par unake saath shaamil ho gaya aur unhen unakee chaachee ke paas le gaya, jahaan unake aphasos aur duhkh aur har shareer kee chinta par achchhee tarah se baat kee gaee thee. - haalaanki, elijaabeth ne, unhonne svechchha se sveekaar kiya ki unakee anupasthiti kee aavashyakata svayan thee thopa hua.

"mainne paaya," unhonne kaha, "jaise hee samay nikat aaya, ki main mistar daarsee se behatar dhang se nahin mila; - ek hee kamare mein rahane ke lie, ek hee paartee mein ek saath itane ghanton tak, main isase jyaada ho sakata hai sahan kar sakata hai, aur vah drshy apane aap se adhik apriy ho sakata hai. "

usane apanee manaahee ko bahut manjooree de dee, aur ve isake baare mein pooree charcha ke lie avakaash praapt kar chuke the, aur sabhee prashansaon ke lie, jo unhonne sabhy roop se ek-doosare ko dee thee, jaisa ki vikam aur ek any adhikaaree unake saath longaboran ke lie vaapas chale gae, aur chalane ke dauraan, unhonne vishesh roop se bhaag liya usake lie. unake saath unaka dohara laabh tha; usane khud ko dee gaee sabhee taareephon ko mahasoos kiya, aur use apane pita aur maan se milaane ke avasar ke roop mein yah sabase sveekaary tha.

unake lautane ke turant baad, mis benet ko ek patr vitarit kiya gaya; yah needaralaind ke kshetr se aaya tha, aur turant khola gaya tha. liphaaphe mein suruchipoorn, chhote, garm dabae gae pepar kee ek sheet thee, jo achchhee tarah se ek mahila ke mele ke saath kavar kiya gaya tha, bahata hua haath; aur elijaabeth ne apanee bahan ke parivartan ko padhate hue dekha, aur kuchh vishesh maargon par use sahajata se dekha. jen ne jald hee khud ko yaad kiya, aur patr ko door rakha, saamaany baatacheet mein use hamesha khush rahane kee koshish kee; lekin elijaabeth ne is vishay par ek chinta mahasoos kee, jisane vikam se bhee usaka dhyaan aakarshit kiya; aur jald hee unake aur unake saathee ne chhuttee nahin lee, jen kee ek nazar se use seedhiyon se chalane ke lie aamantrit kiya. jab unhonne apana kamara praapt kar liya, to jen ne patr nikaalate hue kaha,

"yah kairolin bingale se hai; isamen kya shaamil hai, ne mujhe ek achchha sauda aashcharyachakit kar diya hai. is samay tak pooree paartee ne needaralaind ko chhod diya hai, aur shahar jaane ke apane raaste par hain, aur phir se vaapas aane ke kisee bhee iraade ke bina. aap sunenge ki vah kya hai. kahate hain. "

isake baad usane pahala vaaky padha, jisamen unake bhaee ko seedhe shahar jaane ke lie hal karane kee jaanakaaree thee, aur grosavenar galee mein us din bhojan karane ka unaka arth tha, jahaan mistar harst ka ghar tha. agala inheen shabdon mein tha. "main apane samaaj, apane sabase pyaare dost ko chhodakar, hartaphordashaayar mein kisee bhee cheej par pachhataava karane ka naatak nahin karata; lekin ham bhavishy mein hone vaale sambhog ke kaee ritarn ka aanand lene ke lie aur aane vaale samay mein kuchh ummeed karenge." bahut lagaataar aur sabase adhik patraachaar dvaara alagaav ke dard ko kam karana. main usake lie aap par nirbhar hoon. " in uchch pravaah vaale bhaavon ke lie, elijaabeth ne avishvaas kee sabhee asanvedanasheelata ko suna; aur yadyapi unake nishkaasan kee achaanakata ne use aashcharyachakit kar diya, usane dekha ki vaastav mein vilaap karane ke lie isamen kuchh bhee nahin hai; yah maana nahin jaana chaahie tha ki needaralaind se unakee anupasthiti shree bingale ke vahaan hone se rok sakatee hai; aur apane samaaj ke nukasaan ke roop mein, vah is baat ke lie raajee thee ki jen ko jald hee is sambandh mein, usake aanand mein sangharsh karana band kar dena chaahie.

"yah ashubh hai," usane kaha, ek chhote viraam ke baad, "ki aapako desh chhodane se pahale apane doston ko dekhane mein saksham nahin hona chaahie. lekin kya ham aasha nahin kar sakate ki bhavishy kee khushee kee avadhi jis par mis bingale aage dikhatee hain, ho sakata hai." isase pahale ki vah sajag ho jae, aur vah ramaneey sambhog jise aap mitr ke roop mein jaanate hain, usakee nae sire se bahanon ke roop mein nae sire se pata chalega? - shreematee bingale ko unake dvaara landan mein hiraasat mein nahin liya jaega. "

"kairoleen ne spasht roop se kaha ki paartee ka koee bhee vyakti is sardiyon mein hartaphordashaayar mein nahin lautega. main aapako ise padhoonga-

"jab mere bhaee ne kal hamen chhod diya, to unhonne kalpana kee ki jo vyavasaay unhen landan le gaya tha, vah teen ya chaar dinon mein samaapt ho sakata hai, lekin jaisa ki ham nishchit hain ki yah aisa nahin ho sakata hai, aur saath hee yah aashvast hai ki jab chaarls shahar jaata hai , vah phir se chhodane ke lie jaldee mein nahin hoga

benet lukaas ke saath bhojan karane ke lie lage hue the, aur phir se din ke pramukh ke dauraan mis lukaas itane dayaalu the jaise ki shree kolins ko sunana. elijaabeth ne use dhanyavaad dene ka avasar liya. "yah use achchhe haasy mein rakhata hai," usane kaha, "aur main jitana abhivyakt kar sakata hoon, usase adhik aap ke lie baadhy hain." shaarlet ne apanee santushti mein apane dost ko upayogee hone ka aashvaasan diya, aur kaha ki yah usake samay ke chhote se balidaan ke lie use chukaaya. yah bahut hee anukool tha, lekin elijaabeth kee tulana mein shaarlot kee dayaaluta mein koee antar nahin tha; -is vastu se kam kuchh bhee nahin tha, shree kolins ke pate ke kisee bhee vaapasee se use surakshit karane kee tulana mein, unhen apanee or aakarshit karake. aisee thee mis lukaas kee yojana; aur dikhaave itane anukool the ki jab ve raat mein bhaag lete the, to vah saphalata ke lagabhag nishchit mahasoos karatee thee yadi vah itanee jaldee hartaphordashaayar chhodane ke lie nahin gaee thee. lekin yahaan, usane apane charitr kee aag aur svatantrata ke saath anyaay kiya, isake lie use agalee subah longabarn haus se baahar nikalane ke lie saraahaneey dhoortata ke saath bhaagana pada, aur lukaas loj ko jaldabaajee mein apane pairon par phenkana pada. vah apane chachere bhaiyon ke notis se bachane ke lie utsuk tha, ek drdh vishvaas se ki agar unhonne use vida hote dekha, to ve usake dijain ko khaarij karane mein viphal nahin ho sakate the, aur vah is prayaas ko tab tak karane ke lie taiyaar nahin tha jab tak ki usakee saphalata isee tarah nahin jaanee ja sakatee; haalaanki, lagabhag surakshit mahasoos karane ke lie, aur kaaran ke saath, chaarlot ke lie sahanasheel roop se utsaahajanak tha, vah budhavaar ke saahasik kaary ke baad se tulanaatmak roop se alag tha. haalaanki unaka svaagat sabase chaapaloosee ka tha. mis lukaas ne use ooparee khidakee se maana tha kyonki vah ghar kee or chalee thee, aur turant galatee se use galee mein milane ke lie nikal padee. lekin bahut kam hee use yah ummeed thee ki itana pyaar aur vaakpatuta usaka vahaan intajaar kar rahee thee.

shree kolins ke lambe bhaashanon kee anumati ke roop mein kam samay mein, donon ke beech santosh karane ke lie har cheej unake beech basa dee gaee thee; aur jaise hee ve ghar mein daakhil hue, unhonne eemaanadaaree se use us din ka naam dene ke lie ukasaaya, jo use sabase jyaada khush karane vaala tha; aur yadyapi is tarah ke aagrah ko vartamaan ke lie laharaaya jaana chaahie, lekin mahila ko apanee khushee ke saath chhedachhaad karane mein koee jhukaav mahasoos nahin hua. jis moorkhata ke saath vah svabhaav ka pakshadhar tha, use kisee bhee aakarshan se apanee premaalaap kee raksha karanee chaahie jo ek mahila ko usakee nirantarata kee kaamana kar sakatee hai; aur mis lukaas, jinhonne unhen pooree tarah se ek sthaapana kee shuddh aur udaaseen ichchha se sveekaar kiya, paravaah nahin thee ki sthaapana kitanee jaldee praapt huee thee.

sar viliyam aur ledee lukaas ko unakee sahamati ke lie tejee se laagoo kiya gaya tha; aur ise sabase adhik khushee ke saath diya gaya tha. shree kolins kee vartamaan paristhitiyon ne ise unakee betee ke lie sabase yogy maich bana diya, jinake lie ve bahut kam bhaagy de sakate the; aur bhavishy ke dhan kee usakee sambhaavanaen kaaphee had tak uchit theen. ledee lukaas ne seedhe taur par is baat se adhik dilachaspee ke saath ganana karana shuroo kar diya ki is maamale ne pahale kabhee utsaahit nahin kiya tha, shree benet ke kitane saal rahane kee sambhaavana thee; aur sar viliyam ne ise apanee nishchit raay ke roop mein diya, ki jab bhee shree kolins ko longaboran estet ke kabje mein hona chaahie, to yah bahut sameecheen hoga ki vah aur unakee patnee donon sent jems mein apanee upasthiti banaen. sankshep mein poore parivaar ko is avasar par bahut khushee huee. chhotee ladakiyon ne ek ya do saal baad aane kee ummeed kee, jitana ki shaayad unhonne kiya ho; aur sherlot kee puraanee naukaraanee ke marane kee aashanka se ladakon ko raahat milee. shaarlot khud sahanasheel the. vah apanee baat par adee huee thee, aur usake paas is par vichaar karane ka samay tha. usake pratibimb saamaany santoshajanak the. shree kolins sunishchit karane ke lie na to samajhadaar the aur na hee sahamat the; unaka samaaj apamaanajanak tha, aur unake prati unaka lagaav kaalpanik hona chaahie. lekin phir bhee vah usaka pati hoga. — bina kisee purush ya vivaah ke atyadhik vichaar kie, vivaah hamesha usakee vastu rahee; yah chhote bhaagy kee achchhee tarah se shikshit yuva mahilaon ke lie ekamaatr sammaanajanak praavadhaan tha, aur haalaanki khushee dene ke lie anishchit tha, ve chaahate hain ki unaka sabase sukhad sanrakshak ho. yah parirakshak vah ab praapt kiya tha; aur sattaees saal kee umr mein, kabhee sundar nahin hone ke kaaran, use yah sab achchha laga. vyaapaar mein kam se kam sahamat hone vaalee sthiti, yah aashchary kee baat thee ki yah elijaabeth benet ke paas hona chaahie, jisakee dostee vah kisee any vyakti se pare thee. elijaabeth aashcharyachakit hogee, aur shaayad use dosh degee; aur yadyapi usake sankalp ko hilaana nahin tha, usakee bhaavanaon ko is tarah kee asveekrti se aahat hona chaahie. usane khud ko isakee jaanakaaree dene ka sankalp liya aur isalie shree kolins par aarop lagaaya ki jab vah longabarn se raat ke khaane par lauteen, to parivaar ke kisee bhee vyakti ke saamane jo kuchh bhee hua tha, usaka koee sanket chhodane ke lie. gopaneeyata ka ek vaada beshak bahut kartavyaparaayanata se diya gaya tha, lekin ise bina kathinaee ke nahin rakha ja sakata tha; apanee lambee anupasthiti se utsaahit jigyaasa ke lie, apanee vaapasee par is tarah ke bahut seedhe prashnon mein aage badhen, kyonki unhen baahar nikalane ke lie kuchh saralata kee aavashyakata thee, aur vah usee samay mahaan aatm-nishedh ka abhyaas kar rahe the, kyonki vah apane samrddh prem ko prakaashit karane ke lie taras rahe the.

choonki vah parivaar, samaaroh mein kisee bhee vyakti ko dekhane ke lie apanee yaatra kee shuruaat duhkh kee shuruaat mein karata tha.

elijaabeth apanee maan aur bahanon ke saath baithee thee, jo usane sunee thee, us par pratibimbit karatee hai, aur is baat par sandeh karate hue ki kya vah isaka ullekh karane ke lie adhikrt hain, jab sar viliyam lukaas svayan dikhaee die, apanee betee dvaara parivaar ko apanee sagaee kee ghoshana karane ke lie bheja. kaee taareephon ke saath, aur gharon ke beech sambandh kee sambhaavana par bahut aatm-santushti ke saath, unhonne is maamale ko ujaagar kiya, -ek darshakon ke lie na keval aashcharyachakit, balki avishvasaneey; shreematee benet ke lie, raajaneeti se adhik drdhata ke saath, virodh kiya ki unhen pooree tarah se galat hona chaahie, aur lida, hamesha bina soche samajhe aur aksar asabhy, uddandata se ukasaaya jaata hai,

"achchha bhagavaan! sar viliyam, aap is tarah kee kahaanee kaise suna sakate hain? —kya aap nahin jaanate ki mi. kolins lijee se shaadee karana chaahate hain?"

ek darabaaree kee vivashata se kam kuchh bhee is tarah ke upachaar ke bina krodh paida nahin kar sakata tha; lekin sar viliyam kee achchhee breeding ne use yah sab karava diya; aur yadyapi unhonne apanee jaanakaaree ke saty ke roop mein sakaaraatmak hone ke lie chhuttee kee bheekh maangee, unhonne sabase adhik shishtaachaar ke saath unakee saaree apoornata ko suna.

elijaabeth, use is tarah kee apriy sthiti se raahat dene ke lie us par avalambit mahasoos kar rahee thee, ab khud ko sherlot se isake baare mein poorv gyaan ka ullekh karake apane khaate kee pushti karane ke lie khud ko aage rakha; aur apanee maan aur bahanon ke vismayaadibodhan par rok lagaane ka prayaas kiya, sar viliyam ko badhaee dene ke lie, jisamen vah jen dvaara aasaanee se shaamil ho gaya tha, aur khushee par vibhinn prakaar kee tippanee karake, ummeed kee ja sakatee hai maich, mistar kolins ka utkrsht charitr aur landan se hansaphord kee suvidhaajanak dooree.

shreematee benet vaastav mein bahut jyaada jabardast theen, jab unhonne sar viliyam bane rahane ke lie ek badee baat kahee; lekin jitanee jaldee usane apanee bhaavanaon ko paaya, utanee tejee se vent nahin paaya. pahale sthaan par, usane poore maamale par avishvaas kiya; doosaree baat, use bahut yakeen tha ki mi. kolins ko andar le jaaya gaya tha; teesara, usane bharosa kiya ki ve kabhee bhee ek saath khush nahin honge; aur chautha, ki maich toot sakata hai. haalaanki, do nishkarshon ko spasht roop se poore se ghataaya gaya tha; ek, ki elijaabeth sabhee sharaaraton ka asalee kaaran thee; aur doosara, ki vah khud un sabhee dvaara barbarataapoorvak istemaal kiya gaya tha; aur in do binduon par vah mukhy roop se shesh din ke dauraan ghoomee. kuchh bhee saantvana nahin de sakata tha aur kuchh bhee use khush nahin kar sakata tha. — na hee us din ne apanee naaraajagee jataee. elijaabeth ko bina daante dekhe jaane se pahale ek saptaah beetane ke baad, ek maheene pahale vah sar viliyam ya ledee lukaas se bina baat kie rooth gaee, aur kaee maheene beet gae jab vah apanee betee ko maaph kar sakatee thee.

shree benet kee bhaavanaen is avasar par bahut adhik shaant theen, aur jaise unhonne anubhav kiya ki unhonne ek sabase sahamat hone ke lie uchchaarit kiya; isake lie usane use krtagy kiya, usane kaha ki shaarlot lukaas, jise vah sahaneey samajhadaar samajhane ke aadee tha, apanee patnee kee tarah moorkh aur apanee betee se adhik moorkh thee.

jen ne maich mein khud ko thoda hairaan kiya; lekin usane apanee khushee kee kaamana se kam apanee hairaanee se kaha; na hee elijaabeth ne use ise anuchit maanane ke lie raajee kiya. kittee aur lida mis lukaas se eershya karane se door the, kyonki shree kolins keval paadaree the; aur yah mairyton mein phailaane ke lie samaachaar ke ek tukade ke roop mein kisee any tareeke se unhen prabhaavit karata hai.

ledee lukaas, shreematee benet par punarvichaar karane mein saksham hone ke kaaran vijay ke prati asanvedanasheel nahin ho sakatee thee, jisase betee kee shaadee achchhee tarah se ho sake; aur usane saamaany taur par kahane ke bajaay longabarn ko kaha ki vah kitanee khush thee, haalaanki shreematee benet kee khattee-meethee baaten aur behooda tippanee khushiyon ko door bhagaane ke lie paryaapt theen.

elijaabeth aur chaarlot ke beech ek sanyam tha jisane unhen is vishay par paarasparik roop se maun rakha; aur elijaabeth ne yah mahasoos kiya ki koee bhee vaastavik vishvaas unake beech phir se nahin ho sakata. sherlot mein usakee niraasha ne usakee bahan ke sambandh mein vichaar ke saath usakee baaree bana dee, jisakee nishtha aur naajukata ke baare mein vah nishchit tha ki usakee raay ko kabhee nahin hilaaya ja sakata hai, aur jisakee khushee ke lie vah rojaana adhik chintit ho jaata hai, kyonki bingale ab ek saptaah chala gaya tha, aur kuchh bhee nahin usakee vaapasee ke baare mein suna tha.

jen ne kairolin ko apane patr ka praarambhik uttar bheja tha, aur jab tak vah phir se sunane kee ummeed nahin kar sakatee tab tak dinon kee ginatee kar rahee thee. shree kolins ka dhanyavaad patr mangalavaar ko aaya, unake pita ko sambodhit kiya, aur sabhee krtagyata ke saath likha, jo parivaar mein ek baarahamaasee ke nivaas ne sanket diya hoga. us sir par apanee antaraatma ka nirvahan karane ke baad, vah unhen soochit karane ke lie aage badhe, kaee utsaahapoorn abhivyaktiyon ke saath, apane aanandamay padosee, mis lukaas ka sneh praapt karane ke lie, aur phir samajhaaya ki yah keval unake samaaj ka aanand lene ke drshtikon se tha vah longabarn mein use phir se dekhane kee apanee tarah kee ichchha ke saath band hone ke lie taiyaar tha, jisake lie vah somavaar pakhavaade mein vaapas aane mein saksham hone kee ummeed karata tha; ledee kaithareen ke lie, unhonne kaha, isalie dil se apanee shaadee ko manjooree dee, ki vah ise jald se jald lene kee kaamana karatee hai, jis par vah bharosa karatee hai ki yah ek achook bahas hogee.
mis bingale ka patr aaya, aur sandeh ka ant hua. bahut pahale vaaky ne sardiyon ke lie sabhee ko landan mein basane ka aashvaasan diya, aur desh chhodane se pahale hartaphordashaayar mein apane doston ko apane sammaan ka bhugataan karane ka samay nahin hone par apane bhaee ke khed ke saath nishkarsh nikaala.

ummeed khatm ho gaee thee, pooree tarah se khatm; aur jab jen baakee patr mein bhaag le sakata tha, to use bahut kam mila, sivaay lekhak ke sneh ke, ki use koee dilaasa de sake. mis daarsee kee prashansa ne isake pramukh par kabja kar liya. usake kaee aakarshan phir se kam ho gae, aur kairolin ne apanee badhatee huee aatmeeyata ka khushee se daava kiya, aur ichchhaon ko poora karane kee bhavishyavaanee kee, jo usake poorv patr mein prakat kee gaee thee. usane apane bhaee ke mistar daarsee ke ghar mein kaidee hone kee khushee ke saath yah bhee likha, aur nae pharneechar ke sambandh mein baad ke kuchh yojanaon ka ullekh kiya.

"haan, mis elijaabeth, aapako charch mein aane vaale ravivaar ko ledee kaithareen de borg ko dekhane ka sammaan hoga, aur mujhe yah kahane kee zaroorat nahin hai ki aap usake saath khush honge. vah sabhee milanasaar aur krpaalu hain, aur mujhe sandeh hai ki aap nahin karenge." seva samaapt hone par usake notis ke kuchh hisse se sammaanit kiya jae. mujhe yah kahane mein koee sankoch nahin hai ki vah aapako aur meree bahan maariya ko har aamantran mein shaamil karegee, jisake saath vah aapake yahaan rahane ke dauraan hamaara sammaan karatee hai. mere priy chaarlat ke prati usaka vyavahaar.




is nimantran ke parinaam mein shree kolins kee vijay poorn thee. apane hairaan aagantukon kee bhavyata ko pradarshit karane kee shakti, aur unhen apane aur apanee patnee ke prati usakee nishtha ko dekhane dene kee shakti, vaastav mein vahee tha jisakee unhonne kaamana kee thee; aur yah karane ka ek mauka itanee jaldee diya jaana chaahie, ledee kaithareen kee krpaaluta ka aisa udaaharan tha kyonki vah nahin jaanata tha ki paryaapt prashansa kaise kee jae.

jab ve kapade pahan rahe the, to ve apane alag-alag daravaajon se do-teen baar aae, jaldee se jaldee jaane kee salaah dene ke lie, kyonki ledee kaithareen ko unake khaane ke intajaar mein rakhane par bahut aapatti thee. - unake laadaship ke aise durjey khaate, aur usake jeene ka tareeka kaaphee bhayabheet maariya lukaas, jo kampanee ke lie bahut kam istemaal kiya gaya tha, aur vah roses mein apane parichay ke lie bahut aashanka ke saath dekhatee thee, jaisa ki usake pita ne sent jems mein apanee prastuti ke lie kiya tha.
