jab ve hol mein kadam badhaate hain, to maariya ka alaarm har pal badh raha tha, aur yahaan tak ​​ki sar viliyam bhee pooree tarah se shaant nahin dikhe. - elijaabeth ka saahas use viphal nahin hua. usane ledee kaithareen ke baare mein kuchh nahin suna tha jo use kisee bhee asaadhaaran pratibha ya chamatkaaree gun se bhayaanak bolatee thee, aur keval paise aur raink kee udaaseenata thee, usane socha ki vah bina kisee chhedachhaad ke gavaah ban sakatee hai.

pravesh hol se, jinamen se shree kolins ne ek shaanadaar hava, theek anupaat aur samaapt gahane ke saath ishaara kiya, unhonne ek virodhee kaksh ke maadhyam se naukaron ka peechha kiya, us kamare mein jahaan ledee kaithareen, unakee betee aur shreematee jeskinasan the. baithana. — usakee laadalee, badee hee krpaaluta se, unhen praapt karane ke lie uthee; aur jaisa ki shreematee kolins ne apane pati ke saath milakar tay kiya tha ki parichay ka kaaryaalay unaka hona chaahie, yah uchit tareeke se kiya gaya tha, bina kisee maaphee aur dhanyavaad ke jo unhonne aavashyak socha hoga.

sent jems ke hone ke baavajood, sar viliyam pooree tarah se jaag gaya tha, usake chaaron or kee bhavyata se, ki usake paas itana saahas tha ki vah bahut kam dhanush bana sake, aur ek shabd kahe bina apanee seet le sake; aur usakee betee, lagabhag apanee indriyon se darakar, apanee kursee ke kinaare par baith gaee, na jaane kis raaste se dekhane ke lie. elijaabeth ne khud ko is drshy ke kaaphee samaan paaya, aur teen mahilaon ko unake sammukh aane se pahale dekh sakatee theen. - ledee kaithareen ek lambee, badee mahila theen, jo drdhata se chihnit visheshataon ke saath theen, jo ek baar sundar ho sakatee theen. usakee hava sulag nahin rahee thee, na hee use praapt karane ka usaka tareeka tha, jaise ki usake aagantukon ko apane avar raink ko bhoolane ke lie. use chuppee dvaara durjey nahin diya gaya tha; lekin usane jo kuchh bhee kaha, use aadhikaarik svar mein bola gaya, jaisa ki usake aatm-mahatv ko chihnit karata hai, aur shree vikam ko turant elijaabeth ke dimaag mein laaya; aur din ke avalokan se, vah ledee kaithareen ko vaisa hee maanatee thee jaisa usane pratinidhitv kiya tha.

jab, maan kee jaanch karane ke baad, jinake pratigyaan aur nirvaasan mein unhen jald hee mistar daarsee kee kuchh samaanata dikhee, to unhonne betee kee or aankh maaree, vah maariya ke vismay mein, lagabhag itanee patalee aur itanee chhotee ho sakatee thee. mahilaon ke beech na to koee phigar tha aur na hee chehara, koee samaanata thee.

sar viliyam ne hansaphord mein keval ek saptaah ka manchan kiya; lekin unakee yah yaatra kaaphee lambee thee ki unhen apanee betee ke sabase adhik aaraam se rahane ke lie raajee kiya jae, aur unake paas aise pati aur padosee hone ke naate jaise aksar nahin milate the. jab sar viliyam unake saath the, mistar kolins ne unhen apane gig mein draiving karane ke lie apane desh ko samarpit kiya, aur unhen desh ke lie prerit kiya; lekin jab vah chala gaya, to poora parivaar apane saamaany kaamon par laut aaya, aur elijaabeth ko yah pata lagaane ke lie aabhaaree tha ki unhonne apane chachere bhaee ko parivartan se adhik nahin dekha, naashte aur raat ke khaane ke beech ke pramukh ke lie ab usake dvaara paarit kiya gaya tha bageeche mein kaam karate hain, ya padhane aur likhane mein, aur apane svayan ke pustak kaksh mein khidakee se baahar dekhate hain, jo sadak ke saamane tha. jis kamare mein mahila baithee thee vah peechhe kee or tha. elijaabeth ne pahale socha tha ki chaarlot ko aam upayog ke lie daining-paarlar pasand nahin karana chaahie; yah ek behatar aakaar ka kamara tha, aur isamen ek aanandadaayak pahaloo tha; lekin jald hee usane dekha ki usakee sahelee ke paas usake lie ek utkrsht kaaran tha, shree kolins ke lie nissandeh apane apaartament mein bahut kam tha, kya ve ek samaan roop se jeevant the; aur usane vyavastha ke lie shaarlet ko shrey diya.

draing-room se ve len mein kuchh bhee alag nahin kar sakate the, aur shree kolins ko is baat ke lie aabhaar vyakt kiya gaya tha ki gaadiyaan kya saath jaatee hain, aur kitanee baar vishesh roop se mis dee borg ne apane phetan mein kaam kiya, jise vah kabhee bhee unhen soochit karane ke lie nahin aatee theen. haalaanki, yah lagabhag har din hua. vah anajaane mein paarsonej par nahin rukee, aur shaarlet ke saath kuchh minaton kee baatacheet huee, lekin baahar nikalane ke lie shaayad hee kabhee us par kaaboo paaya gaya.

bahut kam din aise gujare jisamen mistar kolins rojee-rotee ke lie nahin chalate the, aur na hee aise kaee jinamen unakee patnee ne isee tarah jaana jarooree nahin samajha; aur jab tak elijaabeth ko yaad aaya ki parivaar ke any logon ko nipataaya ja sakata hai, vah itane ghanton ke balidaan ko nahin samajh sakatee thee. ab aur tab, unhen usakee laadaship ke ek kol se sammaanit kiya gaya tha, aur in yaatraon ke dauraan kamare mein gujarane vaale unake avalokan se kuchh bhee nahin bacha. usane unake kaamon kee jaanch kee, unake kaam ko dekha, aur unhen ise alag tareeke se karane kee salaah dee; pharneechar kee vyavastha mein dosh paaya, ya laaparavaahee mein grhinee ka pata lagaaya; aur agar vah kisee bhee jalapaan ko sveekaar karatee hai, to aisa lagata hai ki keval yah pata lagaane ke lie ki usake parivaar ke lie shreematee kolins ke maans ke jod bahut bade the.

elijaabeth ne jald hee maana ki yadyapi yah mahaan mahila kauntee ke lie shaanti ke aayog mein nahin thee, vah apanee khud kee pallee mein sabase sakriy majistret thee, jo ki mistar kolins dvaara kee gaee sabase chhotee chintaon ka tha; aur jab bhee kisee bhee kuteer ke logon ko jhagadaaloo, asantusht ya bahut gareeb hone ke lie nipataaya gaya, to unhonne apanee matabhedon ko nipataane, apanee shikaayaton ko shaant karane, aur unhen sadbhaav aur bahut kuchh karane ke lie gaanv mein aage badhaaya.

rojings mein bhojan ka manoranjan saptaah mein do baar doharaaya jaata tha; aur, sar viliyam ke khone kee anumati, aur shaam ko keval ek kaard tebal tha, is tarah ke har manoranjan mein pahale ka pratipaksh tha. unakee any vyastataen kuchh kam theen; saamaany roop se pados ke rahane kee shailee ke roop mein, kolins kee pahunch se pare tha. haalaanki yah elijaabeth ke lie koee buraee nahin thee, aur poore samay usane apana samay aaraam se bitaaya; sherlot ke saath aadhe ghante kee sukhad baatacheet huee, aur mausam saal ke samay ke lie itana theek tha, ki use aksar daravaaje se baahar bahut aanand milata tha. usaka pasandeeda chalana, aur jahaan vah aksar jaatee thee, jabaki any ledee kaithareen ko bula rahe the, khule grov ke saath tha, jisane paark ke us kinaare ko ukasaaya tha, jahaan ek achchha aashray tha, jo kisee ko bhee nahin lagata tha, lekin khud ko aur kahaan use ledee kaithareen kee jigyaasa kee pahunch se pare mahasoos hua.

is shaant tareeke se, usakee yaatra ka pahala pakhavaada jald hee gujar gaya. eestar kareeb aa raha tha, aur jis saptaah yah pahale hua tha, vah rojings mein parivaar ke lie ek atirikt laane ke lie tha, jo ki itane chhote se chakr mein mahatvapoorn hona chaahie. elijaabeth ne apane aagaman ke turant baad suna tha, ki shree daarsee se kuchh haphton ke dauraan ummeed kee ja rahee thee, aur haalaanki unake kaee parichit nahin the, jinhen vah pasand nahin karatee theen, unaka aana unakee tulana mein dekhane ke lie ek tulanaatmak roop se nae ko prastut karega rojings paartiyaan, aur vah yah dekhane mein chakit ho sakatee hai ki mis chingalee kee dijain us par kitanee niraashaajanak thee, jo usake chachere bhaee ke vyavahaar se, jisake lie vah ledee kaithareen dvaara spasht roop se kismat mein thee; jisane sabase badee santushti ke saath aane kee baat kee, usane sabase adhik prashansa ke sandarbh mein baat kee, aur yah jaanakar lagabhag krodhit ho gaya ki vah pahale se hee mis lukaas aur svayan dvaara aksar dekha gaya tha.

unaka aagaman jald hee paarsonej mein hua, kyonki mistar kolins pooree subah paidal chal rahe the, jisamen hansphord len mein khulane vaale loj ko dekhane ke lie jald se jald aashvaasan diya gaya tha; aur apana dhanush banaane ke baad gaadee paark mein badal gaee, badee hoshiyaaree ke saath ghar laut aaya. agalee subah unhonne apanee ijjat chukaane ke lie rojings kee taraph rukh kiya


karnal phitjaviliyam ke shishtaachaar kee prashansa mein bahut prashansa kee gaee thee, aur mahilaon ne mahasoos kiya ki unhen rojings mein apanee vyastata ke aanand ke lie kaaphee jodana chaahie. kuchh din the, haalaanki, isase pahale ki ve kisee bhee nimantran ko praapt karate, jabaki ghar mein aagantuk the, ve aavashyak nahin ho sakate the; aur yah sajjanon ke aagaman ke lagabhag ek saptaah baad eestar-din tak nahin tha, ki unhen is tarah ke dhyaan se sammaanit kiya gaya tha, aur phir unhen shaam ko charch chhodane ke lie kaha gaya tha. pichhale haphte tak unhonne ledee kaithareen ya unakee betee donon mein se bahut kam dekhee theen. karnal phitzaviliyam ne samay ke dauraan ek baar se adhik baar phon kiya tha, lekin mistar daarsee ko unhonne keval charch mein dekha tha.

nimantran ko nishchit roop se sveekaar kar liya gaya, aur ek uchit samay par ve ledee kaithareen ke draing-room mein paartee mein shaamil ho gae. unakee viraasat ne unhen sabhy roop se praapt kiya, lekin yah spasht tha ki unakee kampanee kisee bhee tarah se itanee sveekaary nahin thee jab vah kisee aur ko nahin pa sakatee thee; aur vaastav mein, vah apane bhateejon dvaara lagabhag talleen thee, unase bol rahee thee, vishesh roop se daarsee ke lie, kamare ke kisee bhee any vyakti kee tulana mein bahut adhik.

karnal phitzaviliyam unhen dekhakar vaastav mein prasann the; rojings mein kisee bhee cheej ka unake lie ek raahat kee baat thee; aur shreematee kolins ke sundar mitr ne apane phains ko bahut adhik aakarshit kiya. usane ab khud ko usake paas baitha diya, aur kent aur hartaphordashaayar ke baare mein itanee baat kee, yaatra aur ghar par rahane kee, naee pustakon aur sangeet kee, ki elijaabeth ne pahale kabhee us kamare mein itana achchha manoranjan nahin kiya tha; aur unhonne itanee aatma aur pravaah ke saath baatacheet kee, jaisa ki ledee kaithareen ka dhyaan aakarshit karane ke lie, saath hee saath mistar daarsee ne bhee kiya tha. unakee aankhen jald hee baar-baar jigyaasa kee drshti se unakee or ghoom rahee theen; aur kuchh der ke baad usake ahasaas ko saajha karane ke lie, use khulakar sveekaar kiya gaya, kyonki usane baahar bulaane ke lie haath nahin uthaaya,

"aap kya kah rahe hain, phitzaviliyam? yah aap kisase baat kar rahe hain? mis benet kya kah rahe hain? mujhe sunane do ki yah kya hai."

"ham sangeet ke baare mein baat kar rahe hain, maidam," unhonne kaha, jab koee javaab se bachane mein saksham nahin hai.

"sangeet ka! phir praarthana karen jor se bolen. yah sabhee vishayon mein meree khushee kee baat hai. yadi aap sangeet kee baat kar rahe hain to mere paas baatacheet mein mera hissa hona chaahie. inglaind mein kuchh hee log hain, mujhe lagata hai, jinhen sangeet ka adhik aanand milata hai apane aap se, ya ek behatar praakrtik svaad. yadi mainne kabhee seekha tha, to mujhe ek mahaan praveen hona chaahie tha. aur isalie ainee, agar usake svaasthy ne use aavedan karane kee anumati dee thee. mujhe vishvaas hai ki usane khushee se pradarshan kiya hoga. jorjiyaee kaise karata hai. par jao, daarsee?

shree daarsee ne apanee bahan kee praveenata kee prashansa ke saath pyaar se baat kee.

ledee kaithareen ne kaha, "main usaka itana achchha hisaab sunakar bahut khush hoon." "aur praarthana use mujhase kahatee hai, ki vah utkrshtata kee ummeed nahin kar sakatee hai, agar vah ek mahaan vyavahaar nahin karatee hai."

"main aapako vishvaas dilaata hoon, maidam," usane javaab diya, "use aisee salaah kee aavashyakata nahin hai. vah lagaataar abhyaas karatee hai."

"itana behatar. yah bahut adhik nahin kiya ja sakata hai; aur jab main agalee baar use likhoonga, to main use kisee bhee khaate mein ise upekshit nahin karane ka aarop lagaoonga. main aksar yuva mahilaon ko bataata hoon, ki sangeet mein koee utkrshtata haasil nahin kee jaanee hai, bina nirantar abhyaas. mainne kaee baar mis benet ko bataaya hai, ki vah vaastav mein kabhee bhee achchha nahin khelegee, jab tak ki vah adhik abhyaas nahin karatee hai, aur haalaanki shreematee kolins ke paas koee saadhan nahin hai, vah bahut svaagat karatee hai, jaisa ki mainne aksar use bataaya hai, rojings mein aane ke lie. din, aur shreematee jenakinsan ke kamare mein piyaano-forest par khelate hain. vah kisee ke raaste mein nahin hogee, aap jaanate hain, ghar ke us hisse mein. "

mistar daarsee apanee chaachee kee beemaar breeding ko dekhakar thoda sharama gaya aur usane koee javaab nahin diya.

jab kophee khatm ho gaee, to karnal phitjaviliyam ne elijaabeth ko use khelane ka vaada karane kee yaad dilaee; aur vah seedhe yantr par baith gaee. usane usake paas ek kursee kheenchee. ledee kaithareen ne aadha gaana suna, aur phir pahale kee tarah, apane doosare bhateeje se baat kee; baad mein jab tak vah usase door nahin chala gaya, aur piyaano-forst kee or apane saamaany vichaar-vimarsh ke saath chal raha tha, tab tak usane khud ko tainaat kiya taaki nishpaksh kalaakaar kee ginatee ke baare mein pooree jaanakaaree praapt kar sake. elijaabeth ne dekha ki vah kya kar rahee hai, aur pahale suvidhaajanak thaharaav par, ek kattar muskaan ke saath usakee or mudee, aur kaha,

"aap mujhe sunane ke lie is saaree sthiti mein aakar, shree daarsee, mujhe daraane ka matalab hai? lekin main chintit nahin hooonga, haalaanki aapakee bahan itanee achchhee tarah se khelatee hai. mere baare mein ek jid hai jo kabhee bhee bhayabheet nahin ho sakatee hai. doosaron kee ichchha. mera saahas hamesha mujhe daraane-dhamakaane kee har koshish ke saath uthata hai. ”

"main yah nahin kahoonga ki aap galat hain," unhonne javaab diya, "kyonki aap vaastav mein mujh par vishvaas nahin kar sakate the ki main aapako kisee bhee dijain ka manoranjan karane ke lie, aur mujhe aapake parichit ka aanand lambe samay se pata hai, ki aapako bahut aanand milata hai kabhee-kabhee un vichaaron ko sveekaar karana jo vaastav mein aapake apane nahin hain. ”

elijaabeth khud kee is tasveer par dil se hansee, aur karnal phitjaviliyam se kaha, "aapaka chachera bhaee aapako meree bahut achchhee dhaarana dega, aur aapako mere dvaara kahe gae ek shabd par vishvaas na karane ke lie sikhaata hai. main ek vyakti ke saath milane mein vishesh roop se ashubh hoon. mere asalee charitr ko ujaagar karane mein saksham,elijaabeth agalee subah khud se baithee thee, aur jen ko likh rahee thee, jabaki shreematee kolins aur maariya gaanv mein vyaapaar par gaee theen, jab vah daravaaje par ek angoothee se ghabaraee huee thee, ek aagantuk ka sanket. jaisa ki usane koee gaadee nahin sunee thee, usane socha ki yah ledee kaithareen hone kee sambhaavana nahin hai, aur us aashanka ke tahat apane aadhe-adhoore patr ko door kar rahee thee ki vah sabhee apoorn prashnon se bach sake, jab daravaaja khula, aur use bahut aashchary hua, mi. , daarsee, aur mistar daarsee, keval kamare mein pravesh kiya.

vah use akela paakar bahut hairaan tha, aur usane apanee ghusapaith ke lie maaphee maangee, yah bataakar ki usane sabhee mahilaon ko samajh liya tha.

isake baad ve baith gae, aur jab rozings ke baad unakee poochhataachh huee, to kul milaavat mein doobane ka khatara tha. isalie, kuchh sochana, aur is udhedabun mein ki jab usane use hartaphordashaayar mein aakhiree baar dekha tha, aur yah jaanane ke lie utsuk mahasoos kar raha tha ki vah jaldabaajee mein vida hone ke vishay mein kya kahega, to usane dekha.

"kitanee achaanak aap sabhee ne pichhale navambar mein mistar daarsee ke saath nedarapheeld ka chayan kiya! yah shree bingale ke lie itanee jaldee aap sabhee ko dekhane ke baad sabase jyaada aashcharyachakit karane vaala raha hoga; kyonki agar main sahee yaad karata hoon, to vah ek din pahale gae the. vah aur unakee bahanen achchhee theen, mujhe ummeed hai, jab aap landan chhod denge. ”

"pooree tarah se - main aapako dhanyavaad deta hoon."

usane paaya ki use koee aur javaab nahin milana tha - aur, ek chhote se viraam ke baad,

"mujhe lagata hai ki main samajh gaya hoon ki mistar bingale ko phir se needaralaind lautane ka kabhee vichaar nahin hai?"

"mainne use aisa kahate hue kabhee nahin suna hai; lekin yah sambhav hai ki vah bhavishy mein apana bahut kam samay vahaan bitae. usake kaee dost hain, aur vah jeevan ke aise samay mein hai jab dost aur sagaee lagaataar badh rahee hai."

"agar vah needaralainds mein rahane ka matalab hai, lekin pados ke lie behatar hoga ki vah pooree tarah se jagah chhod de, to shaayad ham vahaan ek base hue parivaar ko pa saken. lekin shaayad mistar bingale ne ghar nahin liya. apane svayan ke lie pados kee suvidha ke lie, aur hamen use usee siddhaant par rakhane ya chhodane kee apeksha karanee chaahie. "

"mujhe aashcharyachakit nahin hona chaahie," daarsee ne kaha, "agar vah ise chhod dena tha, jaise hee koee bhee yogy khareed prastaav."

elijaabeth ne koee javaab nahin diya. vah apane dost se adhik samay tak baat karane se daratee thee; aur, kahane ke lie aur kuchh nahin tha, ab usake lie ek vishay khojane kee pareshaanee ko chhodane ke lie nirdhaarit kiya gaya tha.

vah sanket le gaya, aur jald hee shuroo hua, "yah ek bahut hee aaraamadaayak ghar lagata hai. ledee kaithareen, mera maanana ​​hai ki jab shree kolins pahalee baar hansaford ke paas aae the, to isake lie bahut achchha kiya tha."

"mujhe vishvaas hai ki usane kiya tha - aur mujhe yakeen hai ki vah apanee krtagyata ko adhik aabhaaree vastu par nahin de sakatee thee."

"shree kolins apanee patnee kee pasand mein bahut bhaagyashaalee prateet hote hain."

"haan, vaastav mein; unake dost bahut kam samajhadaar mahilaon mein se ek ke saath milane par khushee mana sakate hain, jinhonne use sveekaar kar liya hota, ya yadi unake paas hai to use khush kar diya hota hai. mere dost kee ek utkrsht samajh hai- haalaanki main nishchit nahin hoon. main use shree kolins se shaadee karane ke lie sabase buddhimaanee ke roop mein maanata hoon jo usane kabhee kiya tha. vah pooree tarah se khush lag rahee hai, haalaanki, aur vivekapoorn roshanee mein, yah nishchit roop se usake lie bahut achchha maich hai. "

"use apane hee parivaar aur doston se itanee aasaanee se door hone ke lie use bahut sahamat hona chaahie."

"ek aasaan dooree aap ise kahate hain? yah lagabhag pachaas meel hai."

"aur achchhee sadak kee pachaas meel kee dooree kya hai? aadhe din kee yaatra se thoda adhik. haan, main ise bahut aasaan dooree kahata hoon."

"mujhe kabhee bhee maich ke phaayadon mein se ek ke roop mein dooree par vichaar nahin karana chaahie," elijaabeth roya. "mujhe kabhee nahin kahana chaahie ki shreematee kolins ko unake parivaar ke paas basaaya gaya tha."

"yah hartaphordashaayar ke lie aapake svayan ke lagaav ka pramaan hai. longaboran ke bahut pados se pare koee bhee cheej, mujhe lagata hai, bahut door dikhaee degee."

jaisa ki unhonne kaha ki ek prakaar kee muskaan thee, jise elijaabeth ne samajh liya tha; vah use jen aur nedarapheeld ke baare mein sochata hua hona chaahie, aur usane javaab dete hue sharama kar kaha,

"mere kahane ka matalab yah nahin hai ki ek mahila ko usake parivaar ke paas bhee nahin basaaya ja sakata hai. door aur paas ka rishtedaar hona chaahie, aur kaee alag-alag paristhitiyon par nirbhar hona chaahie. jahaan yaatra ke mahatvaheen hone ka bhaagy banaana hai, dooree nahin ban jaatee hai. buraee. lekin yahaan aisa nahin hai. mistar aur misej kolins ke paas ek aaraamadaayak aay hai, lekin aisa nahin hai, jo lagaataar yaatra kee anumati dega- aur main raajee hoon ki mera dost khud ko apane parivaar ke paas aadhe se kam mein nahin bulaega. vartamaan dooree. "

mistar daarsee ne apanee kursee ko usakee or thoda kheencha, aur kaha, "aapake paas is tarah ke bahut majaboot sthaaneey lagaav ka adhikaar nahin ho sakata hai. aap hamesha longaborn mein nahin ho sakate."

elijaabeth hairaan dikheen. sajjan ne kuchh parivartan mahasoos kiya; unhonne apanee kursee vaapas le lee, mej se ek akhabaar liya, aur, us par nazar rakhate hue, kaha, thandee aavaaz mein,

"kya aap kent se khush hain?"

desh ke vishay par ek chhotee baatacheet, donon taraph shaant aur sankshipt - aur jald hee shaarlot aur usakee bahan ke pravesh dvaara samaapt ho gaee, bas apane chalane se vaapas aa gaee.



ek se adhik baar elijaabeth ne paark ke bheetar apane rembal mein, apratyaashit roop se mistar daarsee se mulaakaat kee. — use laga ki badamaashon kee saaree shithilata usako milanee chaahie, jahaan use aur koee nahin laaya gaya tha; aur phir se hone se rokane ke lie, pahalee baar mein use soochit karane ka dhyaan rakha, ki yah usaka pasandeeda adda tha. — yah doosaree baar kaise ho sakata hai isalie bahut hee ajeeb tha! - aisa usane kiya, aur ek tihaee ne bhee kiya. yah vilakshan beemaar prakrti ya ek svaichchhik tapasya kee tarah lag raha tha, in avasaron ke lie yah keval kuchh aupachaarik poochhataachh aur ek ajeeb thaharaav nahin tha aur phir door, lekin usane vaastav mein vaapas mudakar usake saath chalana jarooree samajha. usane kabhee koee badee baat nahin kahee, na hee usane khud ko baat karane ya jyaada sunane kee pareshaanee dee; lekin isane unhen apane teesare renakantre ke dauraan maara ki vah kuchh ajeeb tarah ke asambaddh prashn poochh raha tha - hansaphord mein hone ke apane aanand ke baare mein, ekaant kee sair ke baare mein usaka pyaar, aur mistar aur misej kolins kee khushee ke baare mein usakee raay; aur vah rojings ke baare mein aur ghar ko pooree tarah se nahin samajhane ke kaaran, vah yah ummeed karane lagee thee ki jab bhee vah kent mein aaegee to vah bhee vaheen rahegee. usake shabdon se lag raha tha ki yah usaka arth hai. kya vah apane vichaaron mein karnal phitjaviliyam ho sakata hai? vah maanatee thee, agar usaka koee matalab hai, to use us timaahee mein jo kuchh bhee ho sakata hai, usaka matalab hona chaahie. isane use thoda vyathit kar diya, aur vah paarasonej ke saamane ke taal mein khud ko get par paakar kaaphee khush thee.

vah ek din lagee huee thee, jab vah jen ke antim patr ka pun: upayog kar rahee thee, aur kuchh maargon par nivaas kar rahee thee, jisane yah saabit kar diya ki jen ne aatmaon mein nahin likha hai, jab, shree daarsee dvaara phir se aashcharyachakit hone ke bajaay, usane dekha ki vah dekh raha hai karnal phitjaviliyam unase mil rahe the. patr ko turant hata diya aur ek muskaan ke lie majaboor kiya, usane kaha,

"mujhe isase pahale nahin pata tha ki tum is tarah se chale."

"main paark ka daura kar raha hoon," unhonne javaab diya, "jaisa ki main aam taur par har saal karata hoon, aur paarsanoj mein ek kol ke saath ise band karane ka iraada rakhata hoon. kya aap bahut aage ja rahe hain?"

"nahin, mujhe ek pal mein badal jaana chaahie tha."

aur usake anusaar usane baaree kee, aur ve ek saath paarsonej kee or chale.

"kya aap nishchit roop se shanivaar ko kent chhod dete hain?" usane kaha.

"haan-agar daarsee ise phir se band nahin karata hai. lekin main apane nipataan mein hoon. vah vyaapaar kee vyavastha vaise hee karata hai jaise vah chaahe."

"aur agar vyavastha mein khud ko khush karane mein saksham nahin hai, to use pasand kee shakti mein kam se kam bahut khushee hai. main kisee bhee shareer ko nahin jaanata, jo shree daarsee kee tulana mein use pasand karane kee shakti ka aanand lene ke lie adhik lagata hai."

karnal phitjaviliyam ne kaha, "vah apane tareeke se bahut achchha lagata hai." "lekin isalie ham sabhee karate hain. yah keval yah hai ki usake paas kaee any logon kee tulana mein behatar saadhan hain, kyonki vah ameer hai, aur any log gareeb hain. main bahut soch-samajhakar bolata hoon. ek chhota beta, jise aap jaanate hain, use svayan ke prati jaagarook hona chaahie." inakaar aur nirbharata. ”

"meree raay mein, arl ka chhota beta ya to bahut kam jaan sakata hai. ab, gambheerata se, aap kabhee bhee aatm-vanchana aur nirbharata ke baare mein kya jaanate hain? jab bhee aap ko chuna gaya hai, to aapako paise kee ichchha se roka gaya hai ya? aap ke lie ek phainsee tha kisee bhee cheej kee khareed? "

"ye ghar ke savaal hain - aur shaayad main yah nahin kah sakata ki mainne us prakrti ke kaee kashton ka anubhav kiya hai. lekin adhik vajan ke maamalon mein, main paise kee ichchha se peedit ho sakata hoon. chhote bete shaadee nahin kar sakate jahaan ve pasand karate hain."

"jab tak ve bhaagy kee mahilaon ko pasand nahin karate hain, jo mujhe lagata hai ki ve bahut baar karate hain."

"samay seema samaapt hone kee hamaaree aadaten hamen bahut adhik nirbhar karatee hain, aur mere jeevan ke bahut se aise log nahin hain jo paise kee or dhyaan die bina shaadee karane ka jokhim utha sakate hain."

"kya yah hai," elijaabeth socha, "mere lie kya matalab hai?" aur vah is vichaar par rang gaee; lekin, khud ko theek karate hue, ek jeevant lahaje mein kaha, "aur praarthana karo, arl ke chhote bete kee saamaany keemat kya hai? jab tak ki bada bhaee bahut beemaar nahin hai, mujhe lagata hai ki aap pachaas hajaar paund se oopar nahin poochhenge."

usane use usee shailee mein uttar diya, aur vishay gira. ek maun ko baadhit karane ke lie jo use phainsee bana sakata hai, jo beet chuka tha, usase prabhaavit hokar usane jald hee kaha,

"mujhe lagata hai ki aapake chachere bhaee ne apane nipataan mein kisee ke hone ke lie aapako mukhy roop se apane saath laaya tha. mujhe aashchary hai ki vah shaadee nahin karata hai, us tarah kee sthaayee suvidha ko surakshit karane ke lie. lekin, shaayad usakee bahan vartamaan ke lie bhee karatee hai, aur , kyonki vah apanee ekamaatr dekhabhaal ke adheen hai, vah vah kar sakatee hai jo use usake saath pasand hai. man kee is vikrt sthiti mein, vichaaron ke saath jo kuchh bhee nahin kar sakata tha, vah chala gaya; lekin yah nahin hoga; aadhe minat mein patr phir se saamane aaya, aur khud ko ikattha karane ke saath-saath, vah phir se vikeem se sambandhit sabhee ko darakinaar karana shuroo kar diya, aur har vaaky ke arth kee jaanch karane ke lie khud ko ab tak aagya dee. pembale parivaar ke saath usake sambandh ka lekha, vahee tha jo usane khud se sambandhit tha; aur svargeey mistar daarsee kee daya, haalaanki vah apanee had se pahale nahin jaanata tha, apane shabdon ke saath samaan roop se sahamat tha. ab tak pratyek punaraavrtti ne doosare kee pushti kee: lekin jab vah vaseeyat mein aaya, to antar bahut achchha tha. vikkeem ne kaha ki jeevit vyakti usakee yaad mein taaza tha, aur jaisa ki usane apane bahut hee achchhe shabdon ko yaad kiya, yah mahasoos karana asambhav nahin tha ki ek taraph ya doosaree taraph sakal doharaav tha; aur, kuchh palon ke lie, usane apanee chaapaloosee kee ki usakee ichchhaen pooree nahin hueen. lekin jab vah padhatee hai, aur nikatatam dhyaan se phir se padhatee hai, to vishesh roop se vikam ke rahane ke turant baad jeevika ke lie sabhee dikhaava karate hain, isake badale mein use teen hajaar paund ke roop mein kaaphee raashi milatee hai, phir se vah sankoch karane ke lie majaboor thee. usane patr ko neeche rakh diya, har paristhiti ko tauba kar liya jisaka arth tha ki vah nishpakshata ka tha — pratyek kathan kee sambhaavana par vichaar-vimarsh kiya gaya tha - lekin thodee saphalata ke saath. donon taraph yah keval jor tha. phir se vah padhatee hai. lekin har pankti adhik spasht roop se saabit huee ki vah maamala, jise vah asambhav maanatee thee ki koee bhee antarvirodh itana pratinidhitv kar sakata hai, jaise ki mistar daarsee ke aacharan ko badanaam karane se kam mein prastut karana, ek aise mod ke lie saksham tha, jo use pooree tarah se pooree tarah se nirdosh bana de. .

apavyay aur saamaany apavitrata jo unhonne shree vikam ke aarop mein nahin padane ke lie ukasaaya, use bahut dhakka laga; jitana adhik ho sakata hai, kyonki vah apane anyaay ka koee saboot nahin la sakatee hai. —shir milishiya mein pravesh karane se pahale usane kabhee usake baare mein nahin suna tha, jisamen usane us yuvak ke anunay-vinay par sagaee kar lee thee, jo usase galatee se shahar mein milane par, vahaan ek maamoolee parichit vyakti ka naveeneekaran kiya tha. apane poorv jeevan ke tareeke se, hartaphordashaayar mein kuchh bhee gyaat nahin tha lekin unhonne khud ko kya bataaya. apane asalee charitr ke roop mein, usakee shakti mein jaanakaaree thee, usane poochhataachh kee ichchha kabhee nahin mahasoos kee thee. unakee shaaleenata, aavaaj aur dhang ne unhen har gun ke aadhipaty mein sthaapit kar diya tha. usane bhalaee ke kuchh udaaharan, akhandata ya paropakaar ke kuchh vishisht lakshanon ko yaad karane kee koshish kee, jo use shree daarsee ke hamalon se bacha sakata hai; ledee kaithareen ne raat ke khaane ke baad dekha ki mis benet aatmaon se baahar hai, aur turant isake lie khud ko jimmedaar thaharaate hue, yah maanakar ki use itanee jaldee ghar vaapas jaana pasand nahin hai, usane kaha.

elijaabeth ne uttar diya, "main aapakee tarah ke nimantran ke lie aapakee deevaanagee ke lie bahut adhik baadhy hoon," lekin yah sveekaar karana meree shakti mein nahin hai. - mujhe agale shanivaar shahar mein rahana hoga.

"kyon, us dar par, aap keval chhah saptaah ke lie yahaan aae honge. mujhe ummeed thee ki aap do maheene rukenge. mainne aane se pahale shreematee kolins se kaha tha. aapake itanee jaldee jaane ka koee avasar nahin ho sakata hai. shreematee benet nishchit roop se ja sakatee hain. aapako ek aur pakhavaade ke lie chhuttee. "

"lekin mere pita nahin kar sakate. — unhonne meree vaapasee kee jaldee karane ke lie pichhale haphte likha tha."

"oh! aapake pita shaayad aapako bakhsh sakate hain, agar aapakee maan kar sakatee hai. - betiyaan ek pita ke lie kabhee bhee bahut jyaada parinaamee nahin hotee hain. aur agar aap ek aur maheena poora karenge, to yah meree shakti hogee ki main aap mein se ek ko le jaoon. landan ke roop mein, main joon ke shuroo mein ek saptaah ke lie vahaan ja raha hoon, aur jaisa ki dosan ne barauch boks par aapatti nahin jataee hai, aap mein se kisee ek ke lie bahut achchha kamara hoga- aur vaastav mein, agar mausam thanda hona chaahie, mujhe aap donon ko lene mein koee aapatti nahin honee chaahie, kyonki aap donon bade nahin hain. ”

"aap sabhee dayaalu hain, maidam; lekin mera maanana ​​hai ki hamen apanee mool yojana ka paalan karana chaahie."

ledee kaithareen ne isteepha diya.

"shreematee kolins, aapako unake saath ek naukar bhejana hoga. aap jaanate hain ki main hamesha apane man kee baat kahatee hoon, aur main do yuva mahilaon ko khud se yaatra karane ka vichaar sahan nahin kar sakatee. yah bahut anuchit hai. aapako kisee ko bhejane ke lie virodh karana chaahie. main duniya mein us tarah kee sabase badee naapasand. — yuva mahilaon ko jeevan mein unakee sthiti ke anusaar hamesha sahee dhang se pahara dena chaahie aur bhaag lena chaahie. jab ​​meree bhateejee jorjiya pichhalee garmiyon mein raamasaget gaee thee, to mainne usase do purushon ke hone ka ek bindu banaaya. usake saath jao. - mis daarsee, pembarle kee mistar daarsee kee betee aur ledee ainee, alag-alag tareeke se auchity ke saath prakat nahin ho sakatee theen. — main un sabhee cheejon ke prati atyadhik chaukas hoon. aapako jon ko yuva ke saath bhejana hoga. mahilaon, shreematee kolins. mujhe khushee hai ki yah ullekh karane ke lie mere saath hua, kyonki yah vaastav mein aapake lie unhen akele jaane ke lie apamaanajanak hoga. "

"mere chaacha ko hamaare lie ek naukar bhejana hai."

"oh! -tumhaare chaacha! -vah ek aadamee-naukar rakhata hai, vah karata hai? - mujhe bahut khushee hai ki aapake paas koee hai jo un cheejon ke baare mein sochata hai. aap kahaan ghode badalenge? - oh! bromalee, bilkul. - agar aap jaanate hain bel par mera naam, aap mein bhaag liya jaega.

ledee kaithareen ke paas unakee yaatra ka sammaan karane ke lie kaee any prashn the, aur jaisa ki unhonne khud un sabhee ka javaab nahin diya, dhyaan dena aavashyak tha, jise elijaabeth unake lie bhaagyashaalee maanatee thee; ya, man mein itanee vyastata ke saath, vah bhool gaee ki vah kahaan thee. pratibimb ko ekaant ghanton ke lie aarakshit kiya jaana chaahie; jab bhee vah akelee hotee, to use sabase badee raahat ke roop mein raasta detee; aur ek din bhee ekaant tahalane ke bina nahin gaya, jisamen vah apriy yaadon ke sabhee aanand le sakata hai.

mistar daarsee ka patr, vah jald hee dil se jaanane ke lie ek uchit tareeke se tha. usane har vaaky ka adhyayan kiya: aur usake lekhak ke prati usakee bhaavanaen kaee baar vyaapak roop se bhinn theen. jab usane apane pate kee shailee ko yaad kiya, to vah abhee bhee aakrosh se bharee thee; lekin jab usane socha ki usane kitanee anyaayapoorn tareeke se usakee ninda kee aur usakee paravarish kee, to usaka gussa apane hee khilaaph ho gaya; 


shanivaar kee subah elijaabeth aur mi. kolins doosaron ke saamane aane se kuchh minat pahale naashte ke lie mile; aur unhonne bhaag dene vaalee naagarikata ka bhugataan karane ka avasar liya jise unhonne anivaary roop se aavashyak maana.

"main nahin jaanatee, mis elijaabeth," unhonne kaha, "kya shreematee kolins ne abhee tak hamaare paas aane mein aapakee daya kee bhaavana vyakt kee hai, lekin mujhe poora yakeen hai ki aap isake lie dhanyavaad praapt kie bina ghar nahin chhodenge. aapakee kampanee ko bahut mahasoos kiya gaya hai, main aapako vishvaas dilaata hoon. ham jaanate hain ki hamaare vinamr nivaas mein kisee ko lubhaane ke lie kitana kam hai. hamaare saade tareeke se, hamaare chhote kamare, aur kuchh domestiks, aur chhote se ham duniya ko dekhate hain, aadi. hansphord ko apane jaisee ek yuva mahila ke lie behad sust banaana chaahie; lekin mujhe ummeed hai ki aap ham par vishvaas karenge ki ham krpaalu ke lie aabhaaree hain, aur yah ki hamane apanee shakti mein har kaam kiya hai taaki aap apane samay ko apriy roop se vyateet kar saken. "isase mujhe yah sunane mein sabase badee khushee milatee hai ki aapane apana samay nahin beeta hai. hamane nishchit roop se apana sarvashreshth pradarshan kiya hai; aur sabase saubhaagy se yah hamaaree shakti mein hai ki ham aapako bahut shreshth samaaj se parichit karaen, aur rojings ke saath hamaare sambandh se, baar-baar. vinamr ghareloo drshy ko alag karane ke maadhyam se, mujhe lagata hai ki ham khud ko chaapaloosee kar sakate hain ki aapakee hansphord yaatra pooree tarah se apamaanajanak nahin ho sakatee hai. ledee kaithareen ke parivaar ke sambandh mein hamaaree sthiti vaastav mein asaadhaaran laabh aur aasheervaad kee tarah hai jo kuchh ghamand kar sakate hain. ek phuting ham hain. aap dekhate hain ki ham lagaataar vahaan kaise lage rahate hain. sach mein mujhe yah sveekaar karana chaahie ki is vinamr paraajay ke sabhee nukasaanon ke saath, mujhe yah nahin sochana chaahie ki isamen koee bhee vyakti daya ka paatr hai, jabaki ve hamaare hissedaar hain. rojings mein antarangata. "

usakee bhaavanaon kee oonchaee ke lie shabd aparyaapt the; aur vah kamare ke baare mein chalane ke lie baadhy tha, jabaki elijaabeth ne kuchh hee vaakyon mein naagarikata aur sachchaee ko ekajut karane kee koshish kee.

"aap, vaastav mein, mere priy chachere bhaee, hartaphordashaayar mein hamaare lie ek bahut hee anukool riport le sakate hain. main khud ko kam se kam chaapaloosee karata hoon ki aap aisa karane mein saksham honge. shreematee kaithareen ke lie ledee kaithareen ke mahaan dhyaan aapako ek dainik gavaah hai. ; aur pooree tarah se mujhe bharosa hai ki aisa nahin lagata hai ki aapake dost ne ek durbhaagyapoorn chitran kiya hai - lekin is bindu par yah chup rahana hoga. keval mujhe aapako vishvaas dilaata hoon, meree priy mis elijaabeth, ki main apane dil se sabase sauhaardapoorn roop se kaamana kar sakata hoon. aap shaadee mein samaanata rakhate hain. mere pyaare chaarlot aur mere paas ek dimaag aur sochane ka ek tareeka hai. hamaare beech charitr aur vichaaron mein sabase ullekhaneey samaanata har cheej mein hai. ham ek doosare ke lie dijain kie gae lagate hain. "

elijaabeth surakshit roop se kah sakatee hai ki yah ek badee khushee thee jahaan maamala tha, aur samaan eemaanadaaree ke saath jod sakata hai ki vah drdhata se vishvaas karatee thee aur apane ghareloo aaraam mein aanandit thee. haalaanki, jis mahila se ve chhidakate the, usake pravesh se baadhit hone ke lie use khed nahin tha. gareeb chaarlot! —is tarah ke samaaj mein use chhodane ke lie udaasee thee! —lekin usane ise apanee aankhon ke saath chuna tha; aur haalaanki jaahir hai ki usake aagantukon ko jaane ke lie pachhataava tha, vah karuna ke lie poochhane ke lie nahin lagata tha. usake ghar aur usake ghar kee rakhavaalee, usakee pallee aur usake murge, aur unakee sabhee aashrit chintaen, abhee tak apana aakarshan nahin kho chukee theen.

chez kee lambaee par, chaddee par chadha hua tha, paarsal bheetar rakha gaya tha, aur ise taiyaar hone ke lie uchchaaran kiya gaya tha. doston ke beech ek snehee vibhaajan ke baad, elijaabeth mistar kolins dvaara gaadee mein bhaag liya gaya tha, aur jaise hee ve bageeche mein chale gae, vah use apane sabhee parivaar ke lie apane sarvashreshth sammaan ke saath kameeshan kar raha tha, dayaaluta ke lie apana dhanyavaad nahin bhool gaya tha. sardiyon mein longaboran par, aur shree aur shreematee gaardinar ke lie unakee prashansa, haalaanki agyaat. phir usane use maariya ko saump diya, aur daravaaja band hone ke bindu par tha, jab usane achaanak unhen yaad dilaaya, kuchh adachan ke saath, ki ve gulaabon kee mahilaon ke lie koee sandesh chhodane ke lie bhool gae the.

"lekin," unhonne kaha, "aap nishchit roop se apane vinamr sammaan kee ichchha rakhate hain, jab tak aap yahaan rahe hain tab unakee daya ke lie aapaka aabhaaree dhanyavaad."

elijaabeth ne koee aapatti nahin kee; - tab daravaaje ko band karane kee anumati dee gaee, aur gaadee ko baahar nikaal diya gaya.

"aha!" maariya roya, kuchh minaton ke maun ke baad, "aisa lagata hai lekin ek ya do din jab se ham pahalee baar aae hain! aur phir bhee kitanee cheejen huee hain!"

"ek mahaan kaee vaastav mein," ek aah ke saath usake saathee ne kaha.

unakee yaatra bahut adhik baatacheet, ya kisee alaarm ke bina kee gaee thee; aur hansaphord chhodane ke chaar ghante ke bheetar, ve mistar gaardinar ke ghar pahunche.




maee mein yah doosara saptaah tha, jisamen teen yuva mahilaon ne gresacharch-street se, hartaphordashaayar ke shahar ke lie ek saath set kiya; aur, jab ve niyat saraay ke paas pahunche, jahaan mistar benet kee gaadee unase milane aaee thee, to unhonne jaldee se maana, kochamain kee samay kee paabandee mein, kittee aur lidiya donon daining-room kee seedhiyon se baahar dekh rahe the. ye do ladakiyaan ek ghante se oopar kee jagah par theen, khushee se ek vipareet chakkee mein jaane, gaard par praharee ko dekhane, aur ek sallad aur kakadee ke kapade pahane hue theen.

apanee bahanon ka svaagat karane ke baad, unhonne vijayee roop se is tarah ke thande maans ke saath ek tebal set pradarshit kiya, jaisa ki ek saadhaaran lordar aamataur par pratipaadit karata hai, "yah achchha nahin hai? kya yah ek aashcharyajanak aashchary nahin hai?"

aur jab usakee bahanon ne use badasoorat ke roop mein durvyavahaar kiya, to usane ekadam sahee kaha, "oh! lekin dukaan mein do ya teen bahut badasoorat the, aur jab mainne ise nae sire se trim karane ke lie kuchh pritiyar rang ka saatan khareeda hai, to mujhe lagata hai ki bahut sahan karane yogy hoga. isake alaava, yah jyaada sanket nahin dega ki is garmee mein kaun kya pahanata hai, - jab se meriyan ne chhod diya hai, aur ve ek pakhavaade mein ja rahe hain. "

jen aur elijaabeth ne ek-doosare ko dekha, aur vetar se kaha gaya ki use rahane kee jaroorat nahin hai. lida ne hansate hue kaha,

"ai, yah tumhaaree aupachaarikata aur vivek kee tarah hai. tumane socha tha ki vetar ko nahin sunana chaahie, jaise ki vah paravaah karata hai! main kahata hoon ki vah aksar badatar baaten sunata hai jitana main kahane ja raha hoon. lekin vah ek badasoorat saathee hai! main hoon khushee hai ki vah chala gaya. mainne apane jeevan mein itanee lambee thodee kabhee nahin dekhee. khair, lekin ab meree khabar ke lie: yah vikram ke baare mein hai? vetar ke lie bhee achchha hai, hai na? vikram kee mairee king se shaadee karane ka koee khatara nahin hai. tumhaare lie! vah livarapool mein apane chaacha ke paas gaya, rahane ke lie gaya. vikam surakshit hai. elijaabeth yah sochakar hairaan ho gaee ki, haalaanki abhivyakti kee aisee sahooliyat mein asamarth, bhaavukata kee lakeer usake apane stan ke alaava kuchh aur thee jo pahale se hee kathor aur kattar udaar thee!

"mujhe khushee hai ki mainne apana bonat khareed liya, agar yah keval ek aur baindaboks hone ke maze ke lie hai! theek hai, ab hamen kaaphee sahaj aur snoog hone den, aur ghar par sabhee tarah se hansee-mazaak karen. aur sabase pahale, hamen sunane den. aap sabhee ke saath kya hua hai, jab se aap chale gae hain. kya aapane kisee bhee sukhad purush ko dekha hai? kya aapake paas koee chhedakhaanee hai? main bahut ummeed mein tha ki aapake vaapas aane se pahale aapamen se ek ko pati mil jaega. jen kaaphee puraana hoga. jald hee, main ghoshana karata hoon. vah lagabhag teen aur bees hai! bhagavaan, mujhe sharm kaisee hai ki mujhe teen aur bees se shaadee nahin karanee chaahie! meree chaachee philips chaahatee hain ki aapako pati mile, aap soch bhee nahin sakate. vah kahate hain ki lijee behatar thee. shree kolins ko liya hai, lekin mujhe nahin lagata ki isamen koee maza aaya hoga. bhagavaan! main aap mein se kisee se pahale shaadee karana pasand karoon aur phir main aapako sabhee gendon ke baare mein bataoonga. mujhe priy hai! karnal phorstar ke doosare din maza ka itana achchha tukada tha. kittee aur mujhe din bitaane the, aur shreematee phorstar ne thoda dain karane ka vaada kiya tha shaam ko see; (alavida, shreematee phorstar aur mere aise dost hain!) aur isalie usane do heringatan ko aane ke lie kaha, lekin hairiyat beemaar tha, aur isalie pen ko khud hee aane ke lie majaboor hona pada; aur phir, aapako kya lagata hai ki hamane kya kiya? hamane chaimbaralen taiyaar kiya   elijaabeth jen ko jo hua tha usase parichit hone ke lie adheerata ab door nahin ho sakatee; aur lambaee mein har us vishesh ko dabaane ke lie jisamen usakee bahan chintit thee, aur use aashcharyachakit karane ke lie taiyaar kar rahee thee, usane agalee subah shree daarsee aur khud ke beech ke drshy ke pramukh se sambandhit kiya.

"tum par dosh lagao! oh, nahin."

"lekin tum mujhe vikam kee itanee garmajoshee se baat karane ke lie doshee maanate ho."

usane tab patr kee baat kee, jab tak ki vah jorj vikam kee baat karate hue apanee sampoorn saamagree ko dohara deta hai. bechaare jen ke lie yah kya aaghaat tha! jo svechchha se is vishvaas ke bina duniya mein chale gae honge ki maanav jaati kee pooree daud mein itanee dushtata maujood thee, jaisa ki yahaan ek vyakti mein ekatr kiya gaya tha. na hee daarsee kee pratigya thee, haalaanki usakee bhaavanaon ke lie aabhaaree, is tarah kee khoj ke lie use saantvana dene mein saksham. adhikaansh eemaanadaaree se usane truti kee sambhaavana ko saabit karane ke lie shram kiya, aur doosare ko shaamil kie bina ek ko saaph karane kee talaash kee.

"oh! nahin, mera pachhataava aur karuna sab door ho gaee hai aap donon ko itana bhara hua dekhakar. mujhe pata hai ki aap use aisa paryaapt nyaay denge, ki main har pal aur adhik asambaddh aur udaaseen ho raha hoon. aapaka bhram mujhe bachaata hai, aur yadi tum us par adhik der tak vilaap karate raho, mera dil pankh kee tarah halka ho jaega. ”

vah sahaj roop se door ho gaee thee; lekin, unake drshtikon par rok, ek sharmindagee ke saath unakee taareeph praapt karana asambhav ho gaya. unakee pahalee upasthiti thee, ya ve jis chitr kee abhee-abhee pareeksha de rahe the, usakee samaanata any do ko aashvast karane ke lie aparyaapt thee ki unhonne ab apane guru ko nihaarane par, aashchary kee maalee, shree daarsee ko dekha. jab ve apanee bhateejee se baat kar rahe the, to ve thode se khade ho gae, jo hairaan aur ulajhan mein the, ghabaraakar himmat se apanee aankhon ko unake chehare par utha liya, aur na jaane kya javaab diya ki vah apane parivaar ke baad apanee naagarik poochhataachh mein vaapas laut aae. apane tareeke se parivartan par chakit kyonki ve pichhale bhaag the, har vaaky jo usane bola tha vah usakee sharmindagee ko badha raha tha; aur usake vahaan hone kee ayogyata ka har vichaar, usake dimaag mein aa raha hai, kuchh minat jisamen ve ek saath jaaree rahe, usake jeevan ke kuchh sabase asahaj the. aur na hee vah bahut adhik aaraam se lagata tha; jab vah bolata tha, to usake uchchaaran mein usakee saamaany saadagee nahin hotee thee; aur unhonne longabarn chhodane ke samay aur darbeeshaayar mein apane pravaas ke samay ke roop mein apanee poochhataachh ko doharaaya, aur isalie jaldabaajee mein ek tarah se, jaisa ki spasht roop se apane vichaaron kee vyaakulata se baat kee thee.

lambaee mein, har vichaar use viphal karane ke lie lag raha tha; aur, bina kuchh kahe kuchh pal khade rahane ke baad, usane achaanak khud ko yaad kiya, aur chhuttee le lee.

doosare log usake saath shaamil hue, aur apane phigar kee prashansa kee; lekin elijaabeth ne ek shabd nahin suna, aur pooree tarah se usakee bhaavanaon se prabhaavit hokar, maun mein unaka peechha kiya. vah sharm aur aakrosh se ub chukee thee. usaka vahaan aana sabase durbhaagyapoorn tha, jo duniya kee sabase ashubh baat thee! kitana ajeeb lag raha hoga use! kya ek ghrnit prakaash mein yah ek aadamee vyarth hadataal nahin kar sakata hai! aisa lagata hai jaise usane jaanaboojhakar khud ko phir se apane raaste mein phenk diya ho! oh! vah kyon aaee? ya, vah apeksha se ek din pahale hee kyon aaya tha? yadi ve jald hee keval das minat ke the, to unhen apane bhedabhaav kee pahunch se pare hona chaahie tha, kyonki yah spasht tha ki vah us kshan aa gaya tha, vah kshan apane ghode ya usakee gaadee se utara. baithak kee vyaapakata ko lekar vah baar-baar sharamaaya. aur usaka vyavahaar, itanee hadabadee mein badal gaya, isaka kya matalab ho sakata hai? yah bhee ki use usase baat karanee chaahie vah adbhut thee! -lekin aisee shishtata ke saath bolane ke lie, usake parivaar ke baad poochhataachh karane ke lie! apane jeevan mein kabhee bhee unhonne apane shishtaachaar ko itana kam pratishthit nahin dekha tha, kabhee bhee is apratyaashit mulaakaat par itanee vinamrata se baat nahin kee thee. rozing paark mein apane antim pate ke lie yah kya vipareet tha, jab usane apana patr apane haath mein rakha! vah nahin jaanatee thee ki use kya sochana hai aur na hee kaise isaka hisaab dena hai.

ve ab paanee ke kinaare ek khoobasoorat paidal maarg mein pravesh kar gae the, aur har kadam jameen ke ek nebalar girane, ya jangal kee ek maheen pahunch ko aage la raha tha, jahaan ve aa rahe the; lekin elijaabeth ke kisee bhee samajhadaar hone se pahale yah kuchh samay tha; aur, haalaanki usane apane chaacha aur chaachee kee baar-baar kee gaee apeel ka javaab diya, aur apanee aankhon ko aisee vastuon ke lie nirdeshit karane ke lie lag raha tha jaise unhonne bataaya, usane drshy ke kisee hisse ko alag nahin kiya. usake vichaar sabhee pembale haus ke us ek sthaan par tay kie gae the, jo bhee ho, jahaan shree daarsee tab the. use yah jaanane kee laalasa thee ki us pal usake dimaag mein kya chal raha tha; kis tareeke se usane usake baare mein socha, aur kya, har baat ke bachaav mein, vah abhee bhee use priy thee. shaayad vah sabhy tha, keval isalie ki usane khud ko sahaj mahasoos kiya; abhee tak unakee aavaaz mein aisa tha, jo sahaj nahin tha. chaahe use dard jyaada mahasoos hua ho ya use dekhane mein khushee ka anubhav ho, vah bata nahin sakatee thee, lekin usane use nishchit roop se nahin dekha tha.

haalaanki, usake man kee anupasthiti par usake saathiyon kee tippanee ne use naaraaj kar diya, aur use khud kee tarah dikhane kee aavashyakata mahasoos huee.

unhonne jangal mein pravesh kiya, aur thodee der ke lie nadee mein ediyoo kee bolee lagaee, kuchh oonche maidaanon par chadhe; phusaphusaate hue, un sthaanon par jahaan pedon ke khulane se bhatakane kee aankh kee shakti milatee thee, ghaatee ke kaee aakarshak drshy the, vipareet pahaadiyaan, jinamen se kaee jangal lambe samay tak phaile rahate the, aur kabhee-kabhee dhaara ka hissa hote the. mistar gaardinar ne poore paark ke chakkar lagaane kee ichchha vyakt kee, lekin aashanka hai ki yah sair se pare ho sakata hai. vijayee muskaan ke saath, unhen bataaya gaya, ki yah das meel ka chakkar tha. isane maamala sulajha diya; aur unhonne aadee sarkit ka peechha kiya; jo unhen phir se laaya gaya, kuchh samay baad, ek latakate jangal ke beech, paanee ke kinaare par, usake sabase chhote hisson mein. unhonne ise ek saadhaaran pul se paar kiya, drshy kee saamaany hava ke saath charitr mein; yah ek spot kam sajee thee, jisakee tulana mein ve abhee tak gae the; aur ghaatee, yahaan ek chakaachaundh mein anubandhit hai, keval kamare ko dhaara ke lie anumati dee gaee hai, aur isakee ooparee seema ke beech ek sankeern paidal raasta hai, jo isakee seema hai. elijaabeth apanee vainding ka pata lagaane ke lie taras gaee; lekin jab ve pul ko paar kar chuke the, aur ghar se apanee dooree tay kar rahe the, shreematee gaardinar, jo ek mahaan vokar nahin theen, koee aage nahin ja sakeen, aur unhonne socha ki jald se jald gaadee vaapas laut jae.

elijaabeth ne ise nipataaya tha ki mistar daarsee apanee bahan ko usase milane ke lie laegee, usee din pembale ke pahunchane ke baad; aur phalasvaroop us subah kee saraay ke darshan se baahar na hone ka sankalp liya gaya. lekin usaka nishkarsh galat tha; laimbatan mein apane svayan ke aagaman ke baad bahut subah, ye aagantuk aae. ve apane kuchh nae doston ke saath us jagah ke baare mein chal rahe the, aur ek hee parivaar ke saath bhojan karane ke lie khud ko saraay mein lauta rahe the, jab ek gaadee kee aavaaz ne unhen ek khidakee tak kheench liya, aur unhonne ek sajjan aur mahila ko dekha ek kyootikal mein, sadak par gaadee chalaana. elijaabeth ne jhootha pahachaan liya, yah anumaan lagaaya ki isaka kya matalab hai, aur usane apane sambandhon ko aashchary kee koee chhotee digree pradaan nahin kee, unhen us sammaan ke saath parichit karaaya jo usane ummeed kee thee. usake chaacha aur chaachee sabhee vismit the; aur apane tareeke kee sharmindagee, jaisa ki usane baat kee thee, khud paristhiti mein shaamil ho gaee, aur poorvavartee paristhitiyon kee kaee paristhitiyon ne vyavasaay par ek naya vichaar khola. kuchh bhee pahale kabhee bhee isaka sujhaav nahin diya gaya tha, lekin ab unhen laga ki unakee bhateejee ke lie ek pakshapaat kee tulana mein is tarah ke ek chauthaee se is tarah ke dhyaan ke lie lekhaankan ka koee any tareeka nahin tha. jab ye nav-janm dhaaranaen unake sir mein guzar rahee theen, tab elijaabeth kee bhaavanaon kee gadabadee har pal badhatee ja rahee thee. vah apane svayan ke asveekaran par kaaphee chakit thee; lekin bechainee ke any kaaranon ke beech, usane darate hue kaha ki bhaee ke paksh mein usake paksh mein bahut kuchh kahana chaahie tha; aur khush karane ke lie aamataur par adhik utsuk hone ke kaaran, use svaabhaavik roop se sandeh tha ki manabhaavan kee har shakti use viphal kar degee.

vah khidakee se peechhe hat gaee, jise dekhakar dar gaya; aur jab vah oopar chalee gaee aur kamare se neeche chalee gaee, to khud ko rachane ka prayaas karate hue, usane apane chaacha aur chaachee mein aashcharyachakit karane vaale poochhataachh ke aise roop dekhe, jisase har baat bigad gaee.

mis daarsee aur usaka bhaee dikhaee die, aur yah durjey parichay hua. vismay ke saath, elijaabeth ne dekha, ki usaka naya parichit kam se kam utana hee sharminda tha jitana ki vah svayan. choonki usake laimbatan mein hone ke baad, usane suna tha ki mis daarsee ko atyadhik garv tha; lekin kuchh hee minaton ke avalokan ne use aashvast kar diya, ki vah keval atyadhik sharmeelee thee. use ek monosilebal se pare ek shabd bhee praapt karana mushkil tha.

mis daarsee lamba tha, aur elijaabeth kee tulana mein bade paimaane par; aur, solah se thoda adhik hone ke baavajood, usakee aakrti ban gaee thee, aur usakee upasthiti stree aur sundar thee. vah apane bhaee kee tulana mein kam sundar thee, lekin usake chehare par bhaav aur achchha haasy tha, aur usake shishtaachaar pooree tarah se niraadhaar aur komal the. elijaabeth, jisane shree darasee ke roop mein teevr aur nirbaadh roop se ek paryavekshak ko khojane kee ummeed kee thee, samajhadaar aisee vibhinn bhaavanaon se bahut raahat milee thee.

ve lambe samay se saath nahin the, isase pahale ki daarsee ne use bataaya ki bingale bhee us par prateeksha karane ke lie aa raha tha; aur usake paas apanee santushti ko vyakt karane ke lie mushkil samay tha, aur aise aagantuk ke lie taiyaar hone ke lie, jab bingale ka tvarit kadam seedhiyon par suna gaya tha, aur ek pal mein vah kamare mein pravesh kar gaya. usake khilaaph elijaabeth ka saara gussa bahut pahale khatm ho chuka tha; lekin, kya vah ab bhee kisee ko mahasoos kar rahee thee, yah shaayad hee kabhee usake dvaara vyakt kie gae aprabhaavit sauhaard ke khilaaph apanee jameen par khada ho sakata hai. usane apane parivaar ke baad, haalaanki saamaany tareeke se, ek dostaana tareeke se poochhataachh kee, aur usee achchhe-sahajata ke saath dekha aur bola jo usane kabhee kiya tha.

mistar aur misez gaardinar ko vah apane aap se kam dilachasp vyakti lagata tha. ve lambe samay se use dekhana chaahate the. unake saamane pooree paartee ne, vaastav mein, ek jeevant dhyaan aakarshit kiya. shree daarsee aur unakee bhateejee ke baare mein jo sandeh utpann hue the, unhonne pratyek ke prati apanee nishtha ka nireekshan kiya, yadyapi pahara, poochhataachh; aur ve jald hee un jaanchon se pooree tarah se aashvast ho gae ki unamen se kam se kam ek ko pata tha ki ise kya pyaar karana hai. mahila kee sanvedanaon mein se ve kuchh sandeh mein rahe; lekin yah ki sajjan prashansa ke saath bah rahe the, kaaphee spasht tha.

elijaabeth, usake paksh mein, bahut kuchh karana tha. vah apane pratyek aagantuk kee bhaavanaon ka pata lagaana chaahatee thee, vah use apanee rachana karana chaahatee thee, aur khud ko sabhee ke lie sahamat karana chaahatee thee; aur baad kee vastu mein, jahaan use asaphal hone ka sabase adhik dar tha, vah saphalata ke lie sabase adhik sunishchit thee, jinake lie usane khushee dene ka prayaas kiya tha, usake paksh mein poorvagrah the. bingale taiyaar tha, jorjiyaee utsuk tha, aur daarsee ne prasann hone ke lie nirdhaarit kiya.

bingale ko dekhane mein, usake vichaar svaabhaavik roop se usakee bahan ke lie ud gae; aur oh! kitanee der tak vah yah jaanana chaahatee thee ki kya usake kisee bhee tareeke ko nirdeshit kiya gaya tha. kabhee-kabhee vah kalpana kar sakatee thee, ki vah poorv ke avasaron kee tulana mein kam baat karatee hai, aur ek ya do baar khud ko is dhaarana se prasann kiya ki jaisa ki vah use dekhatee hai, vah ek samaanata ka pata lagaane kee koshish kar rahee thee. lekin, haalaanki yah kaalpanik ho sakata hai, use mis daarsee ke saath apane vyavahaar ke roop mein dhokha nahin diya ja sakata tha, jise jen ke pratidvandvee ke roop mein sthaapit kiya gaya tha. vishesh roop se baat karane vaale donon taraph koee nazar nahin aaya. unake beech aisa kuchh nahin hua 

elijaabeth ke roop mein ab yah maana jaata hai ki mis bingale kee usake prati aruchi eershya mein utpann huee thee, vah yah mahasoos karane mein madad nahin kar sakee ki pembale mein usakee upasthiti kitanee apriy hai, vah usake lie zarooree hai, aur yah jaanane ke lie utsuk thee ki us mahila ke paksh mein kitanee shishtata thee, parichit ab naveeneekrt ho.

ghar pahunchane par, unhen hol ke maadhyam se sailoon mein le jaaya gaya, jisaka uttaree pahaloo garmiyon ke lie ramaneey tha. jameen par khulane vaalee isakee khidakiyaan, ghar ke peechhe kee oonchee lakadee kee pahaadiyon aur sabase khoobasoorat ok aur spenish chaasanee ke sabase taaza drshy ko sveekaar karatee hain, jo madhyavartee lon mein bikhare hue the.

is kamare mein unhen mis daarsee milee, jo shreematee harst aur mis bingale ke saath vahaan baithee theen aur vah mahila jinake saath vah landan mein rahatee theen. jorjiyaee ka unaka svaagat bahut hee sabhy tha; lekin un sabhee sharmindagee ke saath bhaag liya, jo haalaanki sharm se aage badhana aur galat karane ke dar se, aasaanee se un logon ko de denge jo khud ko heen mahasoos karate the, usake garv aur aarakshit hone ka vishvaas. shreematee gaardinar aur unakee bhateejee ne, haalaanki, usaka nyaay kiya aur use dang kar diya.

shreematee harst aur mis bingale dvaara, unhen keval ek kartasee dvaara dekha gaya tha; aur unake baithane par ek thaharaav, ajeeb jaisa ki hamesha rukana chaahie, kuchh kshanon ke lie saphal hua. ise sabase pahale shreematee enesalee ne toda tha, jo ek jentil, sahamat-dikhane vaalee mahila thee, jisake kisee tarah ke pravachan ko pesh karane ke prayaas ne use doosaron kee tulana mein adhik achchhee tarah se sahee saabit kar diya; aur usake aur shreematee gaardinar ke beech, elijaabeth kee kabhee-kabhaar madad ke saath, baatacheet jaaree thee. mis daarsee ne dekha ki vah saahas ke lie kaamana karatee hai taaki usamen shaamil ho sake; aur kabhee-kabhee ek chhote se vaaky ka upakram kiya, jab isake sunaee dene ka kam se kam khatara tha.

elijaabeth ne jald hee dekha ki vah mis bingale dvaara khud ko kareeb se dekha gaya tha, aur vah apane dhyaan ko bulae bina, vishesh roop se mis daarsee ko ek shabd bhee nahin bol sakatee thee. is avalokan ne use baad mein baat karane kee koshish karane se nahin roka hoga, kya ve asuvidhaajanak dooree par nahin baithe the; lekin use itana kahane kee aavashyakata hone ka dar nahin tha. usake apane vichaar use rojagaar de rahe the. vah har pal ummeed karatee thee ki kuchh sajjan kamare mein pravesh karenge. vah kaamana karatee hai, use dar hai ki ghar ka svaamee unake beech ho sakata hai; aur chaahe vah sabase jyaada chaahe ya use dar lage, vah shaayad hee yah nirdhaarit kar sake. ek ghante ke is tareeke se baithane ke baad, mis bingale kee aavaaj sune bina, elijaabeth ko apane parivaar ke svaasthy ke baad usakee thandee jaanch se praapt kar liya gaya. usane samaan udaaseenata aur sankshiptata ke saath uttar diya, aur doosare ne kaha ki nahin.

agala badalaav jo unakee yaatra ka kharch tha, vah thanda maans, kek, aur mausam mein sabhee behatareen phalon ke saath naukaron ke pravesh dvaara nirmit kiya gaya tha; lekin misej ensle se mis daarsee ko die gae ek mahatvapoorn roop aur muskaan ke baad yah tab tak nahin hua, jab tak ki use apane pad kee yaad nahin dilaee gaee. ab pooree paartee ke lie rojagaar tha; haalaanki ve sabhee baat nahin kar sakate the, ve sab kha sakate the; aur angoor, amrt aur aadoo ke sundar piraamidon ne jald hee unhen gol-gol kar diya.

is prakaar lage rahane ke dauraan, elijaabeth ko yah nirnay lene ka ek uchit avasar mila ki kya vah kamare mein pravesh karane par jo bhaavanaon se grast thee, usase shree daarsee kee upasthiti kee sabase adhik aashanka ya kaamana thee; aur phir, haalaanki, lekin ek pal pahale vah apanee ichchhaon ko maanana ​​chaahatee thee, vah aphasos karane lagee ki vah aaya tha.

shree gaardinar ke saath vah kuchh samay rahe the, jo ghar se do ya teen any sajjanon ke saath nadee se jude hue the, aur unhen keval yah seekhane par chhod diya tha ki parivaar kee mahilaon ne us subah jorjiyaee yaatra ka iraada kiya tha. elijaabeth ke buddhimaanee se pooree tarah se aasaan aur nirbaadh roop se hal kie jaane kee tulana mein vah jald hee dikhaee nahin diya, - ek sankalp ko aur adhik aavashyak banaaya jaana chaahie, lekin shaayad adhik aasaanee se nahin rakha gaya, kyonki usane dekha ki pooree paartee ka sandeh unake khilaaph jaagrt tha, aur yah ki ek aankh buree tarah se thee jo kamare mein aane par usaka vyavahaar nahin dekhatee thee. kisee bhee ganana mein chaukas jigyaasa nahin thee, jo mis bingale ke roop mein drdhata se chihnit thee, muskuraahat ke baavajood jab bhee vah apanee vastuon mein se ek se baat karatee thee, to usake chehare ko dekhatee thee; eershya ke lie abhee tak use hataash nahin kiya tha, aur shree daarsee ke lie usakee chaukasee koee matalab nahin tha. mis daarsee, apane bhaee ke pravesh par, khud ko baat karane ke lie aur adhik utsaahit karatee thee; aur elijaabeth ne dekha ki vah apanee bahan aur khud se parichit hone ke lie utsuk thee, aur jitana sambhav ho utana sambhav tha, har taraph baatacheet ka prayaas. mis bingale ne yah sab dekha; aur, krodh kee bhaavana mein, kahane ka pahala avasar liya, vyangy ke saath,

"praarthana karo, mis elija, nahin hain — merinatan se hatae gae-meel ka milishiya; ve aapake parivaar ke lie ek badee kshati honee chaahie."

daarsee kee upasthiti mein usane vikkam ke naam ka ullekh nahin kiya; lekin elijaabeth turant samajh gaee ki vah apane vichaaron mein sabase oopar hai; aur usake saath jude vibhinn smaranon ne use ek pal ka kasht diya;


elijaabeth jen se ek patr nahin milane par niraash ho gaee thee, laimbatan mein unake pahale aagaman par; aur is niraasha ko us samay kee pratyek subah ko naveeneekrt kiya gaya tha jo ab vahaan kharch kee gaee thee; lekin teesare par, usaka doharaav khatm ho gaya tha, aur usakee bahan ne ek hee baar mein do patron kee praapti ko sahee thaharaaya tha, jinamen se ek par yah chihnit kiya gaya tha ki yah kaheen aur mis kiya gaya tha. elijaabeth is par aashcharyachakit nahin thee, kyonki jen ne disha ko ullekhaneey roop se beemaar likha tha.

patr aate hee ve chalane kee taiyaaree kar chuke the; aur usake chaacha aur chaachee, use chupachaap aanand lene ke lie chhodakar, khud se door ho gae. sabase pahale ek mis ko upasthit hona chaahie; yah paanch din pahale likha gaya tha. shuruaat mein unake sabhee chhote dalon aur vyastataon ka lekha-jokha tha, jaise ki desh mein aisee khabaren theen; lekin baad ke aadhe hisse ko, jo ek din baad dinaankit kiya gaya tha, aur spasht aandolan mein likha gaya tha, ne adhik mahatvapoorn khuphiya jaanakaaree dee. yah is prabhaav ke lie tha:

    "sabase priy lijee ke oopar likhane ke baad se, kuchh sabase apratyaashit aur gambheer prakrti ka hua hai; lekin main aapako bhayabheet karane se darata hoon - aashvast rahen ki ham sab achchhee tarah se hain. mujhe jo kahana hai vah gareeb lidiya se sambandhit hai. ek eksapres aaya tha. pichhalee raat baarah, jaise hee ham sabhee karnal phorstar se bistar par chale gae the, hamen yah bataane ke lie ki vah apane ek adhikaaree ke saath skotalaind ke lie ravaana hua tha, sach ka saamana karane ke lie! , yah pooree tarah se apratyaashit nahin lagata hai. main bahut, bahut maaphee chaahata hoon. isalie donon taraph se ek maich kee nakal kar raha hoon! lekin main sabase achchhee ummeed karane ke lie taiyaar hoon, aur yah ki usaka charitr galat samajha gaya hai. vichaaraheen aur andhaadhundh main aasaanee se us par vishvaas kar sakata hoon. , lekin yah kadam (aur hamen is par aanandit hone den) dil mein kuchh bhee bura nahin hai. usakee pasand kam se kam hai, kyonki vah jaanata hai ki mere pita use kuchh bhee nahin de sakate. hamaaree gareeb maan dukhee hai. mere pita ise behatar tareeke se nibhaate hain. aabhaaree hoon main, ki hamane unhen kabhee bhee yah bataane nahin diya ki unake khilaaph kya kaha gaya hai, hamen kshama karana chaahie et it khud. ve shanivaar kee raat baarah ke baare mein the, jaisa ki anumaan hai, lekin kal subah aath baje tak yaad nahin kiya gaya tha. eksapres ko seedhe ravaana kar diya gaya. mere pyaare lijee, ve ham se das meel kee dooree se gujare honge. karnal phostar hamen yahaan jald hee unase apeksha karane ka kaaran deta hai. lida ne apanee patnee ko unake iraade kee jaanakaaree dete hue kuchh lainen chhod deen. mujhe nishkarsh nikaalana chaahie, kyonki main apanee gareeb maan se lambee nahin ho sakatee. mujhe dar hai ki aap ise nahin bana paenge, lekin mujhe shaayad hee pata ho ki mainne kya likha hai. "

khud ko vichaar ke lie samay kee anumati ke bina, aur shaayad hee kabhee yah jaanakar ki vah kya mahasoos karatee hai, elijaabeth ne is patr ko khatm karane par, turant doosare ko jabt kar liya, aur ise behad adheerata ke saath khola, nimnaanusaar padhen: yah pahale ke nishkarsh kee tulana mein ek din baad likha gaya tha. .
