"mis benet, aapake lon ke ek taraph ek bahut kam jangal ka ek sundar prakaar lag raha tha. mujhe isamen ek mod lene mein khushee honee chaahie, agar aap mujhe apanee kampanee ke saath rahane ka paksh lenge."

"jao, mere pyaare," usakee maan ne roya, "aur usane alag-alag raaston ke baare mein apanee maan ko bataaya. mujhe lagata hai ki vah hermitej se prasann hogee."

elijaabeth ne aagya ka paalan kiya aur apane chhatr ke lie apane hee kamare mein bhaag kar seedhiyon se neeche apane nek mehamaan ke saath upasthit huee. jaise hee ve hol se guzare, ledee kaithareen ne daining-paarlar aur draing-room mein daravaaje khol die, aur unaka uchchaaran karate hue, ek chhote se sarvekshan ke baad, achchhe dikhane vaale kamare hone ke lie, ve chal pade.

usakee gaadee daravaaje par rahee aur elijaabeth ne dekha ki usakee prateeksha karane vaalee mahila usamen thee. ve bajaree kee sair ke saath maun mein aage badhe, jisake kaaran kopase ka saamana karana pada; elijaabeth ek mahila ke saath baatacheet ke lie koee prayaas nahin karane ke lie drdh thee, jo ab aamataur par dheeth aur asahamat se adhik thee.

"main use bhateeje kee tarah kabhee kaise soch sakata tha?" usane kaha, jaisa ki usane usake chehare mein dekha.

jaise hee ve kops mein daakhil hue, ledee kaithareen nimnalikhit tareeke se shuroo hueen: -

"aap bina kisee nukasaan ke ho sakate hain, mis benet, meree yaatra ke kaaran ko samajhane ke lie. aapaka apana dil, aapaka apana vivek, aapako bataana chaahie ki main kyon aata hoon."

elijaabeth aprabhaavit aashchary ke saath dekha.

"vaastav mein, aap galat hain, maidam. main aapako yahaan dekhane ke sammaan ke lie bilkul bhee saksham nahin hoon."

"mis benet," ne apanee laadalee ko javaab diya, ek gusse bhare lahaje mein, "aapako pata hona chaahie, ki main ke saath trast nahin kiya ja raha hoon. lekin phir bhee aap ka chayan karane ke lie jiddee ho, to aap mujhe aisa nahin paenge. mera charitr kabhee nahin raha apanee eemaanadaaree aur spashtata ke lie manaaya jaata hai, aur is tarah ke ek pal ke kaaran mein, main nishchit roop se isase door nahin jaoonga. sabase khataranaak prakrti kee ek riport, do din pahale mere paas pahunchee. mujhe bataaya gaya, ki aapakee bahan hee nahin thee. sabase adhik laabhaanvit hone kee baat hai, lekin yah ki aap, mis elijaabeth benet, sabhee sambhaavana mein, mere bhateeje ke lie jald hee ekajut ho jaegee, 


aatmaon ka sampark, jise is asaadhaaran yaatra ne elijaabeth mein phenk diya, ko aasaanee se door nahin kiya ja saka; aur na hee vah kaee ghanton ke lie, ise lagaataar kam se kam sochana seekh sakata hai. ledee kaithareen ko yah dikhaee diya, vaastav mein rozee daarsee ke saath usakee kathit sagaee ko todane ke ekamaatr uddeshy ke lie, rozings se is yaatra kee pareshaanee lee thee. yah sunishchit karane ke lie ek tarkasangat yojana thee! lekin unakee sagaee kee riport kya ho sakatee hai, elijaabeth kalpana karane ke lie ek nukasaan mein thee; jab tak vah yaad karatee hai ki usaka bingale ka antarang mitr, aur jen kee bahan hone ke naate, vah paryaapt tha, ek samay mein jab ek shaadee kee ummeed, vichaar kee aapoorti karane ke lie har shareer ko doosare ke lie utsuk bana deta tha. vah khud ko yah mahasoos karane ke lie nahin bhool gaee thee ki usakee bahan kee shaadee ko unhen aur adhik saath laana hoga. aur lukaas mein usake padosee loj mein rahate hain, isalie, (kolins ke saath unake sanchaar ke maadhyam se, jo riport usane nishkarsh nikaala hai vah mahila kaithareen tak pahunchee thee) keval usee nishchit aur tatkaal ke roop mein neeche set kee gaee thee, jise vah sambhav ke roop mein aage dekh rahee thee, kuchh mein bhavishy kaal.

haalaanki, mahila kaithareen ke bhaavon ko sanshodhit karane mein, vah is vyavadhaan mein usake bane rahane ke sambhaavit parinaam ke roop mein kuchh asahajata mahasoos karane mein madad nahin kar sakee. apanee shaadee ko rokane ke lie apane sankalp ke baare mein usane jo kaha tha, usase elijaabeth ko yah laga ki use apane bhateeje ke lie ek aavedan karana chaahie; aur vah apane saath ek sambandh se judee buraiyon ka samaan pratinidhitv kaise le sakata hai, usane uchchaaran nahin kiya. vah apanee chaachee ke prati apane sneh, ya unake nirnay par nirbharata ka sahee ansh nahin jaanatee thee, lekin yah maan lena svaabhaavik tha ki vah jitana kar sakatee thee, usase kaheen adhik usakee laadalee sochatee thee; aur yah nishchit tha, ki ek ke saath ek vivaah ke dukhon kee ganana karane mein, jisake taatkaalik sambandh usake khud ke lie bahut hee asamaan the, usakee chaachee use sabase kamajor paksh par sambodhit karegee. garima kee apanee dhaaranaon ke saath, vah shaayad yah mahasoos karenge ki elijaabeth ko jo tark kamajor aur haasyaaspad dikhaee die, unamen bahut achchhee samajh aur thos tark shaamil the.

yadi vah pahale se dagamaga raha tha, to use kya karana chaahie, jo aksar sambhaavana prateet hotee thee, ek sambandh ke paas salaah aur antahkriya har sandeh ko sulajha sakatee hai, aur use ek hee baar mein khush hone ke lie nirdhaarit karatee hai, jaisa ki garima nishkalank use bana sakatee hai. . us sthiti mein vah aur nahin lautega. ledee kaithareen use shahar ke raaste mein dekh sakatee hai; aur needaralaind ke lie phir se aane ke bingale ke lie usakee sagaee ko raasta dena chaahie.

"agar, isalie, apana vaada nahin nibhaane ka bahaana, kuchh dinon ke bheetar apane dost ke paas aana chaahie," usane kaha, "mujhe pata hoga ki ise kaise samajhana hai. main tab har ummeed, usake kabje kee har ichchha ko chhod doongee. agar vah keval mujhe pachhataava karane se santusht ho jaata hai, jab usane mere sneh aur haath ko praapt kiya ho sakata hai, main jald hee use usase pachhataava nahin karana chaahata. "

baakee parivaar ka aashchary, yah sunane par ki unaka aagantuk kaun tha, bahut mahaan tha; lekin unhonne ise usee tarah ke daman ke saath santusht kiya, jisane shreematee benet kee jigyaasa ko shaant kiya tha; aur elijaabeth ko is vishay par bahut adhik bhaag lene se bakhsha gaya.

agalee subah, jab vah seedhiyon se neeche ja rahee thee, to usakee mulaakaat usake pita se huee, jo usake haath mein ek patr lekar laibreree se baahar aaya tha.

"lijee," usane kaha, "main tumhaaree talaash karane ja raha tha, mere kamare mein aao."

usane usaka peechha kiya; aur yah jaanane ke lie usakee jigyaasa ki use use kya bataana tha, vah usake dvaara pakade gae patr ke saath kisee na kisee tarah se jude rahane ke dabaav se badh gaya tha. isane achaanak use maara ki yah mahila kaithareen se ho sakata hai; aur vah sabhee parinaamee vyaakhyaon ko khaarij kar detee hai.

vah apane pita ke saath aag vaalee jagah par gaee, aur ve donon baith gae. usane phir kaha,

"mujhe aaj subah ek patr mila hai jisane mujhe bahut aashcharyachakit kiya hai. jaisa ki yah mukhy roop se apane aap ko chintit karata hai, aapako isakee saamagree ko jaanana chaahie. mujhe pahale nahin pata tha, ki meree do betiyaan hain jo vivaah ke kagaar par hain. mujhe aapako badhaee dena chaahie, par. ek bahut hee mahatvapoorn vijay. "

rang ab elijaabeth ke gaal mein chala gaya, jo chaachee ke bajaay bhateeje se ek patr hone ke taatkaalik vishvaas mein tha; aur vah anirdhaarit tha ki kya sabase adhik prasann hona chaahie ki usane khud ko bilkul samajhaaya, ya isase naaraaj tha ki usake patr ko khud ko sambodhit nahin kiya gaya tha; jab usake pita ne jaaree rakha,

"aap sachet dikhate hain. yuva mahilaon mein is tarah ke maamalon mein bahut paith hai; lekin mujhe lagata hai ki main aapake shishtata ka naam jaanane ke lie aapakee shithilata ko bhee taal sakata hoon. yah patr shree kolins ka hai."

"mistar kolins se? aur usaka kya kahana hai?"

"nishchit roop se kuchh bahut jyaada. vah meree sabase badee betee ke nikat aane vaale badhaee ke saath shuroo hota hai, jisamen se aisa lagata hai ki use kuchh achchhe-achchhe logon dvaara bataaya gaya hai, luseez gosiping. main aapakee adheerata ke saath khel nahin karoonga. , us bindu par vah jo kahata hai, use padhakar. jo apane aap se sambandhit hai, vah is prakaar hai. "is prakaar aapako shreematee kolins kee eemaanadaaree se badhaee aur khud ko is sukhad ghatana kee badhaee dene ke baad, ab mujhe sabaj mein ek chhota sanket jodana hai.


apane mitr kee or se is tarah ka koee bhee patr praapt karane ke bajaay, jaisa ki elijaabeth aadhe ko mistar bingale se ummeed thee, vah ledee kaitharin kee yaatra ke baad kaee dinon se pahale daarsee ko longaboran ke saath laane mein saksham tha. sajjan jaldee aa gae; aur, isase pahale ki shreematee benet ke paas unakee chaachee ko dekhane ka samay tha, jisamen se unakee betee kshanik ghabaraahat mein baithee thee, bingale, jo jen ke saath akele rahana chaahata tha, ne apane sabhee ghoomane ka prastaav rakha. is par sahamati banee. shreematee benet ko chalane kee aadat nahin thee, mairee kabhee bhee khaalee samay nahin de sakatee theen, lekin shesh paanch ek saath set ho gaeen. haalaanki, bingale aur jen ne jald hee doosaron ko unase aage nikalane kee anumati de dee. ve pichhad gae, jabaki elijaabeth, kittee aur daarsee, ek doosare ka manoranjan karane vaale the. ya to bahut kam kaha gaya tha; kitee ko usase baat karane mein bahut dar lagata tha; elijaabeth chupake se ek hataash sankalp taiyaar kar rahee thee; aur shaayad vah bhee yahee kar raha hoga.

ve lukaas kee or chal pade, kyonki kitee maariya ko bulaana chaahata tha; aur jab elijaabeth ne ise saamaany chinta ka vishay nahin banaaya, to jab kittee ne unhen chhod diya, to vah akele hee unake saath chalee gaeen. ab usake sankalp ko kriyaanvit karane ka kshan tha, aur, jabaki usakee himmat adhik thee, usane turant kaha,

"mistar daarsee, main ek bahut hee svaarthee praanee hoon; aur, apanee bhaavanaon ko raahat dene ke lie, mujhe paravaah hai ki main aapake ghaav ko bharane mein kitana saksham ho sakata hoon. main ab aapakee gareeb bahan ke lie aapakee dayaaluta ke lie dhanyavaad dene mein aapakee madad nahin kar sakata. . jab se mainne ise jaana hai, mujhe sabase jyaada chinta is baat ko maanane kee huee hai ki main ise kitana aabhaaree mahasoos karata hoon. kya yah mere parivaar ke baakee logon ko pata tha, mujhe keval apana aabhaar vyakt karane ke lie nahin hona chaahie. "

"mujhe khed hai, atyadhik khed hai," daarsee ne aashchary aur bhaavana ke lahaje mein kaha, "aapako kabhee bhee is baat kee jaanakaaree dee gaee hai ki galatee se prakaash mein aane se aapako kya bechainee huee hogee. mujhe nahin lagata tha ki shreematee gaardinar aisa tha. thoda bharosa kiya jae. "

"aapako meree chaachee ko dosh nahin dena chaahie. lida kee vichaaraheenata ne mujhe sabase pahale dhokha diya ki aap is maamale mein the, aur nishchit roop se, main tab tak aaraam nahin kar sakata tha jab tak main vishesh ko nahin jaanata. mujhe baar-baar dhanyavaad den. mere sabhee parivaar, us udaar karuna ke lie, jisane aapako itanee pareshaanee uthaane ke lie prerit kiya, aur unakee khoj ke lie, itanee saaree hatyaen sahan keen. "

"yadi aap mujhe dhanyavaad denge," unhonne javaab diya, "ise apane lie akele rahane den. aapako khushee dene kee ichchha, any preranaon mein bal jod sakatee hai, jisane mujhe aage badhaaya, main inakaar karane ka prayaas nahin karoonga. mujhe kuchh bhee nahin dena. jitana main unaka sammaan karata hoon, mujhe vishvaas hai, mainne keval tumhaare baare mein socha. "

elijaabeth ek shabd kahane ke lie bahut sharminda thee. ek chhote se viraam ke baad, usake saathee ne kaha, "aap mere saath trishool lene ke lie bahut udaar hain. yadi aapakee bhaavanaen abhee bhee hain ki ve pichhale aprail mein the, to mujhe ek hee baar mein bataen. mere pyaar aur ichchhaen aparivartit hain, lekin aapase ek shabd bhee maun rahega. mujhe is vishay par hamesha ke lie. "

elijaabeth apanee sthiti kee saamaany ajeebata aur chinta se adhik mahasoos kar rahee thee, ab khud ko bolane ke lie majaboor kiya; aur turant, haalaanki bahut dhaaraapravaah nahin, use yah samajhane ke lie diya, ki usakee bhaavanaon mein bahut badalaav aaya hai, kyonki jis avadhi ke lie usane use sveekaar kiya, use aabhaar aur khushee ke saath praapt karane ke lie, usake vartamaan aashvaasan. is uttar ne jo khushee paida kee, vah aisee thee jaise usane pahale kabhee mahasoos nahin kee thee; aur unhonne is avasar par khud ko samajhadaaree ke saath aur pyaar se hinsak roop se vyakt kiya. agar elijaabeth usakee aankh ka saamana karane mein saksham thee, to usane dekha hoga ki usake chehare par prasannata, prasannata kee abhivyakti kitanee achchhee thee; lekin, yadyapi vah nahin dekh sakatee thee, vah sun sakatee thee, aur usane use apanee bhaavanaon ke baare mein bataaya, jo usake lie kya mahatv tha, yah saabit karane mein, har pal apane sneh ko aur adhik moolyavaan bana diya.

bina kisee disha mein jaane, ve chal pade. bahut socha jaana tha; aur mahasoos kiya, aur kaha, kisee bhee any vastuon par dhyaan dene ke lie. usane jald hee yah jaan liya ki ve apanee chaachee ke prayaason ke lie unakee vartamaan achchhee samajh ke lie rnee hain, jinhonne landan se lautane ke dauraan unhen phon kiya tha, aur vahaan longabarn kee yaatra, isaka makasad aur elijaabeth ke saath unakee baatacheet ka vishay tha; baad kee har abhivyakti par sashakt roop se nivaas karana, jo ki usakee laadalee kee aashanka mein, ajeebogareeb dhang se usakee shishtata aur aashvaasan ko darshaata hai, is tarah ke sambandh mein use apane bhateeje se us vaade ko praapt karane ke lie apane prayaason mein madad karanee chaahie, jise usane dene se inakaar kar diya tha. lekin, usakee lay ke lie anajaane mein, isaka prabhaav bilkul vipareet tha.

"isane mujhe ummeed karana sikhaaya," unhonne kaha, "jaisa ki mainne pahale kabhee khud ko ummeed karane kee anumati dee thee. mujhe pata tha ki aapaka svabhaav kaaphee had tak nishchit hai, ki, aap bilkul mere khilaaph phaisala kar chuke the, aap ise sveekaar kar lenge." ledee kaithareen ko, khulakar aur khulakar. "

elijaabeth rangeen aur hansate hue usane javaab diya, "haan, aap mujhe is baat par vishvaas karane ke lie meree spashtata ke baare mein paryaapt jaanate hain ki aapake chehare par itanee ghinaunee harakat karane ke baad, mujhe aapake sabhee sambandhon ka durupayog karane mein koee sandeh nahin hai."
mere priy lijee, aap kahaan tak ja sakate hain? "ek prashn tha jo elijaabeth ne jen se praapt kiya tha jaise hee usane kamare mein pravesh kiya, aur any sabhee se jab ve tebal par baith gae. use keval uttar mein kahana tha. ve tab tak bhatakate rahe, jab tak vah apane gyaan se pare nahin rahee. vah bolee jaane vaalee ke roop mein rangee huee thee, lekin na to vah, aur na hee koee aur cheej, sachchaee ka sandeh jagaatee thee.

shaam chupachaap gujar gaee, kisee bhee cheej ko asaadhaaran roop se chinhit kiya. sveekaar kie gae premiyon ne baat kee aur hanse, anajaan log chup the. daarsee ek svabhaav nahin tha jisamen khushee mirth mein bahatee thee; aur elijaabeth, uttejit aur bhramit, balki jaanatee thee ki vah khush thee, aisa khud ko mahasoos hua; tatkaal sharmindagee ke alaava, usake saamane any buraiyaan theen. usane anumaan lagaaya ki jab usakee sthiti gyaat ho jaegee to parivaar mein kya mahasoos hoga; vah jaanatee thee ki koee bhee use pasand nahin karata lekin jen; aur yahaan tak ​​ki yah bhee dar tha ki doosaron ke saath yah ek naapasand tha jo usake bhaagy aur parinaam ko door nahin kar sakata hai.

raat mein usane apana dil jen ke lie khol diya. haalaanki sandeh mis benet kee saamaany aadaton se bahut door tha, vah yahaan bilkul avishvasaneey tha.

"aap majaak kar rahe hain, lijee. yah nahin ho sakata hai! - shree daarsee ke lie jimmedaar! nahin, nahin, aap mujhe dhokha nahin denge. mujhe pata hai ki yah asambhav hai."

"yah vaastav mein ek manahoos shuruaat hai! meree ekamaatr nirbharata aap par thee; aur mujhe yakeen hai ki koee aur mujh par vishvaas nahin karega, agar aap nahin karate hain. phir bhee, vaastav mein, main bayaana mein hoon. main sach ke alaava kuchh nahin bolata. vah abhee bhee mujhase pyaar karata hai. , aur ham lage hue hain. ”

jen ne usakee taraph shak se dekha. "oh, lijee! yah nahin ho sakata. mujhe pata hai ki aap use kitana naapasand karate hain."

"aap is maamale ke baare mein kuchh bhee nahin jaanate hain. yah sab bhool jaana hai. shaayad main usase hamesha itana pyaar nahin karata tha jitana ab karata hoon. lekin aise maamalon mein, ek achchhee yaad akaaran hotee hai. yah aakhiree baar hai jab main kabhee bhee karoonga. ise khud yaad rakho. ”

mis benet abhee bhee sabhee aashcharyachakit dikh rahee theen. elijaabeth phir se, aur adhik gambheerata se use isakee sachchaee ka aashvaasan diya.

"achchha svarg! kya yah vaastav mein aisa ho sakata hai! phir bhee ab mujhe aap par vishvaas karana chaahie," jen ne roya. "mere pyaare, priy lijee, main aapako badhaee doonga - lekin kya aap nishchit hain? prashn ko kshama karen - kya aap kaaphee nishchit hain ki aap usake saath khush rah sakate hain?"

"isamen koee sandeh nahin ho sakata hai. yah hamaare beech pahale se hee tay hai, ki ham duniya ke sabase khush jode hain. lekin kya aap khush hain, jen? kya aapako aisa bhaee rakhana pasand hai?"

"bahut, bahut. kuchh bhee nahin hai ya to bingale ya khud ko aur adhik khushee de sakata hai. lekin hamane ise maana, hamane ise asambhav ke roop mein baat kee. aur kya aap vaastav mein use kaaphee pasand karate hain? oh, lijee! pyaar ke bina shaadee ke bajaay kisee bhee cheej ko karen! kya aap nishchit hain ki aapako lagata hai ki aapako kya karana chaahie? "

"oh, haan! aap keval sochenge ki mujhe jitana karana chaahie, usase adhik mujhe lagata hai, jab main aapako bataata hoon."

"tum kya matalab hai?"

"kyon, mujhe kabool karana chaahie, ki main use bingale se behatar pyaar karata hoon. mujhe dar hai ki aap naaraaj honge."

"meree sabase pyaaree bahan, ab gambheer ho jao. main bahut gambheerata se baat karana chaahata hoon. bina kisee deree ke mujhe har vo baat bataen jo mujhe pata hai. kya aap mujhe bataenge ki aap usase kitane samay se pyaar karate hain?"

"yah itanee dheere-dheere aa raha hai, ki mujhe shaayad hee pata ho ki yah kab shuroo hua. lekin mera maanana ​​hai ki mujhe pembarlee mein apane khoobasoorat maidaanon ko dekhakar pahalee baar se hee ise det karana hoga."

ek aur dhamakee ki vah gambheer hoga, haalaanki, vaanchhit prabhaav paida kiya; aur usane jald hee jen ko apane lagaav ke aashvaasan se santusht kar diya. jab us lekh par yakeen kiya gaya, to mis benet ke paas ichchha karane ke lie kuchh bhee nahin tha.

"ab main kaaphee khush hoon," usane kaha, "aap ke lie khud ke roop mein khush honge. mere lie hamesha usake lie ek mooly tha. kuchh bhee nahin hai lekin aap ke pyaar ke lie, mujhe hamesha use sammaan dena chaahie tha; lekin ab, jaisa ki bingale ke dost aur aapake pati, mere lie keval bingale aur khud ko adhik priy ho sakate hain. lekin lizee, aap bahut dhoort hain, mere saath bahut hee aarakshit hain. aapane mujhe pembale aur laimbatan mein kya paarit kiya, yah mujhe kam hee pata tha! mujhe isaka pata hai, doosare ko, tumhen nahin. ”

elijaabeth ne use apanee gopaneeyata ke makasad batae. vah bingale ka ullekh karane ke lie taiyaar nahin tha; aur usakee khud kee bhaavanaon kee anasulajhee sthiti ne use apane dost ke naam se bachane ke lie samaan bana diya tha. lekin ab vah usase nahin chhipega, lida kee shaadee mein usaka hissa. sabhee ko sveekaar kiya gaya, aur aadhee raat baatacheet mein bitaee.

elijaabeth kee aatma jald hee phir se chanchalata kee or badh rahee thee, vah chaahatee thee ki mistar daarsee ko usake pyaar mein padane ka hisaab diya jae. "aap kaise shuroo kar sakate hain?" usane kaha. "jab aap ek baar shuruaat kar chuke the, to aap aakarshak roop se aage badh sakate hain; lekin pahalee baar mein aap kya kar sakate hain?"

"main ghante, ya spot, ya luk, ya shabdon ko theek nahin kar sakata, jisane neenv rakhee thee. yah bahut pahale se hai. mujhe pata tha ki main shuroo kar chuka tha."

"meree sundarata aap jaldee khatm ho gaee thee, aur mere shishtaachaar ke roop mein - mere lie aapaka vyavahaar kam se kam hamesha asabhy par seemaabaddh tha, aur mainne aapako bina dard ke dene kee ichchha ke bina aapase kabhee baat nahin kee. ab eemaanadaaree se kaam karen; aapakee prashansa kee. mujhe apanee apoornata ke lie? "

"apane man kee aajeevika ke lie, mainne kiya."

"aap ek hee baar mein ise apoornata kah sakate hain. yah bahut kam tha. tathy yah hai ki, aap naagarikata se, apamaan ke, aapattijanak dhyaan ke the. aap un mahilaon se ghrna karate the jo hamesha bolatee theen aur dekh rahee theen, aur soch rahee theen. keval aapake anumodan ke lie. mainne aap par krodh kiya, aur aapakee ruchi kee, kyonki main unake vipareet tha. yadi aap vaastav mein uttaradaayee nahin hote, to aap isake lie mujhase ghrna karate; lekin dard ke baavajood aapane apane aap ko chhipaane ke lie liya, aapakee bhaavanaen hamesha mahaan theen. aur bas, aur aapake dil mein, aapane un logon ko achchhee tarah se tiraskrt kiya, jinhonne aapako itanee vinamrata se chhod diya tha. vahaan-mainne aapako isake lie lekhaankan kee pareshaanee se bachaaya hai; aur vaastav mein, sabhee cheejon par vichaar kiya gaya hai, main ise pooree tarah se uchit samajhane ke lie sunishchit karane ke lie. , tum mere baare mein koee vaastavik achchha nahin jaanate the - lekin jab ve pyaar mein padate hain to koee bhee isake baare mein nahin sochata.

"kya vah aapake snehapoorn vyavahaar mein jen se achchhee nahin thee, jabaki vah nedarapheeld mein beemaar thee?"

"sabase priy jen! jo usake lie kam kar sakata tha; lekin har tarah se isaka ek gun bana sakata hai. mere achchhe gun aapake sanrakshan mein hain, aur aap unhen jitana sambhav ho utana atiranjit kar sakate hain; aur badale mein, yah mera hai. aap ke saath jitanee baar ho sake utanee baar jhagadane aur jhagadane ke avasar dhoondhana, aur main aapase seedhe poochhakar shuroo karoonga ki aakhirakaar aapako is mudde par aane ke lie kitana anichchhuk banaaya gaya hai. jab aapane pahalee baar phon kiya tha, tab aap mujhase bahut sharminda the. baad mein yahaan bhojan kiya? kyon, vishesh roop se, jab aapane phon kiya, to kya aapane aisa dekha jaise aapane meree paravaah nahin kee? "

"kyonki aap gambheer aur chup the, aur mujhe koee protsaahan nahin diya."

"lekin main sharminda tha."

"aur isalie main tha."

"jab aap raat ke khaane mein aae to aapane mujhase adhik baat kee hogee."

"ek aadamee jisane kam mahasoos kiya tha, ho sakata hai."

"kitana ashubh hai ki aapake paas dene ke lie ek uchit uttar hona chaahie, aur yah ki mujhe ise sveekaar karane ke lie itana uchit hona chaahie! lekin mujhe aashchary hai ki aap kitane samay tak chale honge, agar aap khud par chhod die gae the. mujhe aashchary hai ki aapake paas kab hoga. bola, agar mainne aapase nahin poochha hota! lida ke prati aapakee dayaaluta ke lie aapako dhanyavaad dene ka mera sankalp nishchit roop se bahut prabhaav daalata tha. bahut jyaada, main darata hoon, naitikata ka kya ho jaata hai, agar hamaare aaraam ka vaada karane se bach jaata hai, to main is vishay ka ullekh nahin karana chaahie? yah kabhee nahin hoga. "

"aapako apane aap ko pareshaan karane kee aavashyakata nahin hai. naitik roop se pooree tarah se uchit hoga. hamen alag karane ke lie ledee kaithareen ke anyaayapoorn prayaas, mere sabhee sandehon ko door karane ke saadhan the. main aapakee krtagyata vyakt karane kee aapakee utsuk ichchha ke lie meree vartamaan khushee ke lie rnee nahin hoon. main tha. aapake kisee bhee udghaatan ke lie intajaar karane ke lie haasy mein nahin. meree chaachee kee buddhi ne mujhe aasha dee thee, aur mujhe har baat jaanane ke lie ek baar mein nirdhaarit kiya gaya tha. "

"ledee kaithareen anant upayog kee hai, jo use khush karane ke lie chaahie, kyonki vah upayog karane ke lie pyaar karatee hai. lekin mujhe batao, kya aap needaralaind ke lie neeche aae? kya yah keval longabarn kee savaaree karana aur sharminda hona tha ya? aapane kisee aur gambheer parinaam ka iraada kiya hai? "

"mera asalee uddeshy aapako dekhane ke lie tha, aur agar main kar sakata tha, to main aapako pyaar karane ke lie aasha kar sakata hoon ya nahin. yah jaanane ke lie ki mera bahan ne kya haasil kiya, yah dekhane ke lie ki kya aapakee bahan abhee bhee bingale mein aanshik thee. , aur agar vah thee, to use sveekaar karane ke lie jo mainne banaaya hai. "

"kya aapane kabhee ledee kaithareen kee ghoshana karane ka saahas kiya hai, use kya karana hai?"

"main saahas se adhik samay chaahata hoon, elijaabeth. lekin yah kiya jaana chaahie, aur yadi aap mujhe ek pepar denge, to yah seedhe kiya jaega."

"aur agar mere paas khud ko likhane ke lie koee patr nahin tha, to main aapake paas baith sakata hoon, aur aapake lekhan kee saamarthy kee prashansa kar sakata hoon, jaisa ki ek baar ek any yuva mahila ne kiya tha. lekin meree ek chaachee bhee hai, jise ab upekshit nahin hona chaahie."

anichchha se yah sveekaar karane ke lie ki mistar daarsee ke saath usakee aatmeeyata kitanee adhik ho chukee hai, elijaabeth ne abhee tak shreematee gaardinar ke lambe patr ka javaab nahin diya tha, lekin ab, yah sampreshan karane ke lie ki use pata tha ki usaka sabase adhik svaagat hoga, vah lagabhag sharminda thee. paate hain, ki usake chaacha aur chaachee pahale hee teen din kee khushee kho chuke the, aur turant is prakaar likha tha:

    "main aapako pahale dhanyavaad deta tha, meree pyaaree chaachee, jaisa ki mainne aapake lambe, dayaalu, santoshajanak, vivaranon ke vivaran ke lie kiya hai; lekin sach kahoon, to main likhane ke lie bahut paar tha. aap vaastav mein maujood the. , lekin ab jitana aap chusate hain maan leejie, apane phains ko ek dheelaapan den, apanee kalpana ka aanand len
apanee sabhee maatr bhaavanaon ke lie khush vah din tha jis din shreematee benet ne apanee do sabase yogy betiyon se chhutakaara paaya. shreematee bingale ke jaane ke baad vah kis garv se prasann hueen aur shreematee daarsee kee baat ka anumaan lagaaya ja sakata hai. kaash, main usake parivaar kee khaatir kah sakata, ki usake kaee bachchon kee sthaapana mein usakee sabase badee ichchha kee siddhi, itana khushahaal prabhaav paida kiya ki vah use ek samajhadaar, milanasaar, achchhee tarah se parichit mahila bana sake. usake jeevan ke baakee; haalaanki shaayad yah usake pati ke lie bhaagyashaalee tha, jisane ghareloo phelisitee ko itane asaamaany roop mein yaad nahin kiya hoga, ki vah abhee bhee kabhee-kabhee ghabara jaatee thee aur hamesha moorkhataapoorn.

shree benet ne apanee doosaree betee ko bahut yaad kiya; unake prati unake sneh ne unhen ghar se door karane vaale kee tulana mein kisee bhee any cheej ke lie aakarshit kiya. vah pembale jaane mein prasann tha, khaasakar jab use kam se kam ummeed thee.

mistar bingale aur jen needaralaind mein keval ek baarahamaasee bane rahe. to usakee maan aur merietan sambandhon ke aasapaas ke kshetr mein apane aasaan svabhaav, ya usake snehee dil ke lie bhee vaanchhaneey nahin tha. apanee bahanon kee kaamana ko tab krtaarth kiya gaya tha; unhonne ek padosee kauntee mein darbeeshaayar, aur jen aur elijaabeth ko khushee ke har doosare srot ke alaava, ek doosare ke tees meel ke daayare mein ek sampatti khareedee thee.

kittee, use bahut bhautik laabh ke lie, apane do badee bahanon ke saath apana samay bitaaya. samaaj mein vah jo aam taur par jaana jaata tha, usase behatar, usaka sudhaar bahut achchha tha. vah lida ke roop mein itanee asahaneey nahin thee, aur, lida ke udaaharan ke prabhaav se hata diya gaya, vah uchit dhyaan aur prabandhan, kam chidachida, kam agyaanee aur kam dheeth thee. lida ke samaaj ke door ke nukasaan se vah nishchit roop se dhyaan se rakha gaya tha, aur haalaanki shreematee vikam aksar use gendon aur yuva purushon ke vaade ke saath aane aur rahane ke lie aamantrit karatee thee, usake pita kabhee bhee usake saath jaane ke lie sahamat nahin honge.

mairee ikalautee betee thee jo ghar par hee rahatee thee; aur vah jarooree shreematee benet dvaara upalabdhiyon kee khoj se nikaala gaya tha, akele baithane mein kaaphee asamarth tha. mairee duniya ke saath aur adhik ghulane-milane ke lie baadhy thee, lekin vah har subah kee yaatra par usaka manobal badha sakatee thee; aur jaisa ki vah ab apanee bahanon kee sundarata aur khud ke beech tulana karake nahin maratee thee, yah usake pita ko sandeh tha ki usane bahut anichchha ke bina parivartan ke lie prastut kiya.

vikam aur lida ke lie, unake paatron ko unakee bahanon kee shaadee se koee kraanti nahin huee. unhonne darshanashaastr ke saath vishvaas kiya ki elijaabeth ko ab apane agyaatavaas aur asaty ke baare mein jo kuchh bhee pata tha usase parichit hona chaahie; aur har baat ke baavajood, is ummeed ke bina pooree tarah se nahin tha ki daarsee abhee tak apana bhaagy banaane ke lie prabal ho sakata hai. elijaabeth ko shaadee ke baad elijaabeth ko jo badhaee patr mila, usane use samajhaaya ki usakee patnee kam se kam, agar khud se nahin, to aisee ummeed poshit thee. is aashay ka patr tha:

    "mere pyaare lijee,

    "main aapako khushee kee shubhakaamana deta hoon. yadi aap mistar daarsee se pyaar karate hain aur saath hee saath main apana priy vikram bhee karata hoon, to aapako bahut khushee hogee. aapake paas itana samrddh hone ke lie bahut aaraam hai, aur jab aapake paas karane ke lie aur kuchh nahin hai, to mujhe ummeed hai aap hamaare baare mein sochenge. mujhe yakeen hai ki vikam adaalat mein ek jagah ko bahut pasand karenge, aur mujhe nahin lagata ki hamaare paas bina kisee madad ke rahane ke lie paryaapt paisa hoga. koee bhee jagah, lagabhag teen ya chaar sau saal ka hoga. , lekin, haalaanki, isake baare mein shree daarsee se baat na karen, agar aapake paas nahin tha.

    "tumhaara, aur see."

jaisa ki yah hua ki elijaabeth ke paas bahut adhik nahin tha, usane apane javaab mein prayaas kiya ki vah har tarah kee dhamakee aur ummeed ko khatm kar de. is tarah kee raahat, haalaanki, yah kharch karane kee usakee shakti mein thee, jo ki apane nijee vistaar mein arthavyavastha kaha ja sakata hai, ke abhyaas se, vah aksar unhen bhejatee thee. yah unake lie hamesha spasht raha hai ki unakee aay ke roop mein is tarah kee aay, do vyaktiyon kee disha mein unake chaahane vaalon ke atirikt, aur bhavishy kee paravaah kie bina, unake samarthan ke lie bahut aparyaapt honee chaahie; aur jab bhee unhonne apane kvaartar badale, jen ya khud ko unake bilon ke nirvahan kee disha mein kuchh kam sahaayata ke lie laagoo kiya jaana sunishchit tha. unake rahane ka tareeka, yahaan tak ​​ki jab shaanti kee bahaalee ne unhen ek ghar mein khaarij kar diya, to charam mein anishchitata thee. ve hamesha ek sastee sthiti kee talaash mein ek sthaan se doosare sthaan par ja rahe the, aur hamesha jitana ve chaahate the usase adhik kharch kar rahe the. usake prati usaka sneh jald hee udaaseenata mein doob gaya; vah thodee der tak chalee; aur usakee javaanee aur usake shishtaachaar ke baavajood, usane pratishtha ke sabhee daavon ko barakaraar rakha jo usakee shaadee ne use diya tha.

haalaanki daarsee unhen pembale mein kabhee bhee praapt nahin kar saka, phir bhee, elijaabeth ke lie, usane use apane peshe mein aage badhane mein sahaayata kee. lida kabhee-kabhaar vahaan aatee thee, jab usaka pati landan ya baath mein khud ka aanand lene gaya tha; aur bingaliyon ke saath ve donon aksar itane lambe samay tak ghooma karate the, ki bingale kee achchhee hansee bhee door ho gaee, aur vah itanee door aage badh gae ki unhen jaane ka sanket dene kee baat kee.

jaisa ki yah hua ki elijaabeth ke paas bahut adhik nahin tha, usane apane javaab mein prayaas kiya ki vah har tarah kee dhamakee aur ummeed ko khatm kar de. is tarah kee raahat, haalaanki, yah kharch karane kee usakee shakti mein thee, jo ki apane nijee vistaar mein arthavyavastha kaha ja sakata hai, ke abhyaas se, vah aksar unhen bhejatee thee. yah unake lie hamesha spasht raha hai ki unakee aay ke roop mein is tarah kee aay, do vyaktiyon kee disha mein unake chaahane vaalon ke atirikt, aur bhavishy kee paravaah kie bina, unake samarthan ke lie bahut aparyaapt honee chaahie; aur jab bhee unhonne apane kvaartar badale, jen ya khud ko unake bilon ke nirvahan kee disha mein kuchh kam sahaayata ke lie laagoo kiya jaana sunishchit tha. unake rahane ka tareeka, yahaan tak ​​ki jab shaanti kee bahaalee ne unhen ek ghar mein khaarij kar diya, to charam mein anishchitata thee. ve hamesha ek sastee sthiti kee talaash mein ek sthaan se doosare sthaan par ja rahe the, aur hamesha jitana ve chaahate the usase adhik kharch kar rahe the. usake prati usaka sneh jald hee udaaseenata mein doob gaya; vah thodee der tak chalee; aur usakee javaanee aur usake shishtaachaar ke baavajood, usane pratishtha ke sabhee daavon ko barakaraar rakha jo usakee shaadee ne use diya tha.

haalaanki daarsee unhen pembale mein kabhee bhee praapt nahin kar saka, phir bhee, elijaabeth ke lie, usane use apane peshe mein aage badhane mein sahaayata kee. lida kabhee-kabhaar vahaan aatee thee, jab usaka pati landan ya baath mein khud ka aanand lene gaya tha; aur bingaliyon ke saath ve donon aksar itane lambe samay tak ghooma karate the, ki bingale kee achchhee hansee bhee door ho gaee, aur vah itanee door aage badh gae ki unhen jaane ka sanket dene kee baat kee.

daarsee kee shaadee se mis bingale bahut gaharaee se mar chuka tha; lekin jaisa ki usane pembale mein jaane ke adhikaar ko banae rakhana uchit samajha, usane apanee saaree naaraajagee door kar dee; jorjiyaee ke pahale se kaheen jyaada chaara tha, lagabhag daarsee ke roop mein hetophor ke roop mein, aur elijaabeth ko naagarikata ke har bakaaya ka bhugataan kiya.

pembale ab jorjiyaee ka ghar tha; aur bahanon ka lagaav theek vaisa hee tha jaisa daarsee ko dekhane kee ummeed thee. ve ek-doosare se pyaar karane mein saksham the, yahaan tak ​​ki ve bhee iraada karate the. jorjiyaee kee elijaabeth kee duniya mein sabase jyaada raay thee; haalaanki pahale-pahal vah aksar apane bhaee se baat karane ke tareeke, usake jeevant, sportee, alaarm par chaunka dene vaalee aavaaj sunatee thee. vah, jisane hamesha apane aap ko ek sammaan ke lie prerit kiya tha, jisane usake sneh ko lagabhag khatm kar diya tha, usane ab khulee sukhadata kee vastu dekhee. usake man ko gyaan praapt hua jo usake raaste mein aane se pahale kabhee nahin hua tha. elijaabeth ke nirdeshon se vah yah samajhane lagee ki ek mahila apane pati ke saath svatantrata le sakatee hai, jise ek bhaee hamesha ek bahan ko apane se das saal se adhik chhotee umr mein nahin hone dega.

ledee kaithareen apane bhateeje kee shaadee par behad aakrosh mein thee; aur jaisa ki usane apane charitr kee sabhee vaastavik spashtata ke lie raasta diya tha, patr ke javaab mein jisane isakee vyavastha kee ghoshana kee, usane use vishesh roop se elijaabeth ke lie itanee apamaanajanak bhaasha bhejee, ki kuchh samay ke lie sabhee sambhog ek ant mein tha. lekin lambaee mein, elijaabeth ke anunay se, vah aparaadh ko najarandaaj karane ke lie prabal hua, aur sulah kee maang kee; aur, apanee chaachee kee or se thode door ke pratirodh ke baad, unakee naaraajagee ne raasta de diya, ya to unake prati sneh, ya unakee jigyaasa yah dekhane ke lie ki unakee patnee ne khud ko kaise sanchaalit kiya; aur vah pambarle mein un par prateeksha karane ke lie krpaalu ho gaya, us pradooshan ke baavajood jo usakee lakadiyaan praapt huee theen, na keval aisee maalakin kee upasthiti se, balki shahar se usake chaacha aur chaachee kee yaatraon se.

gaardinars ke saath, ve hamesha sabase antarang shabdon par the. daarsee, saath hee elijaabeth, vaastav mein unase pyaar karatee thee; aur ve donon kabhee un vyaktiyon ke prati sabase adhik aabhaar ke prati samajhadaar the, jo use darbeeshaayar mein laakar, unhen ekajut karane ka maadhyam bane the.
